**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-3.0-6.0-4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12826827`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute Duration of P(S)Cell L2-LO Local Burst by subtracting T4 timestamp and T1 timestamp received in [Before CB015504-A] LoData\_DlDataBurstInfoInd.DrbBurstInfo (5G\_L2\_IF\_4862\_replaced([10986386](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WOmHfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB015504-A] LoData\_DlDataBurstInfoInd:drbBurstInfo:drbBurstDetails ([12825308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_DLieuatOEfCyQasEtWkQ4A)) [End CB015504-A] / Xg-U DU DDDS ([10995372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2XLBQvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) from corresponding L2-LO.

For example as explained in [11234345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AxOg_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), Duration of burst for BW Counter is calculated as below :

1. Duration for Pcell Burst 1 is calculated as = T4 - T1

2. Duration for Scell Burst 2 is calculated as = T4 - T1

3. Duration for Pcell Burst 3 is calculated as = T4 - T1

PM Counters
Measurement: NR High RLC Report Cell

NetAct name: DL\_RLC\_PDU\_UE\_TPUT\_DENOM\_FR1

PI ID: M55349C00046

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

[Before CB010636-D-UPD001]

1. Last slot exclusion is not applied while calculating Duration BW.

[CB010636-D-UPD001]

1. Last slot exclusion applied for merged Burst (5G\_L2\_11998\_replaced([11234345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AxOg_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) will be applied for Duration BW computation as well (5G\_L2\_17601\_replaced([11234632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AzDw_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End CB010636-D-UPD001]

1. This counter is applicable for both FR1 SA and NSA DRBs
2. This counters is applicable for all FR1 SA CA types, both intra-gNB and inter-gNB.
3. 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall report this counter in MHz \* microseconds and BOAM/BSTAT will convert it to MHz \* milliseconds.

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-3.0-7.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11234732`)

PM Counters
Online modification of actPerCCDLUserThpt while actMacUserThpt is TRUE

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-3.0-7.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11234736`)

PM Counters
Since actMacUserThput is set to TRUE, 5G-L2-HI shall compute DL RLC PDU Throughput as explained in 5G\_L2\_XXx to report volume and time counters for the combined bursts based on feedback reports from all 5G-L2-LO instances.

But for computing DL Per CC UE Throughput counters (5G\_L2\_17748\_replaced([11234748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-HI shall consider these feedback reports from 5G-L2-LO instances only if actPerCCDLUserThpt is set to TRUE.

* If actPerCCDLUserThpt will change from TRUE to FALSE during the ongoing burst, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall ignore Burst reports received from L2-LO for DL Per CC UE Throughput counters (5G\_L2\_17748\_replaced([11234748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) computation.
* If actPerCCDLUserThpt will change from FALSE to TRUE, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute DL Per CC UE Throughput counters (5G\_L2\_17748\_replaced([11234748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for only those L2-LO Burst that are received after actPerCCDLUserThpt = TRUE at 5G-L2-HI (DU).
* If actPerCCDLUserThpt will change from TRUE to FALSE during the ongoing burst and then will change to TRUE, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall ignore Burst reports (if there was before burstStartInfo) received from L2-LO for DL Per CC UE Throughput  counters (5G\_L2\_17748\_replaced([11234748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) computation.

Note:

Different scenarios regarding online modification of actMacUserThput and actPerCCDLUserThpt and 5G-L2-HI (DU) behavior can be found under the following link: <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:f:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane>

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-3.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `11234742`)

PM Counters
DL Per CC Combination Throughput

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-3.0-7.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11234748`)

PM Counters
DL Per CC Combination Throughput Computation

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-3.0-7.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11234759`)

PM Counters
DL Per CC UE Throughput computation is illustrated with the help of below example for CA Case with 1 Primary Cell and 2 Secondary Cells (Scell 1 and SCell 2).

As explained in 5G\_L2\_11998\_replaced([11234345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AxOg_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall receive local burst report from each L2-LO Instance that contain start and end time of burst and volume of burst.

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute global merged Burst based on these L2-LO Burst reports.

In below example,

V1 = TotVol (total volume of all RLC PDUs(MAC SDUs) of Burst 1 reported from PCell L2-LO Instance)

T1 = timeLastTbTransmitted (Timestamp when last TB of Burst1 transmitted over air as reported by PCell L2-LO Instance in Burst1 report) –

timeFirstTbTransmitting (Timestamp when first TB of Burst1 transmitted over air as reported by PCell L2-LO Instance in Burst1 report)

Similarly V2,T2...V4,T4 are reported by corresponding L2-LO Instance in Burst Report.

When ever L2-LO burst starts or ends, the CC combination during that portion of Global Merged Burst gets changed.

1. Based on overlapping of L2-LO bursts, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute per CC time as below:

In below example, ta ... tg represent per CC time.

ta = T2s (Start of SCell1 Burst) - T1s (Start of Pcell Burst1)

tb = T3s (Start of SCell2 Burst) - T2s (Start of SCell1 Burst)

tc = T1e (End of Pcell Burst1) - T3s (Start of SCell2 Burst)

...

...

tg = T4e (End of Pcell Burst2) - T2e (End of SCell2 Burst)

1. For each per CC time (computed in above step 1), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute per CC volume as below:

per CC volume = per CC time \* (sum of average throughput of all L2-LO burst that are contributing to portion of global merged burst volume during this per CC time ta)

In below example, va ... vg represent per CC volume.

va = ta \* V1/T1

ta is overlapping completely with PCell Burst1 only so PCell Burst1 average throughput is considered.

Since here it is Pcell Burst1 only, ta and va get updated under 1CC counter.

ta and va get updated under 1CC counter since here only Pcell Burst1 are considered.

vb = tb \* ((V1/T1) + (V2/T2))

tb is overlapping completely with PCell Burst1 and SCell1 Burst and hence PCell Burst1 and SCell1 Burst average throughput are considered.

tb and vb get updated under 2CC counter since here only Pcell Burst1 and SCell Burst are considered.

vc = tc \* ((V1/T1) + (V2/T2) + (V3/T3))

tc is overlapping completely with PCell Burst1, SCell1 and SCell2 Bursts,hence PCell Burst1, SCell1 and SCell2 Burst average throughput are considered.

tc and vc get updated under 3CC counter since here Pcell Burst1, SCell1 and SCell2 Burst are considered.

...

...

vg = tg \* V4/T4

1. Last slot exclusion is applied on global merged burst but not applied for each CC burst.

In below example, vs and ts are excluded from global merged burst. Hence vs and ts excluded only for last per CC combination counter.

1. Finally at the end of global merged Burst, per CC throughput counters are updated as below for given example.

DL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC ≈ va + (vg-vs)

DL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_2CC ≈ vb + vd + vf

DL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_3CC ≈ vc + ve

DL\_RLC\_TIM\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC ≈ ta + (tg-ts)

DL\_RLC\_TIM\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_2CC ≈ tb + td + tf

DL\_RLC\_TIM\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_3CC ≈ tc + te

Note:

1. per CC time and volume counters are pegged only in PCell and applicable only for FR1 non-GBR DRBs.
2. FR1 non-GBR, non-CA burst volume and time is considered under 1CC counters.
3. per CC time and volume counters are applicable for both SA (5G\_L2\_17753\_replaced([11234782](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R2fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_17758\_replaced([11234808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R3vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  and NSA (5G\_L2\_17755\_replaced([11234793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R2_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_17760\_replaced([11234818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R4fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
4. per CC time and volume counters are applicable for all CA Types (intra-gNB and inter-gNB)

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-3.0-7.0-4.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11234786`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR High RLC Report Cell

NetAct name: DL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC ... DL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_6CC

PI ID: M55349C00026 ... M55349C00031

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time:

These 1CC ... 6CC counters are updated only when both HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actMacUserThpt and HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPerCCDLUserThhpt are TRUE and

for FR1 SA nonGBR DRBs only which are configured with secondary L2-LO Instance (either local or remote).

These counters provide portion (as computed in 5G\_L2\_17748\_replaced([11234748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of ThpVolDl (5G\_L2\_11937\_replaced([11234513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AycovvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is transmitted utilizing 1CC ... 6CC

Increment value:

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update the portion (as computed in 5G\_L2\_17748\_replaced([11234748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of ThpVolDl (5G\_L2\_11937\_replaced([11234513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AycovvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is transmitted utilizing 1CC ... 6CC.

Note:

1. 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall identify DRB as SA or NSA based on PmCountersInfo.typeOfBearer received in HiUserDu\_BearerSetupReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_4188\_replaced([10990186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WqD5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
2. For FR1 SA nonGBR DRBs that are not configured with secondary L2-LO Instance (either local or remote), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update Burst Volume ThpVolDl (5G\_L2\_11937\_replaced([11234513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AycovvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) under DL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC (M55349C00026)  counter.
3. These counters will be reported by 5G-L2-Hi (DU) in bits, and BOAM/BSTAT will convert them to kbits.

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

for FR1 NSA nonGBR DRBs only which are configured with secondary L2-LO Instance (either local or remote).

Increment value:

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update the portion (as computed in 5G\_L2\_17748\_replaced([11234748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of ThpVolDl (5G\_L2\_11937\_replaced([11234513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AycovvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is transmitted utilizing 1CC ... 2CC.

Note:

2. For FR1 NSA nonGBR DRBs that are not configured with secondary L2-LO Instance (either local or remote), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update Burst Volume ThpVolDl (5G\_L2\_11937\_replaced([11234513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AycovvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) under DL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_NSA\_1CC (M55349C00038) counter.
3. These counters will be reported by 5G-L2-Hi (DU) in bits, and BOAM/BSTAT will convert them to kbits

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11234851`)

PM Counters
Flow Control on LoData Interface

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11234857`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI shall increment

M55348C00001 (AVG\_NO\_AVAL\_SCELL\_PER\_BEARR) The average number of available secondary cells per bearer during a sample period

with the average number of available Secondary cells per bearer during a 100ms sample period.

The following counts are maintained internally:

1. the total number of Secondary cells that are marked as available across all bearers  (TOT\_NO\_OF\_SCELLS\_MARKED\_AVAIL).

2. the total number of bearers which are activated with a secondary cell(s)).  (TOT\_NO\_OF\_BEAR\_WITH\_ACTIV\_SCELL)

The average number of available secondary cells per bearer is updated as:

TOT\_NO\_OF\_SEC\_CELLS\_MARKED\_AVAIL / TOT\_NO\_OF\_BEAR\_WITH\_ACTIV\_SCELL

5G-L2-HI shall increment

M55348C00002 (AVG\_NO\_USD\_SCELL\_PER\_BEARR) The average number of used Secondary cells per bearer during a sample period

with the average number of used Secondary cells per bearer during a 100ms sample period.

The following counts are maintained internally:

1. The total number of Secondary cells that are marked as used for data sending across all bearers               (TOT\_NO\_OF\_SCELLS\_MARKED\_USED)

2. The total number of bearers which have activated secondary cell(s).  (TOT\_NO\_BEAR\_WITH\_ACTIV\_SCELL)

The average number of used secondary cells per bearer is updated as-

TOT\_NO\_OF\_SCELLS\_MARKED\_USED / TOT\_NO\_BEAR\_WITH\_ACTIV\_SCELL

Note:

For M55348C00001 (AVG\_NO\_AVAL\_SCELL\_PER\_BEARR) The average number of available secondary cells per bearer during a sample period timer which runs every 100ms calculates the value of available SCells and bearers with available SCells. The used SCell counter M55348C00002 (AVG\_NO\_USD\_SCELL\_PER\_BEARR) The average number of used Secondary cells per bearer during a sample period is incremented by the first PDU transmitted in the 100ms period for every bearer.

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11234923`)

PM Counters
Counters for DL F1-U Packet Loss Rate

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11234927`)

PM Counters
General information

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-7.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11234935`)

PM Counters
For DL F1-U Packet Loss Rate, L2Hi shall provide the following counters for NRPMQAP:

1. Number of DL PDCP PDUs that are lost over F1 (5G\_L2\_20759\_replaced([11234940](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A1f9fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on missed GTP-U SNs
2. Number of DL PDCP PDUs that are received at gNB-DU over F1 in order (5G\_L2\_20761\_replaced([11234950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A1f9_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on GTP-U SNs received in order
3. Number of DL PDCP PDUs that are received at gNB-DU over F1 out of order (5G\_L2\_20763\_replaced([11234962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A1f-_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on GTP-U SNs received out of order
4. These counters are provided based on GTP-U sequence numbers assigned to GTP-U packets. GTP-U SN field is optional in GTP-U header. L2Hi CU shall assign GTP-U SNs only if actGtpUpSeqNum=TRUE (HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq:pmCountersInfo, 5G\_L2\_IF\_5258\_replaced([10987189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This flag set to TRUE means that L2Hi CU shall assign GTP-U SNs (please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28659\_replaced([11225210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyLzqvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Data packets (GTP-U carrying PDCP SDU) shall always contain GTP-U SN once flag for this function is activated so that L2Hi DU could consider those packets in counters for DL F1-U Packet Loss Rate. Counters will be updated only if GTP-U SN will be present in GTP-U packets. L2Hi DU should not get duplicated GTP-U SN on any interface since there is no retx concept on GTP-U (If duplicated GTP-U SN will appear, L2Hi shall accept that packet, and repeated sequence number shall be counted as out of order). GTP-U SN should be assigned only for G-PDU packets with DUD extension header and PDCP Data PDUs (so with non-zero payload) as well as for PDCP control PDUs (ROHC feedback, PDCP status report). In case of pure polling (DUD without DL data packet) and GTP-U control PDUs (like SEHN, Error Indication, Tunnel Status, End Marker), GTP-U SN shall not be assigned. If packet will be a G-PDU packet and will have GTP-U SN assigned, L2Hi shall handle it and report it into counters.
5. Packet shall be counted as lost when there is a gap in the GTPU SN received in order. Such packet may be later received out of order or never received (really lost). Packet received out of order is also counted as lost. Receiving window for GTPU SN is equal to half range of GTPU SN (32767) so any GTPU SN received out of the receiving window should be considered as out of order (not applicable for starting point of counting, L2Hi shall handle first incoming GTP-U SN as described in 5G\_L2\_21923\_replaced([11233543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3ArH5_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For KPI purpose number of really lost packets may be calculated as: number of lost packets - number of packets received out of order.
6. All retransmissions shall be considered as new transmission from GTP-U protocol perspective as it does not support native GTP-U retransmission. All retx will be assigned new GTP-U SN and shall be considered in packet loss calculations.
7. Packets dropped at reception due to:

- bip overload protection (L2Hi discards packets when it runs out of bip descriptors for events),

- unsupported extension header,

shall be counted in normal way into received in order/out of order counters, but not counted in lost counter to not generate artificial losts (discarded packet is formally received packet; whereas lost is counted as difference between discarded packet and last received in order packet). Cases when packets are dropped at reception like: parsing error (malformed packet), no bearer found for packet (based on TEID), incorrect destination IP address shall not be included in received (in order/out of order) nor lost counter.

Note:

1. Packet Loss Rate KPI = (PDCP\_PDU\_LOST\_F1\_PMQP - PDCP\_PDU\_RCV\_F1\_OUTORD\_DU\_PMQP) / (PDCP\_PDU\_LOST\_F1\_PMQP + PDCP\_PDU\_RCV\_F1\_ORDR\_DU\_PMQP)

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11234972`)

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11234979`)

PM Counters
General information

---

**4.11.0-8.0-2.0-7.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11234984`)

PM Counters
For DL Xn-U Packet Loss Rate, L2Hi shall provide the following counters for NRPMQAP:

1. Number of DL PDCP PDUs that are lost over XN during Inter-gNB NR-DC (5G\_L2\_20766\_replaced([11234990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A1gAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on missed GTP-U SNs
2. Number of DL PDCP PDUs that are received at MN gNB-DU over XN in order (5G\_L2\_20768\_replaced([11234999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A1gAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on GTP-U SNs received in order
3. Number of DL PDCP PDUs that are received at MN gNB-DU over XN out of order (5G\_L2\_20770\_replaced([11235014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A2HAfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on GTP-U SNs received out of order
4. These counters are provided based on GTP-U sequence numbers assigned to GTP-U packets. GTP-U SN field is optional in GTP-U header. L2Hi CU SN (secondary node) shall assign GTP-U SNs only if actGtpUpSeqNum=TRUE (HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq:pmCountersInfo, 5G\_L2\_IF\_5258\_replaced([10987189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This flag set to TRUE means that L2Hi CU shall assign GTP-U SNs (please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28659\_replaced([11225210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyLzqvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Data packets (GTP-U carrying PDCP SDU) shall always contain GTP-U SN once flag for this function is activated so that L2Hi DU could consider those packets in counters for DL Xn-U Packet Loss Rate. Counters shall be updated by L2Hi DU MN (master node) only if GTP-U SN will be present in GTP-U packets. L2Hi DU should not get duplicated GTP-U SN on any interface since there is no retx concept on GTP-U (If duplicated GTP-U SN will appear, L2Hi shall accept that packet, and repeated sequence number shall be counted as out of order). GTP-U SN should be assigned only for G-PDU packets with DUD extension header and PDCP Data PDUs (so with non-zero payload) as well as for PDCP control PDUs (ROHC feedback, PDCP status report). In case of pure polling (DUD without DL data packet) and GTP-U control PDUs (like SEHN, Error Indication, Tunnel Status, End Marker), GTP-U SN shall not be assigned. If packet will be a G-PDU packet and will have GTP-U SN assigned, L2Hi shall handle it and report it into counters.
5. Packet shall be counted as lost when there is a gap in the GTPU SN received in order. Such packet may be later received out of order or never received (really lost). Packet received out of order is also counted as lost. Receiving window for GTPU SN is equal to half range of GTPU SN (32767) so any GTPU SN received out of the receiving window should be considered as out of order (not applicable for starting point of counting, L2Hi shall handle first incoming GTP-U SN as described in 5G\_L2\_21923\_replaced([11233543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3ArH5_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For KPI purpose number of really lost packets may be calculated as: number of lost packets - number of packets received out of order.
6. All retransmissions shall be considered as new transmission from GTP-U protocol perspective as it does not support native GTP-U retransmission. All retx will be assigned new GTP-U SN and shall be considered in packet loss calculations.
7. Packets dropped at reception due to:

- bip overload protection (L2Hi discards packets when it runs out of bip descriptors for events),

- unsupported extension header,

shall be counted in normal way into received in order/out of order counters, but not counted in lost counter to not generate artificial losts (discarded packet is formally received packet; whereas lost is counted as difference between discarded packet and last received in order packet). Cases when packets are dropped at reception like: parsing error (malformed packet), no bearer found for packet (based on TEID), incorrect destination IP address shall not be included in received (in order/out of order) nor lost counter.

Note:

1. Packet Loss Rate KPI = (PDCP\_PDU\_LOST\_XN\_PMQP - PDCP\_PDU\_RCV\_XN\_OUTORD\_DU\_PMQP) / (PDCP\_PDU\_LOST\_XN\_PMQP + PDCP\_PDU\_RCV\_XN\_ORDR\_DU\_PMQP)

NetAct name: UL\_RLC\_AM\_SDU\_RX\_INI\_TRANS

PI ID: M55349C00075

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: This counter provides the total number of UL RLC SDUs received in RLC AM by initial transmission.

Note:

1. Only initial transmissions are counted.
2. DRBs which are UL CA configured as well as not configured are conisdered. For UL CA DRB, initial transmissions via P(S)Cell or SCell(s) are counted in P(S)Cell.
3. This counter is only for FR1.
4. Both SA & NSA RLC AM SDUs are considered.
5. RLC SDUs which are received as complete RLC SDUs are counted. RLC SDUs received as RLC SDU segments are ignored in this calculation.

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update this counter on P(S)Cell when an AM RLC SDU is successfully received by initial transmission.

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-1.0-2.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `12689736`)

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-1.0-2.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12689737`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR High RLC Report Cell (NHRRC)  
NetAct name: RLC\_SDU\_CELL\_THP\_UL\_MAX  
PI ID: M55349C00087  
Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD.

Update time:

If NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount has "RLC SDU Cell level peak throughput PM Counters" selected (i.e.,Bit 0:RLCSDUPEAKTHPUT is set in HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall sample every 1 sec the cumulative received UL RLC SDU volume of all DRBs in NRCELL and report the maximum value from all samples during the measurement period.

Increment value:

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute cumulative received UL RLC SDU volume of all DRBs in NRCELL during sampling interval of 1 sec, compares against cumulated UL RLC SDU volume computed in previous sampling interval of 1 sec and updates if current value is bigger than previous value.

Additional Information:

1. In case of CA, UL RLC SDU volume received via SCell is pegged in PCell of that DRB and RLC\_SDU\_CELL\_THP\_DL\_MAX is not updated in SCell.
2. In case of online modification of NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount to select or deselect  "RLC SDU Cell level peak throughput PM Counters" then 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall consider new value of Bit 0:RLCSDUPEAKTHPUT in HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount immediately from the next sampling interval.

M55314C05020 (UL\_PDCP\_VOL\_SNT\_F1\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... UL\_PDCP\_VOL\_SNT\_F1\_QoS\_GRP\_20) counters in Bytes and BOAM shall convert to kB.

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11235319`)

PM Counters
UL RLC PDU and UL RLC data PDU volume discarded due to other causes - SRB2 and SRB3

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11235325`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (RLC) shall increment the following counters when UL RLC PDUs are discarded due to reasons other than during Bearer Release procedure

M55311C36003 (UL\_RLC\_VOL\_D\_OTH\_H\_SRB3) UL RLC data PDU volume discarded by RLC due to other causes - SRB3

M55311C37003 (UL\_RLC\_PDU\_D\_OTH\_H\_SRB3) UL RLC data PDUs discarded by RLC due to other causes - SRB3

[5GC000752-F] M55311C36002 (UL\_RLC\_VOL\_D\_OTH\_H\_SRB2) UL RLC data PDU volume discarded by high RLC due to other causes - SRB2

[5GC000752-F] M55311C37002 (UL\_RLC\_PDU\_D\_OTH\_H\_SRB2) UL RLC data PDUs discarded by high RLC due to other causes - SRB2

UL RLC PDUs or PDU segments can be discarded due to the following reasons (not limited to):

* Full buffer
* UL PDUs or PDU segments fall outside of the receiving window
* UL PDUs or PDU segments are detected as duplicate
* Protocol error (Invalid LIs detected in UL PDUs/PDU segments or Invalid SO detected in UL PDUs/PDU segments)

---

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11235335`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (RLC) shall increment the following counters during the bearer release procedure (during cleanup of resources)

M55311C34003 (UL\_RLC\_VOL\_D\_RBR\_H\_SRB3) UL RLC data PDU volume discarded by RLC due to bearer release - SRB3 - total number of UL RLC PDU or PDU segment bytes discarded for SRB3

M55311C35003 (UL\_RLC\_PDU\_D\_RBR\_H\_SRB3) UL RLC data PDUs discarded by RLC due to bearer release - SRB3 - total number of UL RLC PDUs or PDU segments discarded for SRB3

[5GC000752-F] M55311C34002 (UL\_RLC\_VOL\_D\_RBR\_H\_SRB2) UL RLC data PDU volume discarded by high RLC due to bearer release - SRB2

[5GC000752-F] M55311C35002 (UL\_RLC\_PDU\_D\_RBR\_H\_SRB2) UL RLC data PDUs discarded by high RLC due to bearer release - SRB2

PI ID: M55404C00006

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall increment this counter per PMQAP profile by 1 when UL RLC Data PDU is requested for retransmission at RLC level. This counter is PMQAP version of the legacy QoS Counters UL\_RLC\_PDU\_RETX\_H\_QOS\_GRP\_01...UL\_RLC\_PDU\_RETX\_H\_QOS\_GRP\_20 defined in [11235447: Number of RLC Data PDUs requested for retransmission](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

Measurement: NR High RLC Report Cell (NHRRC)

NetAct name: UL\_RLC\_PDU\_RETX\_HPI ID: M55349C00093

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update this counter at Cell Level when status report requesting for retransmission of missing UL RLC PDUs/PDU segments is sent towards 5G-L2-LO and irrespective of value of HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to PMQAP/QoS ([10989717: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WnnoPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). In case of Carrier Aggregation (CA), this counter shall be pegged on the PCell only.

Increment value: This counter shall be incremented at Cell Level by 1 when UL RLC Data PDU is requested for retransmission at RLC level. This counter is Cell Level version of the legacy QoS Counters UL\_RLC\_PDU\_RETX\_H\_QOS\_GRP\_01...UL\_RLC\_PDU\_RETX\_H\_QOS\_GRP\_20 defined in [11235447: Number of RLC Data PDUs requested for retransmission](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

PM Counters
Measurement: NR High RLC Report Cell

NetAct name: RLC\_PDU\_VOL\_RX\_SEC\_SA\_CA\_FR1

PI ID: M55349C00025

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

UL RLC SDU throughput mechanism

PM Counters
Measuring UL RLC SDU throughput mechanism

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11235505`)

PM Counters
Burst Identification

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11235519`)

PM Counters
**[Before 04286263]**

Uplink burst relies on UE buffer state.

5G-L2-HI DU shall start a burst when UE buffer becomes nonempty due to reception of LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = FALSE and then the first PDU (LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd).

5G-L2-HI DU shall end given burst if:

 Received LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd message indicates empty UE buffer for this bearer,

OR

 Bearer Delete reception.

Note:

1) 5G-L2-Hi shall take into account reordering of the PDUs and consider end of the burst as the timestamp of the latest (but not last) received PDU.

2)  If thpTimeCalc = 1 (enabled) received via HiUserDu\_BearerSetupReq, 5G-L2-Hi DU shall consider:

 L1Timestamp **(composed of sfn, slot, btuNr, slotDurationUs and slotInFrame)** received via **LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd to get the TB reception time.**\*\*\*\*

 and LoDataUeID & L2LoAddress Pair received via LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd to differentiate between PCell and SCell burst.

**[04286263]**

Uplink burst relies on UE buffer state.

When there is no ongoing Burst, 5G-L2-HI DU shall start a burst with reception of first PDU via LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd (refer 5G\_L2\_IF\_3501\_replaced([10985970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WLizvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) either from PCell or SCell.

5G-L2-HI DU shall end given burst if:

· Received LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd (refer 5G\_L2\_IF\_3509\_replaced([10986199](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WNX-vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message indicates empty UE buffer for this bearer,

OR

· Bearer Delete reception.

Note:

1) 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall take into account reordering of the PDUs and consider end of the burst as the timestamp of the latest (but not last) received PDU.

2) 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall consider:

 L1Timestamp **(composed of sfn, slot, btuNr, slotDurationUs and slotInFrame)** received via **LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd (refer 5G\_L2\_IF\_3509\_replaced([10986199](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WNX-vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to get the TB reception time.**\*\*\*\*

 LoDataUeID & L2LoAddress Pair received in LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd (refer 5G\_L2\_IF\_3509\_replaced([10986199](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WNX-vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd (refer 5G\_L2\_IF\_3501\_replaced([10985970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WLizvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used to differentiate between PCell/SCell burst which helps in computing below counters

1. UL Per CC UE Throughput Counters (5G\_L2\_17783\_replaced([11235671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6YfvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_17798\_replaced([11235755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6_jPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & 5G\_L2\_17803\_replaced([11235771](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6_j_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to know Burst start time for Pcell and Scell

2. UL RLC PDU volume received over secondary path for FR1 SA CA (5G\_L2\_17066\_replaced([11235478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

3) In case of UL CA, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall start a burst with reception of first PDU (LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd) either from PCell or SCell and shall end given burst if LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd message with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE is received either from PCell or SCell.

**[End 04286263]**

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11235526`)

PM Counters
Exclusions

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11235532`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI DU shall exclude transmission time and volume of:

1. burst, which is:

a. smaller than [Before CB008009-B] VolThresholdDiscard [CB008009-B] volThresDiscardUl [End CB008009-B]

OR

b. shorter than [Before CB008009-B] DurationThresholdDiscard [CB008009-B] durationThresDiscardUl [End CB008009-B].

2. Last slot when the buffer is emptied according to 5G\_L2\_3082\_replaced([11235505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KXvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Notes:

1. [Before CB008009-B] VolThresholdDiscard and DurationThresholdDiscard [CB008009-B] volThresDiscardUl and durationThresDiscardUl [End CB008009-B] are configured per bearer and delivered to 5G-L2-HI DU via HiUserDu\_BearerSetupReq. If any of these thresholds is set to 0, 5G-L2-Hi DU shall report burst only if the value is greater than 0. However, if thresholds are not set at all, 5G-L2-Hi DU shall use default values.

2. According to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6184\_replaced([11228541](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyjABfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PDU data, (i.e. volume and time) of PDUs received in last slot when ueBufferEmpty=true shall be excluded from burst volume and duration calculations. When last slot PDUs was received with ueBufferEmpty=false followed by empty buffer information in a separate message (LoData\_UeBufferEmptyInd) 5G-L2-Hi shall include those PDUs in burst volume and duration calculations.

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11235556`)

PM Counters
Mobility cases during Measuring UL RLC SDU throughput

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11235561`)

PM Counters
Upon reception of HiUserDu\_BearerModifyReq message, 5G-L2-HI shall check if the newly received NrCellIdentity parameter value is set and is different than previously set (in HiCnfgDu\_BearerSetupReq or HiCnfgDu\_BearerModifyReq).

If this condition is fulfilled, 5G-L2-HI shall stop the Burst and incrementing counters for old NrCellIdentity and start incrementing counters for new NrCellIdentity.

Rationale: The new NrCellIdentinty represents the Target cell in case of intra-gNB Handover, when only modification of bearer is needed.

Note: the inter-RAT or inter-gNB Handover types need creating new bearer contexts in CU and DU L2-HI instances, so they are handled by bearer setup requests.

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11235567`)

PM Counters
Histogram

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11235572`)

PM Counters
Scale and ranges

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11235578`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-Hi DU shall provide the distribution of the UE throughput in UL via histogram based on throughput distribution counters (please refer to 5G\_L2\_ 9885) and UL burst definition (please refer to 5G\_L2\_\_3082).

To configure the throughput ranges of the histogram, 5G-L2-HI DU shall use the following NIDD Distribution Parameters obtained via HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq:

 HistScale [Linear, Logarithmic]: This parameter allows the user to set the Histogram BIN distribution ranges as Linear or Logarithmic scale.

 HistUplinkMaxRange [bps]: This parameter set's the lower bound in range of the highest BIN. This value is the estimated value of the highest BIN i.e. BIN 20 for UL throughput distribution. NOTE: This is an estimated max, thus if during calculation, the UL throughput for a certain measurement period exceeds this value, it is still reported under BIN 20.

 HistUplinkMinRange [bps]: This parameter set's the upper bound in range of the lowest BIN. This value is the highest value of the lowest BIN i.e. BIN 01 for UL throughput distribution.

Note. This parameter is set only when the HistScale parameter is set as Logarithmic.

Note:

1) The distribution of the histogram shall be spread into 20 BINs.

2) 5G-L2-Hi DU shall use PMQAP Profile (please refer to 5G\_L2\_3343\_replaced([11235547](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5xbfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for creating distribution counters when distribution to BIN is done for the Throughput counters per QCI, 5QI, PLMN and Slice. BIN definition is for each PMQAP profile and one for non-PMQAP.

3) The BIN range is set as follows: lower range < thr value < = upper range and under the following excel file: <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB008000%20-%20CB008499/CFAM/CB008009%20Throughput%20distribution%20counters/CB008009%20bin%20ranges.xlsx?d=w3b92ddb0513648e382571ad32c7b126d&csf=1&web=1&e=IpbrPf>

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11235583`)

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11235592`)

[CB013684-G]

[End CB013684-G]

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11235614`)

PM Counters
Volume Counters

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12689012`)

PM Counters
ThpVolUl UL UE throughput volume at RLC SDU level Total

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12688853`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR High RLC Report Cell (NHRRC)  
NetAct name: UL\_RLC\_SDU\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_TOT  
PI ID: M55349C00085  
Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD.

Update time:

For each UL RLC Burst identified as per 11235505, if HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actIpThpt = TRUE (See 10989717), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update this counter with RLC SDU level volume of UL data burst.

Increment value:

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall increment the counter with RLC SDU level volume of UL data burst, excluding the RLC SDU volume transmitted in the last slot when the buffer is emptied (see 11235532).

Additional Information:

1. Legacy UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_TOT (M55349C03001) counter are updated with RLC PDU level volume of UL data burst.
2. Similar to legacy UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_TOT (M55349C03001) counter, this UL\_RLC\_SDU\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_TOT counter shall only be pegged at PCell.
3. Legacy discard mechanism of UL data burst based on UL RLC PDU as described in 11235526 is not changed. 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall discard RLC SDU level volume of UL data burst if UL data burst based on UL RLC PDU is discarded as described in 11235526
4. Existing LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd message from 5G-L2-LO to 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall provide RLC PDU volume and 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute UL RLC SDU size for updating this counter. RLC SDU size is calculated as RLC PDU Size - RLC Header Size.

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12689319`)

PM Counters
ThpVolUl UL UE Throughput Volume at RLC SDU level Total NRPMQAP

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12689323`)

PM Counters
Measurement: High RLC Cell NRPMQAP (HRLCQ)  
NetAct name: UL\_RLC\_SDU\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_PMQAP  
PI ID: M55353C00034  
Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD.

Update time:

For each UL RLC Burst identified as per 11235505, if HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actIpThpt = TRUE (See 10989717), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update this counter with RLC SDU level volume of UL data burst at PMQAP level. Also, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall exclude RLC SDU level volume of UL data burst as per 11235532.

Increment value:

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall increment the counter with RLC SDU level volume of UL data burst at PMQAP level, excluding the RLC SDU volume transmitted in the last slot when the buffer is emptied (see 11235532).

Additional Information:

1. Legacy PMQAP level UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_PMQAP (M55353C00001) counter is updated with RLC PDU level volume of UL data burst.
2. Similar to legacy PMQAP level UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_PMQAP (M55353C00001), this UL\_RLC\_SDU\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_PMQAP counter shall only be pegged at PCell.
3. Existing LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd message from 5G-L2-LO to 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall provide RLC PDU volume and 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute UL RLC SDU size for updating this counter. RLC SDU size is calculated as RLC PDU Size - RLC Header Size.

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `13384078`)

PM Counters
Volume of multi-slot UL data bursts that are less than discard parameters at RLC PDU level for FR1

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13384080`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR High RLC Report Cell (NHRRC)

NetAct name: UL\_RLC\_PDU\_VOL\_BURST\_DISC\_THR

PI ID: M55349C00099

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update this counter with RLC PDU level volume of UL data burst (as explained in [11235505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KXvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if this UL data burst gets discarded due to discard thresholds (volThresDiscardUl and durationThresDiscardUl) as explained in [11235526: Exclusions](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5xY_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actIpThpt is set to TRUE (See [10989717: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WnnoPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). This counter shall be pegged on the PCell only. This counter is applicable only for FR1 both SA and NSA DRBs. This counter is applicable for both CA and non-CA configurations.

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall increment the counter at Cell Level with RLC PDU volume of UL data burst that gets discarded due to discard thresholds (volThresDiscardUl and durationThresDiscardUl) as explained in [11235526: Exclusions](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5xY_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall include last slot volume of UL data burst (as explained in [11235505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KXvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in this counter.

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-5**  (ID: `13384082`)

PM Counters
Volume of multi-slot UL data bursts that are less than discard parameters at RLC PDU level NRPMQAP for FR1

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13384085`)

PM Counters
Measurement:  High RLC Cell NRPMQAP2 (HRLCQ2)

NetAct name: UL\_RLC\_VOL\_BURST\_DISC\_THR\_PMQP

PI ID: M55404C00012

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update this counter per PMQAP profile with RLC PDU level volume of UL data burst (as explained in [11235505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KXvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if this UL data burst gets discarded due to discard parameters (volThresDiscardUl and durationThresDiscardUl) as explained in [11235526: Exclusions](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5xY_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actIpThpt is set to TRUE (See [10989717: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WnnoPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). This counter shall be pegged on the PCell only. This counter is applicable only for FR1 both SA and NSA DRBs. This counter is applicable for both CA and non-CA configurations.

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall increment the counter per PMQAP profile with RLC PDU volume of UL data burst that gets discarded due to discard parameters (volThresDiscardUl and durationThresDiscardUl) as explained in [11235526: Exclusions](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5xY_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall include last slot volume of UL data burst (as explained in [11235505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KXvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in this counter.

Max Counters

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11235646`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI DU shall update uplink max throughput counter for the cell M55349C02001 (MAX\_UL\_RLC\_UE\_TPUT) Max UL UE throughput transmitted for the cell , with Uplink throughput ThpUli value calculated for each valid burst occurring on any QoS group, only if the current calculated throughput is greater than the previous max value.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in italics. The equation is:
$ThpUli = \frac{ThpVolUli}{TheTimeUli}$, where
The equation defines $ThpUli$ as the ratio of $ThpVolUli$ to $TheTimeUli$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_14899.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

 ThpUli- Throughput of i-th uplink burst

 ThpVolUli– Volume of i-th uplink burst

 ThpTimeUli- Time of i-th uplink burst

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11235654`)

PM Counters

 M55349C06000 … M55349C06019 (UL\_RLC\_UE\_TPUT\_BIN1… UL\_RLC\_UE\_TPUT\_BIN20) UL UE Throughput at RLC SDU Level BIN1-20

 M55353C01002 … M55353C01021 (UL\_RLC\_UE\_TPUT\_BIN1\_PMQAP… UL\_RLC\_UE\_TPUT\_BIN20\_PMQAP) UL UE Throughput at RLC SDU Level BIN1-20 per profile

for each identified burst (See 5G\_L2\_3082\_replaced([11235505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KXvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-8.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13383992`)

PM Counters
Measurement: High RLC Cell NRPMQAP2 (HRLCQ2)

NetAct name: UL\_RLC\_VOL\_RX\_H\_PMQAP

PI ID: M55404C00002

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall increment this counter per PMQAP profile with number of UL RLC SDU bytes received and transmitted to the higher layer. This counter is PMQAP version of the legacy QoS Counters UL\_RLC\_VOL\_RX\_H\_QOS\_GRP\_01...UL\_RLC\_VOL\_RX\_H\_QOS\_GRP\_20 defined in [11235661: Measuring UL RLC SDU received bytes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6YfPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). This counter shall not include Control PDU bytes nor discarded UL RLC PDU bytes.

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-9.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11235705`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (DU) stores new value of PmCountersInfo.actPerCCULUserThpt (described in 5G\_L2\_IF\_5263\_replaced([10989717](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WnnoPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and

[Before CB010636-C-UPD001]

Online modification of PmCountersInfo.actPerCCULUserThpt is applied for all existing and newly created bearers.

[CB010636-C-UPD001]

 if PmCountersInfo.actPerCCULUserThpt is modified from TRUE to FALSE, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall not compute UL per CC UE Throughput counters (5G\_L2\_17794\_replaced([11235715](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6_h_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only for newly created bearers that are created after this modification.

OR

* if PmCountersInfo.actPerCCULUserThpt is modified from FALSE to TRUE, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute UL per CC UE Throughput counters (5G\_L2\_17794\_replaced([11235715](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6_h_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only for newly created bearers that are created after this modification.

[End CB010636-C-UPD001]

UL Per CC Combination ThroughPut

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-9.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11235715`)

PM Counters
UL Per CC Combination ThroughPut Computation

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-9.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11235738`)

PM Counters
[Before 04286263]

As explained in 5G\_L2\_3082\_replaced([11235505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KXvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute UL Bursts based on LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd (ueBufferEmpty = FALSE/TRUE) and LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd.

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall start UL Burst when either PCell or SCell or both L2-LO Instances send LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = FALSE and then LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall end UL Burst when each L2-LO Instance sends explicit LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE if corresponding L2-LO Instance sent LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd earlier.

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute per CC UL throughput counters by determining the subsplits of merged global Burst.

Subsplits of merged global Burst is determined when any of the below conditions satisfies:

1. either Pcell or SCell sends (LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = FALSE and then LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd)
2. either Pcell or SCell sends (LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE)

UL Per CC UE Throughput computation is illustrated with the help of below example for CA Case with 1 Primary Cell and 1 Secondary Cell (SCell1).

In below example,

V1 = Total volume of all RLC PDUs of Burst1 reported from PCell L2-LO Instance

T1 = Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU (LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = FALSE and then LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd) received for PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst1

-

Timestamp when LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE received from PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst1

V2 = Total volume of all RLC PDUs of Burst2 reported from SCell1 L2-LO Instance

T2 = Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU (LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = FALSE and then LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd) received for SCell1 L2-LO Instance for Burst2

-

Timestamp when LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE received from SCell1 L2-LO Instance for Burst2

V3 = Total volume of all RLC PDUs of Burst3 reported from PCell L2-LO Instance

T3 = Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU (LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = FALSE and then LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd) received for PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst3

-

Timestamp when LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE received from PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst3

VM = Volume of Global Merged Burst

TM = Time duration of Global Merged Burst

1. Based on triggers for Burst Start or end from each L2-LO Instance, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute subsplit duration as below:

In below example, ta ... tg represent per CC time.

ta = T2s (Start of SCell1 Burst2) - T1s (Start of Pcell Burst1)

tb = T1e (End of Pcell Burst1) - T2s (Start of SCell1 Burst)

...

...

te = T3e (End of Pcell Burst2) - T2e (End of SCell1 Burst1)

1. For each subsplit time duration (computed in above step 1), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute volume during subsplit time duration:

per CC volume = per CC time \* (sum of average throughput of all L2-LO burst that are contributing to portion of global merged burst volume during this per CC time ta)

In below example, va ... ve represent per CC volume.

va = ta \* V1/T1

ta is overlapping completely with PCell Burst1 only so PCell Burst1 average throughput is considered.

Since here it is Pcell Burst1 only, ta and va get updated under 1CC counter.

ta and va get updated under 1CC counter since here only Pcell Burst1 are considered.

vb = tb \* ((V1/T1) + (V2/T2))

tb is overlapping completely with PCell Burst1 and SCell1 Burst and hence PCell Burst1 and SCell1 Burst average throughput are considered.

tb and vb get updated under 2CC counter since here only Pcell Burst1 and SCell Burst are considered.

...

...

ve = te \* V3/T3

1. Last slot exclusion is applied on global merged burst but not applied for each CC burst.

In below example, vs and ts are excluded from global merged burst. Hence vs and ts are excluded only for last per CC combination counter.

1. Finally at the end of global merged Burst, per CC throughput counters are updated as below for given example.

UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC ≈ va + vc + (ve-vs)

UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_2CC ≈ vb + vd

UL\_RLC\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC ≈ ta + tc + (te-ts)

UL\_RLC\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_2CC ≈ tb + td

UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_TOT ≈ VM- vs ≈ va + vc + (ve-vs) + vb + vd

U\_RLC\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT ≈ TM – ts ≈ ta + tc + (te-ts) + tb + td

Note:

1. UL per CC time and volume counters are pegged only in PCell and applicable only for FR1 non-GBR DRBs.
2. FR1 non-GBR, non-CA UL burst volume and time is considered under 1CC counters.
3. Per CC time and volume counters are applicable only for SA (5G\_L2\_17799\_replaced([11235760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6_jfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_17804\_replaced([11235775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A7mkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
4. Per CC time and volume counters are applicable for all CA Types (intra-gNB and inter-gNB)

[04286263]

As explained in 5G\_L2\_3082\_replaced([11235505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A5KXvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall start UL Burst when either PCell or SCell or both L2-LO Instances send LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd.

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall end UL Burst when either PCell or SCell L2-LO Instance sends LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE.

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute per CC UL throughput counters by determining the subsplits of merged global Burst.

Subsplits of merged global Burst is determined when any of the below conditions satisfies:

1. either Pcell or SCell sends LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd
2. either Pcell or SCell sends LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE.

UL Per CC UE Throughput computation is illustrated with the help of below example for CA Case with 1 Primary Cell and 1 Secondary Cell (SCell1).

In below example, there are 3 merged global Bursts (Burst 1, Burst 2 and Burst 3) and where

V1 = Total volume of all RLC PDUs reported from PCell L2-LO Instance till end of Burst 1

T1 = Timestamp when Burst 1 ended with reception of LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE from PCell L2-LO Instance.

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd from PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst1

V2 = Total volume of all RLC PDUs reported from SCell L2-LO Instance till end of Burst 1

T2 = Timestamp when Burst 1 ended with reception of LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE from PCell L2-LO Instance.

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd from SCell L2-LO Instance for Burst1

V3 = Total volume of all RLC PDUs reported from SCell L2-LO Instance till end of Burst 2

T3 = Timestamp when Burst 2 ended with reception of LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE from SCell L2-LO Instance.

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd (i.e after Burst 1 ended) from SCell L2-LO Instance for Burst2

V4 = Total volume of all RLC PDUs reported from PCell L2-LO Instance till end of Burst 2

T4 = Timestamp when Burst 2 ended with reception of LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE from SCell L2-LO Instance.

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd (i.e after Burst 1 ended) from PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst2

V5 = Total volume of all RLC PDUs reported from PCell L2-LO Instance till end of Burst 3

T5 = Timestamp when Burst 3 ended with reception of LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE from PCell L2-LO Instance.

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd (i.e after Burst 2 ended) from PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst3

1. Based on triggers for Burst Start or end from each L2-LO Instance, 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute subsplit duration as below:

In below example, ta ... tg represent per CC time.

ta = Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd from SCell L2-LO Instance for Burst1

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd from PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst1

tb = Timestamp when Burst 1 ended with reception of LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE from PCell L2-LO Instance.

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd from SCell L2-LO Instance for Burst1

tc = Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd from PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst2

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd from SCell L2-LO Instance for Burst2

td = Timestamp when Burst 2 ended with reception of LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE from SCell L2-LO Instance.

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd from PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst2

te = Timestamp when Burst 3 ended with reception of LoDataUeBufferEmptyInd with ueBufferEmpty = TRUE from PCell L2-LO Instance.

-

Timestamp when 1st RLC PDU received with LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd from PCell L2-LO Instance for Burst3

1. For each subsplit time duration (computed in above step 1), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall compute volume during subsplit time duration:

per CC volume = per CC time \* (sum of average throughput of all L2-LO burst that are contributing to portion of global merged burst volume during this per CC time ta)

In below example, va ... ve represent per CC volume.

va = ta \* V1/T1

ta is overlapping completely with PCell only and hence PCell average throughput (V1/T1) is considered.

Since here it is Pcell Burst1 only, ta and va get updated under 1CC counter.

vb = tb \* ((V1/T1) + (V2/T2))

tb is overlapping completely with PCell and SCell Burst. Hence PCell average throughput (V1/T1) and SCell average throughput (V2/T2) are considered.

tb and vb get updated under 2CC counter since here both Pcell and SCell are considered.

...

...

ve = te \* V3/T3

1. Last slot exclusion is applied on each global merged burst (i.e., Burst 1, Burst 2 and Burst 3) but not applied for each CC burst.

In below example, vs and ts are excluded from global merged Burst 3. Hence vs and ts are excluded only for last per CC combination counter i.e 1CC.

1. Finally at the end of 3 global merged Bursts (i.e., Burst 1, Burst 2 and Burst 3) , per CC throughput counters are updated as below for given example.

UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC ≈ va + vc + (ve-vs)

UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_2CC ≈ (vb-vp) + (vd-vr)

UL\_RLC\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC ≈ ta + tc + (te-ts)

UL\_RLC\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_2CC ≈ (tb-tp) + (td-tr)

UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_TOT ≈ va + vc + (ve-vs) + (vb-vp) + (vd-vr)

U\_RLC\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT ≈ ta + tc + (te-ts) + (tb-tp) + (td-tr)

Note:

1. UL per CC time and volume counters are pegged only in PCell and applicable only for FR1 non-GBR DRBs.
2. FR1 non-GBR, non-CA UL burst volume and time is considered under 1CC counters.
3. Per CC time and volume counters are applicable only for SA (5G\_L2\_17799\_replaced([11235760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6_jfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_17804\_replaced([11235775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A7mkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
4. Per CC time and volume counters are applicable for all supported UL CA Types.

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-9.0-4.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11235765`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR High RLC Report Cell

NetAct name: UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC ... UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_2CC

PI ID: M55349C00042 ... M55349C00043

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: These 1CC ... 2CC counters are updated when HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPerCCULUserThhpt is TRUE and only for FR1 SA nonGBR DRBs which are configured with secondary L2-LO Instance (either local or remote). These counters provide portion (as computed in 5G\_L2\_17794\_replaced([11235715](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6_h_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of UL data burst (ThpVolUl, 5G\_L2\_3079\_replaced([11235614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6YdPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which was received during the 1CC ... 2CC duration of UL burst.

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update portion (as computed in 5G\_L2\_17794\_replaced([11235715](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6_h_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of UL data burst (ThpVolUl, 5G\_L2\_3079\_replaced([11235614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6YdPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which was received during the 1CC ... 2CC duration of UL burst.

Note:

1. 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall identify DRB as SA or NSA based on PmCountersInfo.typeOfBearer received in HiUserDu\_BearerSetupReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_4188\_replaced([10990186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WqD5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
2. For FR1 SA nonGBR DRBs that are not configured with secondary L2-LO Instance (either local or remote), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update UL Burst Volume ThpVolUl (5G\_L2\_3079\_replaced([11235614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6YdPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) under UL\_RLC\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC (M55349C00042)  counter.

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-3.0-9.0-4.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12819374`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR High RLC Report Cell

NetAct name: UL\_RLC\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC ... UL\_RLC\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_2CC

PI ID: M55349C00044 ... M55349C00045

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Update time:

These 1CC ... 2CC counters are updated when HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPerCCULUserThhpt is TRUE and only for FR1 SA nonGBR DRBs which are configured with secondary L2-LO Instance (either local or remote).

These counters provide portion (as computed in [11234748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of ThpTimeUl ([11235626](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6YdvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) during which 1CC ... 2CC portion of UL Burst  is received.

Increment value:

5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update the portion (as computed in [11234748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A0R1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of ThpTimeUl ([11235626](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6YdvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) during which 1CC ... 2CC portion of UL Burst is received. [PR854412] These counters will be reported by 5G-L2-HI in microseconds, and OAM will convert them to milliseconds. [End PR854412]

Note:

1. 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall identify DRB as SA or NSA based on PmCountersInfo.typeOfBearer received in HiUserDu\_BearerSetupReq ([10990186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WqD5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. For FR1 SA nonGBR DRBs that are not configured with secondary L2-LO Instance (either local or remote), 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall update ThpTimeDl ([11235626](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6YdvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) under UL\_RLC\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT\_FR1\_SA\_1CC (M55349C00044) counter.

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11235795`)

RLC entity in 5G-L2-HI shall send uplink RLC SDUs containing SRB data to C-Plane.

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-4.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11235799`)

PM Counters
In the uplink, when the RLC entity in 5G-L2-HI decides to send RLC SDU(s) for SRB to the upper layers [5G\_UP\_IF\_3270\_replaced([11529001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWEyZfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))], 5G-L2-HI shall send HiSgnlDu\_SrbReceiveInd as per [5G\_L2\_IF\_1247\_replaced([10991176](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WwKhfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11235805`)

PM Counters
UL RLC SDU and UL RLC SDU volume received by RLC - SRB1, SRB2 and SRB3

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-4.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11235808`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (RLC) shall increment the following counters when it transmits UL RLC SDUs (containing SRB data) to the C-Plane:

M55311C24003 (UL\_RLC\_VOL\_RX\_H\_SRB3) UL RLC SDU volume received by RLC - SRB3 - total number of RLC SDU bytes for SRB3

M55311C25003 (UL\_RLC\_SDU\_RX\_H\_SRB3) UL RLC SDUs received by RLC - SRB3 - total number of RLC SDUs for SRB3

[5GC000723-D] M55311C24001 (UL\_RLC\_VOL\_RX\_H\_SRB1) UL RLC SDU volume received by RLC - SRB1- total number of RLC SDU bytes for SRB1

[5GC000723-D] M55311C25001 (UL\_RLC\_SDU\_RX\_H\_SRB1) UL RLC SDUs received by RLC - SRB1- total number of RLC SDUs for SRB1

[5GC000752-F] M55311C24002 (UL\_RLC\_VOL\_RX\_H\_SRB2) UL RLC SDU volume received by high RLC - SRB2

[5GC000752-F] M55311C25002 (UL\_RLC\_SDU\_RX\_H\_SRB2) UL RLC SDUs received by high RLC - SRB2

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11235814`)

PM Counters
Recording the delay in handling UL RLC PDUs within gNB DU - SRB1, SRB2 and SRB3

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-4.0-1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13407207`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (RLC) shall increment the following counters to record the delay in handling UL RLC PDUs within gNB DU.

M55311C31003 (UL\_RLC\_DELAY\_H\_SRB3) UL RLC delay - SRB3 - sum of time (in us) taken for each UL RLC PDU for SRB3

M55311C41003 (UL\_RLC\_COML\_RX\_H\_SRB\_3) UL RLC SDUs received as complete RLC SDU by High RLC - SRB3- number of UL complete RLC SDUs transmitted to the higher layer for SRB3

[5GC000723-D] M55311C31001 (UL\_RLC\_DELAY\_H\_SRB1) UL RLC delay - SRB1 - sum of time (in us) taken for each UL RLC PDU for SRB1

[5GC000723-D] M55311C41001 (UL\_RLC\_COML\_RX\_H\_SRB\_1) UL RLC SDUs received as complete RLC SDU by High RLC - SRB1 - number of UL complete RLC SDUs transmitted to the higher layer for SRB1

[5GC000752-F] M55311C31002 (UL\_RLC\_DELAY\_H\_SRB2) UL RLC delay - SRB2

[5GC000752-F] M55311C41002 (UL\_RLC\_COML\_RX\_H\_SRB\_2) UL RLC SDUs received as complete RLC SDU by High RLC - SRB2

The delay is calculated as the time difference between reception of the RLC PDU including complete RLC SDU from the air interface and when the RLC SDU is sent towards PDCP. The start point corresponds to the end of the air interface slot when the MAC PDU including the complete RLC SDU is received.

To achieve this, the 5G-L2-LO would associate a time stamp to a complete RLC SDU and include this information while delivering this to the 5G-L2-HI. 5G-L2-HI shall then use this information to create the delta time when it would send this RLC SDU to PDCP.

[PR873731]  
Only RLC SDUs received as complete SDUs are counted. SDUs received as segments are ignored for this calculation.

The calculation shall compensate the offset between the internal BCN time and the air‑interface time relative to GPS (by default  86 µs), to ensure consistent timing across layers and components.

See BTS\_E2E\_TIMING\_1271 for details.

[End PR873731]

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11235824`)

PM Counters
DRB related counters

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11235830`)

PM Counters
Sum of RLC delay

---

**4.11.0-8.0-3.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11235840`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (RLC) shall increment the following counters provided the sum of UL RLC delay in gNB-DU of the given QoS Group. :

M55311C10001 ... 20 (UL\_RLC\_DELAY\_H\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) UL RLC delay - QoS Group 01 ... 20

[CNI-109641-J]

Notes:

Counters are calculated based on delays collected for RLC SDUs which weren't segmented.

Calculation of counter shall take into account the offset between the BCN time and air interface time compared to the BCN time at GPS timing, 86us by default, see BTS\_E2E\_TIMING\_1271 for details.

[End CNI-109641-J]

**4.11.0-8.0-4**  (ID: `11235846`)

**4.11.0-8.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11235850`)

PM Counters
Number of time intervals for which the L2HI-DU is in non-critical load state

---

**4.11.0-8.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11235857`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR L2 overload report per DU (L2OLD)

NetAct name: NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_L2\_DU

PI ID: M55383CRD50001

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time:

If rdCpuOverloadCounters (5G\_L2\_21298\_replaced([11233340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Ap5wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled, this R&D counter is updated for 5G-L2-HI (DU) by each 5G-L2-HI instance when average CPU load (as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13833\_replaced([11228977](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  for cloud and classical deployments) of this 5G-L2-HI instance over measurement interval (100ms) is greater than or equal to rdCpuNonCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13448\_replaced([11229407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyn4iPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than rdCpuCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13446\_replaced([11229333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kynRevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Increment value: Each 5G-L2-HI shall increment by 1 each time average CPU load (as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13833\_replaced([11228977](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of this 5G-L2-HI instance over measurement interval (100ms) is greater than or equal to rdCpuNonCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13448\_replaced([11229407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyn4iPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than rdCpuCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13446\_replaced([11229333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kynRevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Additional Information:

Classical Deployment:

1. In case of Classical Deployment, 5G-L2-HI (CU) and 5G-L2-HI (DU) are co-located and share the cores, average CPU load computed (as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13833\_replaced([11228977](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  ) will be same for both 5G-L2-HI (CU) and 5G-L2-HI (DU). Hence counters NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_PDCP\_CUUP and NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_RLC\_DU will have same values. Similarly, CRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_PDCP\_CUUP and CRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_RLC\_DU will have same values.

2. In case of multiple 5G-L2-HI instances, BOAM shall aggregate this counter values across multiple 5G-L2-HI instances and report the aggregated value under NRDU.

Cloud Deployment:

1. In case of Cloud Deployment, 5G-L2-HI instance in vDU only shall report this counter under NRDU.

Hence counters NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_PDCP\_CUUP and NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_RLC\_DU will have same values. Similarly, CRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_PDCP\_CUUP and CRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_RLC\_DU will have same values.

2. In case of multiple 5G-L2-HI instances, BOAM shall aggregate this counter values across multiple 5G-L2-HI instances and report the aggregated value under NRDU.

Cloud Deployment:

## 4.11.0-9 PM Counters 5G-L2-HI (CU) (ID: 11235872)

**4.11.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11235879`)

PM Counters
General

---

**4.11.0-9.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11235898`)

PM Counters
See 5G\_L2\_2776\_replaced([11233420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Aqg0PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for general information.

5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report PM counters with the following aggregation levels, for URI construction see 5G\_L2\_IF\_1490\_replaced([10994810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2XHW5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Granularity | Aggregation Level | Network Profile | First Feature |
| NRBTS | NRBTS | PLMN-MRBTS-NRBTS | 5GC000425-Y |
| NRBTS per PLMN | NRBTS,MNC | PLMN-MRBTS-NRBTS,MCC-MNC | 5GC000738-B |
| NRBTS per PLMN per Slice | NRBTS,MNC,SD | PLMN-MRBTS-NRBTS,MCC-MNC,SST-SD | 5GC001008-PD |
| NRCELL | NRBTS,NRCELL | PLMN-MRBTS-NRBTS-NRCELL | 5GC002637-A |
| [CB009352-B] NRCUUP [End CB009352-B] | NRBTS,NRCUUP | PLMN-MRBTS-NRBTS-NRCUUP | CB009352-B |
| [CNI-134375-H] NRPMQAP [End CNI-134375-H] | NRBTS,NRCELL,NRPMQAP | PLMN-MRBTS-NRBTS-NRCELL-NRPMQAP | CB006898-A |

1) 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report NRBTS specific PM counters per NRBTS.

* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall create a NRBTS object for NRBTS specific PM counters at reception of a HiCnfgCu\_AddressDistributionReq.
* Note that deletion of a NRBTS related object instance is not currently supported.

2) 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report PLMN specific PM counters per PLMN.

5G-L2-HI (CU) shall create a new PLMN related PM object per each new plmnId at reception of a HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.

* There can be up to 10 PLMNs per gNB.
* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall remove PLMN related PM object instance for each deleted plmnId from plmnDeleteList at reception of a HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.

Note: plmnDeleteList is processed prior to plmnAddList.

3) 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report Slice specific PM counters per Slice per PLMN, if PLMN per slice related PM objects exists.

* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall create a new PLMN Slice related PM object per each new plmnId/SNSSAI pair at reception of a HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.
* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall remove PLMN per slice related PM objects for each deleted plmnId/SNSSAI pair at reception of a HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.

4) 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report NRCELL specific PM counters per NRCELL.

* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall create a new NRCELL related PM object per each new cell in [Before CNI-134375-H] nrCellIdsForThroughputReporting [CNI-134375-H] nrCellIdsForCountersReporting [End CNI-134375-H] at reception of a HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.
* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall remove NRCELL per cell related PM objects for each deleted cell in [Before CNI-134375-H] nrCellIdsForThroughputReporting [CNI-134375-H] nrCellIdsForCountersReporting [End CNI-134375-H] at reception of a HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.

[CB009352-B]

5) 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report NRCUUP specific PM counters per NRCUUP.

* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall create a NRCUUP object instance for PM counters at reception of a HiCnfgCu\_AddressDistributionReq.
* Note that deletion of a NRCUUP related PM object instance is not currently supported.

[End CB009352-B]

[CNI-134375-H]

6) 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report NRPMQAP specific PM counters per NRPMQAP object.

* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall create a new NRPMQAP related PM object per each new profile in PmqapProfileList at reception of a HiCnfCu\_ConfigParamReq.
* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall remove NRPMQAP per profile related PM objects for each deleted profile in PmqapProfileList at reception of a HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.

[End CNI-134375-H]

**4.11.0-9.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11235920`)

PM Counters
L2Hi shall round down the following input measurements for VoNR mute rates PM Counters (please see the note below):

* time difference between two RTP packets
* voice packet interval

Note:

Above measurements are input for the following VoNR mute rates counters for DL and UL:

* Distribution of downlink backhaul interface mute for VoNR (5G\_L2\_19877\_replaced([11238813](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Number of VoNR active session for downlink backhaul interface (5G\_L2\_19878\_replaced([11238828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaBfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Distribution of uplink air interface mute for VoNR (5G\_L2\_19882\_replaced([11240103](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BdLCPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Number of VoNR active session for uplink air interface (5G\_L2\_19884\_replaced([11240120](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BdLC_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
