**4.11.0-9.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11235925`)

PM Counters
Detection and mobility cases handling for number of VoNR bearers with mute

---

**4.11.0-9.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11235955`)

PM Counters
[CB013550-A-UPD001]

Detection to update:

* counter for number of VoNR bearers with UL air interface mute (5G\_L2\_21227\_replaced([11240140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BdLDvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB013550-B-UPD001]

* counter for number of VoNR bearers with DL Backhaul interface mute (5G\_L2\_21225\_replaced([11238844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaCPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB013550-B-UPD001]

shall happen when 5G-L2-HI (CU) detect the updating of BIN Distribution of uplink air interface mute for VoNR  (5G\_L2\_19882\_replaced([11240103](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BdLCPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB013550-B-UPD001] or BIN Distribution of downlink backhaul interface mute for VoNR  (5G\_L2\_19877\_replaced([11238813](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) respectively [End CB013550-B-UPD001].

[04539084]

5G-L2-HI (CU) shall activate monitoring of DL Backhaul interface mute for VoNR (5G\_L2\_19877\_replaced([11238813](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after reception of first UL RTP or RTCP packet from the UE. (see Note)

[End 04539084]

For intra-gNB mobility cases, at the moment of the resume (with receive of HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause=Resume, 5G\_L2\_IF\_1033\_replaced([10988005](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WazWvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) there shall be a mute monitoring reset.

The period between the last packet on the source and the first packet on the target is not considered for counters:

* Distribution of downlink backhaul interface mute for VoNR (5G\_L2\_19877\_replaced([11238813](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Number of VoNR active session for downlink backhaul interface (5G\_L2\_19878\_replaced([11238828](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaBfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Distribution of uplink air interface mute for VoNR (5G\_L2\_19882\_replaced([11240103](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BdLCPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Number of VoNR active session for uplink air interface (5G\_L2\_19884\_replaced([11240120](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BdLC_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

For these counters mentioned above, voice mute monitoring is continued after reception of first RTP packet in target cell.

At the moment of intra-gNB HO:

* in case of inter cell HO - there is an update of VONR\_DL\_BHIF\_MUTE (5G\_L2\_21225\_replaced([11238844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaCPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and VONR\_UL\_AIRIF\_MUTE (5G\_L2\_21227\_replaced([11240140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BdLDvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in source cell if mute appeared before HO,
* in case of intra cell HO - VONR\_DL\_BHIF\_MUTE (5G\_L2\_21225\_replaced([11238844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaCPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and VONR\_UL\_AIRIF\_MUTE (5G\_L2\_21227\_replaced([11240140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BdLDvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are not updated and information if mute appeared before HO is kept till bearer delete or till next intra-gNB inter cell HO and then these counters shall be updated.

The following diagrams show, how L2Hi CU shall update the counters VONR\_DL\_BHIF\_MUTE (5G\_L2\_21225\_replaced([11238844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BTaCPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and VONR\_UL\_AIRIF\_MUTE (5G\_L2\_21227\_replaced([11240140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BdLDvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for different HO cases:

Inter-gNB HO:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays two diagrams illustrating a handover (HO) scenario in a cellular network, specifically involving gNB A and gNB B, each with Cell 1. Both diagrams depict a timeline with colored segments representing different states.
**Top Diagram:**
\* **gNB A, Cell 1:** A green segment followed by a red segment labeled "Mute".
\* **gNB B, Cell 1:** A blue segment followed by a red segment labeled "Mute".
\* **Text Box 1 (pointing to the transition between gNB A and gNB B):** "HO happens. Mute monitoring reset that means delete of source context and continuation of transmission on target side in other gNB when completely new bearer context is established. Bearer is released from Cell 1 in gNB A. Due to mute occured, counter is updated for Cell 1 in gNB A."
\* **Text Box 2 (pointing to gNB B, Cell 1):** "Bearer is released from Cell 1 in gNB B. Due to mute occured, counter is also updated for Cell 1 in gNB B."
**Bottom Diagram:**
\* **gNB A, Cell 1:** A green segment followed by a red segment labeled "Mute".
\* **gNB B, Cell 1:** A blue segment followed by a red segment labeled "Mute".
\* **Text Box 3 (pointing to the transition between gNB A and gNB B):** "HO happens. Mute monitoring reset that means delete of source context and continuation of transmission on target side in other gNB when completely new bearer context is established. Bearer is released from Cell 1 in gNB A. Due to mute occured, counter is updated for Cell 1 in gNB A."
\* **Text Box 4 (pointing to gNB B, Cell 1):** "Bearer is released from Cell 1 in gNB B. Due to mute did not occure at Cell 1 in gNB B, counter shall not be updated."
The diagrams visually represent two distinct outcomes of a handover event, focusing on the impact of a "mute" state and bearer release on counter updates in different gNBs. The top diagram shows counter updates in both gNB A and gNB B, while the bottom diagram shows a counter update in gNB A but not in gNB B, implying a difference in the mute occurrence or handling.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_14951.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Intra-gNB inter cell HO:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image displays two diagrams illustrating a scenario involving a gNB (Next Generation NodeB) named "gNB A" with two cells, "Cell 1" and "Cell 2". Each diagram shows a timeline with colored bars representing different states or durations within each cell.
**Top Diagram:**
\* **Cell 1:** A green bar is followed by a red bar labeled "Mute".
\* **Cell 2:** A green bar is followed by a blue bar, which is then followed by a red bar labeled "Mute".
\* **Annotation 1 (pointing to the transition between Cell 1 and Cell 2):** "HO happens. Mute monitoring reset. Bearer is released from Cell 1 in gNB A. Due to mute occured, counter is updated for Cell 1 in gNB A." This indicates a handover event, a reset of mute monitoring, and the release of a bearer from Cell 1, with a counter update for Cell 1 due to a mute event.
\* **Annotation 2 (pointing to the end of Cell 2's timeline):** "Bearer is released from Cell 2 in gNB A. Due to mute occured, counter is also updated for Cell 2 in gNB A." This signifies the release of a bearer from Cell 2, and a counter update for Cell 2 because a mute event occurred.
**Bottom Diagram:**
\* **Cell 1:** A green bar is followed by a red bar labeled "Mute".
\* **Cell 2:** A green bar is followed by a blue bar.
\* **Annotation 1 (pointing to the transition between Cell 1 and Cell 2):** "HO happens. Mute monitoring reset. Bearer is released from Cell 1 in gNB A. Due to mute occured, counter is updated for Cell 1 in gNB A." This annotation is identical to the first one in the top diagram.
\* **Annotation 2 (pointing to the end of Cell 2's timeline):** "Bearer is released from Cell 2 in gNB A. Due to mute did not occure at Cell 2 in gNB A, counter shall not be updated." This indicates the release of a bearer from Cell 2, but crucially, the counter for Cell 2 is *not* updated because a mute event did not occur in Cell 2.
The diagrams visually represent the impact of "mute" events on counter updates when a bearer is released from different cells within the same gNB, particularly in the context of a handover. The top diagram shows mute occurring in both cells, leading to counter updates in both. The bottom diagram shows mute occurring only in Cell 1, leading to a counter update for Cell 1 but not for Cell 2.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_14951.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Intra-gNB intra cell HO:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image displays two diagrams illustrating a scenario involving gNBs (Next Generation NodeBs) and cells, with a focus on "Mute" periods and Handover (HO) events. Each diagram consists of a horizontal bar representing a timeline, segmented into different colored sections and labeled with "Mute" or implied normal operation. Text boxes with arrows point to specific events on these timelines.
**Top Diagram:**
\* **Timeline:** Labeled "gNB A Cell 1".
\* Starts with a green segment.
\* Followed by a red segment labeled "Mute".
\* Then a blue segment.
\* Another red segment labeled "Mute".
\* **Event 1:** An upward arrow points from the end of the first "Mute" segment to a text box.
\* **Text Box Content:** "HO happens due to i.e. security key refreshment. Mute monitoring reset. L2Hi keeps information that mute was detected on source side to update the counter on bearer deletion."
\* **Event 2:** An upward arrow points from the end of the second "Mute" segment to a text box.
\* **Text Box Content:** "Bearer is released from Cell 1 in gNB A. Due to mute occured, counter is updated for Cell 1 in gNB A with the value 1 (no matter how many times mute occured till bearer release)."
**Bottom Diagram:**
\* **Timeline:** Labeled "gNB B Cell 1".
\* Starts with a green segment.
\* Followed by a red segment labeled "Mute".
\* Then a blue segment.
\* **Event 1:** An upward arrow points from the end of the "Mute" segment to a text box.
\* **Text Box Content:** "HO happens due to i.e. security key refreshment. Mute monitoring reset. L2Hi keeps information that mute was detected on source side to update the counter on bearer deletion."
\* **Event 2:** An upward arrow points from the end of the blue segment to a text box.
\* **Text Box Content:** "Bearer is released from Cell 1 in gNB A. Due to mute occured, counter is updated for Cell 1 in gNB A with the value 1 (no matter how many times mute occured till bearer release)."
The diagrams visually represent the impact of "Mute" periods and Handover events on a counter, particularly in the context of security key refreshment and bearer release. The top diagram shows a scenario within gNB A, while the bottom diagram shows a similar scenario involving gNB B and gNB A.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_14951.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

[End CB013550-A-UPD001]

[04539084]

Note:

After reception of first UL RTP or RTCP packet from the UE, internal message is sent from PDCP UL to PDCP DL to activate DL Backhaul VoNR mute monitoring. After activation, monitoring is started when 2 consecutive DL RTP packets are received from Core.

[End 04539084]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `12689853`)

PM Counters
Number of DL PDCP SDUs whose size is in Bin0...Bin9

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12689854`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell (PDCPC)  
NetAct name: DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN0...DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN9  
PI ID: M55350C00070...M55350C00079  
Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD.

Update time:

If NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount has "DL PDCP SDU size  
distribution PM counters" selected (i.e.,Bit 1: DLPDCPSDUSIZEDIST is set in HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount), 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall check the size of each received PDCP SDU and updates one of these BIN counters DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN0...DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN9 if received PDCP SDU size is within the respective counter BIN range.

Increment value:

5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment one of these BIN counters DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN0...DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN9 by 1, if received PDCP SDU size is within the respective counter BIN range.

Additional Information:

1. BIN range is defined as below:
2. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN0 is 0 Byte < x <= 31 Bytes
3. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN1 is 32 Bytes <= x <= 63 Bytes
4. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN2 is 64 Bytes <= x <= 95 Byte
5. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN3 is 96 Bytes <= x <= 223 Bytes
6. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN4 is 224 Bytes <= x <= 575 Bytes
7. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN5 is 576 Bytes <= x <= 991 Bytes
8. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN6 is 992 Bytes <= x <= 1215 Bytes
9. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN7 is 1216 Bytes <= x <= 1439 Bytes
10. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN8 is 1440 Bytes <= x <= 1504 Bytes
11. BIN range for DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SIZE\_BIN9 is > 1504 Bytes
12. 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall consider PDCP SDUs received in all below cases:
13. PDCP SDUs directly received from UPF.
14. PDCP SDUs received from the source gNB via direct data forwarding during XN handover. ([11195165: DL Data Forwarding for Inter-gNB mobility](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BftZ-_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
15. PDCP SDUs received from the source gNB via indirect data forwarding. ([11195165: DL Data Forwarding for Inter-gNB mobility](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BftZ-_vREe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
16. PDCP SDUs received from MeNB via data forwarding during SGNB addition. ([11188021: PSCell Addition](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfIyPfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
17. PDCP SDUs received from SN gNB PSCell to MN gNB PCell during inter-gNB split bearer takeback procedure. ([11191005: Bearer takeback (success)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BfYp0PvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
18. In case of online modification of NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount to select or deselect  "DL PDCP SDU size distribution PM counters" then 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall consider new value of Bit 1: DLPDCPSDUSIZEDIST in HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount immediately for the next PDCP SDU arriving at 5G-L2-HI (CU)

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-3.0-1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11236129`)

PM Counters
[Before CB008490-DT]

5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counters provided the number of DL PDCP SDU bytes discarded at PDCP level due to bearer release for the given QoS Group.:

M55320C01001 ... 20 (DL\_VOL\_DISC\_REL\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDU volume discarded due to bearer release - QoS Group 01 ... 20

[CB008490-DT]

Measurement: DL PDCP SDU volume discarded due to bearer release - QoS Group 01 ... 20

NetAct name: DL\_VOL\_DISC\_REL\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20

PI ID: M55320C01001 ... 20

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Additional info:

In case when Traffic Shaping functionality is enabled (L2TrafficShapingXxFwdParams (5G\_L2\_IF\_6905\_replaced([10988127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WcBcvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) structure was present in HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq) and there is large amount of DL data to be forwarded and incoming SDUs on S1-U/Ng-U tunnel, counters value might increase. Refer 5G\_L2\_12812\_replaced([11223333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_p0NfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rationale.

[End CB008490-DT]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-3.0-18**  (ID: `12480219`)

PM Counters
Number of MDBV-compliant DC-GBR DL PDCP SDUs discarded in gNB-CU-UP for NRPMQAP

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-3.0-18.0-1**  (ID: `12480223`)

PM Counters
Measurement: PDCP Latency PMQAP Profile

NetAct name: DC\_GBR\_DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_DIS\_CU\_PMQP

PI ID: M55159C00010

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

Update time: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Note: Bearer is DC-GBR bearer if HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq/Qos/Mapping/resourceType IE is set to dcGBR. DL PDCP SDU is MDBV compliant if dlMdbv for the discarded packet does not exceed ulRanPdb (DL Maximum Data Burst Volume enforcement control for DC-GBR is enabled - HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq/SecandaryPathParams/FlowControlParams/mdbvEnforce is filled).

This PM counter is not updated when DL PDCP SDU is discarded due to PDCP SDU size 0 bytes or exceeding 9000 bytes (max allowed packet size).

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11236335`)

PM Counters

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11236344`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counter:

M55328C00003 (PDCP\_SDU\_DATA\_VOL\_DL\_SLICE) DL PDCP SDUs transmitted volume per Slice per PLMN

The counter provides the total number of DL PDCP SDU bytes transmitted via gNB for the given Slice and PLMN

Discarded DL PDCP SDUs are not counted.

Retransmitted DL PDCP PDUs are not counted.

[CB008828-A] In case when slices extension feature is enabled, this slice based counter should not be updated. [End CB008828-A]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13473495`)

PM Counters
For each DL PDCP PDU that is sent towards RLC layer, PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI sums up the total data volume of the packets sent for respective SA Bearer-QoS group and updates the appropriate counter:

**M55319C12001 ... 20 (DL\_VOL\_TX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDU volume transmitted for SA Bearer - QoS Group 01 ... 20**

Note:

1. Discarded DL PDCP SDUs are not counted.
2. [CB015891-E] 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report **M55319C12001 ... 20 (DL\_VOL\_TX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) counters in Bytes and BOAM shall convert to kB. [End CB015891-E]**

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-4.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `13479445`)

PM Counters
[Before CB015891-E]

For each DL PDCP SDU that is received over NR NG-U DL GTP-U tunnel, PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI sums up the total data volume of the received packets for a respective SA Bearer-QoS group and updates the appropriate counter:

[CB015891-E]

Measurement: NR NG-U Interface Report

NetAct name: DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_RCV\_NGU\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_RCV\_NGU\_QOS\_GRP\_20

PI ID: M55327C02001 ... M55327C02020

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment these counters M55327C02001 ... M55327C02020 (DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_RCV\_NGU\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_RCV\_NGU\_QOS\_GRP\_20) by total data volume of the received packets for a respective SA Bearer-QoS group in Bytes. [End CB015891-E]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-4.0-11**  (ID: `11236423`)

PM Counters
Maximum PDCP SDUs data volume sent over NG-U data tunnel

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-4.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11236428`)

PM Counters
Every 1 second the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI calculates the volume of data of the packets sent for respective SA Bearer-QoS group. If the value is bigger than for the previous sample, the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI updates the appropriate counter:

M55319C13001 ... 20 (MAX\_DL\_VOL\_TX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Max DL PDCP SDU volume transmitted for SA Bearer in sample time - QoS Group 01 ... 20

Every 1 second the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI calculates the volume of data of the packets sent for respective SA Bearer-QoS group. If the value is smaller than the previous sample, the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI updates the appropriate counter:

M55319C14001 ... 20 (MIN\_DL\_VOL\_TX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Min DL PDCP SDU volume transmitted for SA Bearer in sample time - QoS Group 01 ... 20

The SA Bearer-QoS group value is received in the Bearer Setup (see qciCounterGroup in 5G\_L2\_IF\_1020\_replaced([10987413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WWh6Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-4.0-19**  (ID: `12689667`)

PM Counters
Max DL Cell throughput in PDCP layer

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-4.0-19.0-1**  (ID: `12689668`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell (PDCPC)  
NetAct name: PDCP\_SDU\_CELL\_THP\_DL\_MAX  
PI ID: M55350C00068  
Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD.

Update time:

If NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount has "PDCP SDU Cell level peak throughput PM Counters" selected (i.e.,Bit 2: PDCPSDUPEAKTHPUT is set in HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount), 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall sample every 1 sec the cumulative transmitted DL PDCP SDU volume of all DRBs in NRCELL and report the maximum value from all samples during the measurement period.

Increment value:

5G-L2-HI (CU) shall compute cumulative transmitted DL PDCP SDU volume of all DRBs in NRCELL during sampling interval of 1 sec, compares against cumulated DL PDCP SDU volume computed in previous sampling interval of 1 sec and updates if current value is bigger than previous value.

Additional Information:

1. In case of EN-DC Split bearer, 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall consider cumulative DL PDCP SDU volume transmitted via F1-U Interface and X2 Interface.
2. In case of NR-DC Split bearer, SN 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall consider cumulative DL PDCP SDU volume transmitted via F1-U Interface and XN Interface.
3. In case of online modification of NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount to select or deselect  "PDCP SDU Cell level peak throughput PM Counters" then 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall consider new value of Bit 2: PDCPSDUPEAKTHPUT in HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount immediately from the next sampling interval.

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `11236524`)

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11236531`)

PM Counters
Sum of PDCP delay

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11236541`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counters provided the sum of PDCP delay for the given QoS Group.:

M55319C09001 ... 20 (DL\_DELAY\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDU delay - QoS Group 01 ... 20

[Before CB008225-B-UPD003]

NOTE: The delay for PDCP SDU is calculated as time difference between "the reception of the PDCP SDU from S1 or NG-U" and "DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB".

[End CB008225-B-UPD003]

[CB008225-B-UPD003]

NOTE: The delay for PDCP SDU is calculated as time difference between

"DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB" and "the reception of the PDCP SDU from S1 or NG-U for the bearer marked as Active"

OR

"DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB" and "transition of the bearer from Inactive to Active state for the DL PDCP SDUs received from S1 or NG-U while the bearer was marked as Inactive".

[PR725228]

OR

"DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB" and "transition of the bearer from Inactive to Active state for the DL PDCP SDUs received from S1 or NG-U while the bearer was marked as Active but remained in the buffer when the bearer was transitioned to Inactive state".

[End PR725228]

[End CB008225-B-UPD003]

Note that average delay can be obtained using SDU amount counters:

"M55319C01001: DL PDCP SDUs transmitted for NSA Bearer - QoS Group 01"

+

"M55319C11001: DL PDCP SDUs transmitted for SA Bearer- QoS Group 01

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11236557`)

PM Counters

M55328C00006 (PDCP\_SDU\_DELAY\_DL\_SLICE) DL PDCP SDU delay per Slice per PLMN

[Before CB008225-B-UPD003]

NOTE: The delay for PDCP SDU is calculated as time difference between the reception of the PDCP SDU from NG-U and DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer

[End CB008225-B-UPD003]

[CB008225-B-UPD003]

NOTE: The delay for PDCP SDU is calculated as time difference between

"DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB" and "the reception of the PDCP SDU from S1 or NG-U for the bearer marked as Active"

OR

"DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB" and "transition of the bearer from Inactive to Active state for the DL PDCP SDUs received from S1 or NG-U while the bearer was marked as Inactive".

[PR725228]

OR

"DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB" and "transition of the bearer from Inactive to Active state for the DL PDCP SDUs received from S1 or NG-U while the bearer was marked as Active but remained in the buffer when the bearer was transitioned to Inactive state".

[End PR725228]

[End CB008225-B-UPD003]

Note that average delay can be received using DL PDCP SDU amount counters:

"M55328C00002: DL PDCP SDUs transmitted per Slice per PLMN "

[CB008828-A] In case when slices extension feature is enabled, this slice based counter should not be updated. [End CB008828-A]

QoS Level

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11236574`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counters provided the sum of PDCP delay of SDUs discarded at PDCP level due to SDU queueing delay exceeding the threshold for the given QoS Group.:

M55320C11001 ... 20 (DL\_DELAY\_DISC\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP delay of discarded SDUs - QoS Group 01 ... 20

[Before CB008225-B-UPD003]

NOTE: The delay for PDCP SDU is calculated as time difference between the reception of the PDCP SDU from S1 or NG-U and discarding of the SDU from PDCP buffer.

[End CB008225-B-UPD003]

[CB008225-B-UPD003]

NOTE: The delay for PDCP SDU is calculated as time difference between

"DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB" and "the reception of the PDCP SDU from S1 or NG-U for the bearer marked as Active"

OR

"DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB" and "transition of the bearer from Inactive to Active state for the DL PDCP SDUs received from S1 or NG-U while the bearer was marked as Inactive".

[PR725228]

OR

"DL PDCP PDU is sent towards RLC layer in either gNB or eNB" and "transition of the bearer from Inactive to Active state for the DL PDCP SDUs received from S1 or NG-U while the bearer was marked as Active but remained in the buffer when the bearer was transitioned to Inactive state".

[End PR725228]

[End CB008225-B-UPD003]

The average PDCP delay of discarded SDU can be calculated by dividing with "M55320C09001: DL PDCP SDUs discarded due to the exceeding Queuing delay - QoS Group 01".

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `11236580`)

PM Counters
Average DL PDCP SDU delay in CU-UP

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11236586`)

PM Counters
DL PDCP SDU delay in CU UP

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11236590`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI CU shall update counters:

 M55350C00023 (DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_DLY\_CUUP) DL PDCP SDU delay in CU UP

 M55159C00001 (DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_DLY\_CUUP\_PMQAP) DL PDCP SDU delay in CU UP at Profile level

Notes:

1. PMQAP information can be found under 5G\_L2\_3337\_replaced([11238528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BQ9wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. Counters are reported in microsecond, but average DL PDCP SDU delay in CU-UP (DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_DLY\_CUUP/DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SENT\_TOT) will be reported in miliseconds by OAM.
3. The below delays are taken into consideration for this counter:

 time spent on GTP parsing,

 time spent on the crypto operation,

 potential packet bundling before passing the data to the crypto entity,

 potential packet bundling before sending the data to the RLC entity

---

 M55159C00002 (DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SENT\_TOT\_PMQAP) Number of DL PDCP SDU send to gNB-DU over F1U/XnU at Profile level

Notes:

1. PMQAP information can be found under 5G\_L2\_3337\_replaced([11238528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BQ9wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. Counters DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SENT\_TOT/DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SENT\_TOT\_PMQAP can be used as the denominator of DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_DLY\_CUUP/DL\_PDCP\_SDU\_DLY\_CUUP\_PMQAP (5G\_L2\_13068\_replaced([11236586](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BBGLPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) respectively to calculate the average DL PDCP SDU delay in CU-UP.

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-5.0-1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11236628`)

PM Counters
[Before CB012119-G]

5G-L2-HI CU shall update counters:

 M55350C00025 (DL\_GTP\_PKT\_F1\_DLY) DL GTP Packet delay over F1-U

 M55159C00003 (DL\_GTP\_PKT\_F1\_DLY\_PMQAP) DL GTP Packet delay over F1-U at Profile level

Notes:

1. PMQAP information can be found under 5G\_L2\_3337\_replaced([11238528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BQ9wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. Counters DL\_GTP\_PKT\_F1\_DLY and DL\_GTP\_PKT\_F1\_DLY\_PMQAP should be equal to 0 for gNB classical deployment. This is because in fact F1-U is internal interface and the approximate actual delay is in microseconds and the counter is in miliseconds, so in fact the counter value will show 0.

[CB012119-G]

Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline.Please see 5G\_L2\_17013\_replaced([11236633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BBtNvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_17015\_replaced([11236647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BBtOPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB012119-G]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11236633`)

PM Counters
DL GTP Packet delay over F1-U

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-5.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11236639`)

PM Counters
Measurement: PDCPC

NetAct name: DL\_GTP\_PKT\_F1\_DLY

PI ID: M55350C00025

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: 5G-L2-Hi CU shal collect metrics for time needed for the computation of the counter as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26068\_replaced([11229631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kypGq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The flow shall be the following:

1. GTP packet is sent towards L2Hi DU and T1 is noted by L2Hi CU.
2. The packet is received by L2Hi DU in time T2.
3. L2Hi DU generates DDDS feedback in T3 with the feedback delay time as T3-T2.
4. L2Hi CU receives the feedback in T4.
5. L2Hi calculates F1-U Delay over F1-U as (T4-T1)-(T3-T2) and increments the counter.

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Additional info:

1. Counter is for Cloud only.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-5.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11236647`)

PM Counters
DL GTP Packet delay over F1-U at profile level

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-1.0-6.0-5.0-1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11236650`)

Measurement: PDLTQ

NetAct name: DL\_GTP\_PKT\_F1\_DLY\_PMQAP

PI ID: M55159C00003

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: 5G-L2-Hi CU shal collect metrics for time needed for the computation of the counter as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26068\_replaced([11229631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kypGq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The flow shall be the following:

1. GTP packet is sent towards L2Hi DU and T1 is noted by L2Hi CU.
2. The packet is received by L2Hi DU in time T2.
3. L2Hi DU generates DDDS feedback in T3 with the feedback delay time as T3-T2.
4. L2Hi CU receives the feedback in T4.
5. L2Hi calculates F1-U Delay over F1-U as (T4-T1)-(T3-T2) and increments the counter.

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11236742`)

PM Counters
Data volume sent over DRB data tunnel

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13480764`)

PM Counters
[Before CB015891-E]

5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counters provided the total number of downlink data bytes sent over DL PDU session data forwarding GTP-U tunnel for the given QoS Group.:

**M55337C01001 ... 20 (DL\_FW\_VOL\_SNT\_PDUSES\_QOS\_01 ... 20) DL data volume sent over DL PDU session or DRB data forwarding GTP-U tunnel - For QoS Group 01 ... 20**

NOTE:

* Counter is incremented by payload (PDCP SDU) size of sent GTP-U packet.
* 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall peg these counters when HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

[CB015891-E]

Measurement: NR PDU Session or DRB DL Forwarding

NetAct name: DL\_FW\_VOL\_SNT\_PDUSES\_QOS\_01 ... DL\_FW\_VOL\_SNT\_PDUSES\_QOS\_20

PI ID: M55337C01001 ... M55337C01020

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall update these counters M55337C01001 ... M55337C01020 (DL\_FW\_VOL\_SNT\_PDUSES\_QOS\_01 ... DL\_FW\_VOL\_SNT\_PDUSES\_QOS\_20) when downlink GTP-U user data packet is sent over DL PDU session or DRB data forwarding GTP-U tunnel for the given QoS Group. 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall peg these counters when HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment these counters M55337C01001 ... M55337C01020 (DL\_FW\_VOL\_SNT\_PDUSES\_QOS\_01 ... DL\_FW\_VOL\_SNT\_PDUSES\_QOS\_20) by DL PDCP SDU data volume sent over DL PDU session or DRB data forwarding GTP-U tunnel for given QoS Group in Bytes. BOAM shall convert the reported value to kB.

[End CB015891-E]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11236809`)

PM Counters
[Before CB013554-A] PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI increments

* M55323C00001.. 20 counters with the number of DL PDCP PDUs transmitted at PDCP level according to the QoS Group when the PDUs are sent towards RLC entiy of 5G-L2-HI.
* M55323C01001...20 with the number of kilobytes of DL PDCP PDUs transmitted at PDCP level according to the QoS Group when the PDUs are sent towards RLC entity of 5G-L2-HI.
* M55323C07001...20 (MAX\_DL\_SNT\_F1\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Max downlink data volume sent over F1-U in the sample time- QoS Group 1 ... 20 according to the QoS Group every 1s.
* M55323C08001 ... 20 (MIN\_DL\_SNT\_F1\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Min downlink data volume sent over F1-U in the sample time- QoS Group 1 ... 20 according to the QoS Group every 1s.

NR UP instance of 5G-L2-HI increments:

* M55313C26001 … 20 (DL\_WOPDU\_NUM\_SNT\_X2\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Number of NR-U DUD without PDCP PDU sent over X2-U - QoS Group 1 with the number of NR downlink PDU without PDCP PDU on X2-U interface according to the QoS Group when NR downlink PDU without any PDCP PDU is sent over the X2-U (see Note3).
* M55323C16001…20 (DL\_WOPDU\_NUM\_SNT\_F1\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Number of NR-U DUD without PDCP PDU sent over F1-U - QoS Group 1 ... 20 with the number of NR downlink PDU without PDCP PDU on F1-U interface according to the QoS Group when NR downlink PDU without any PDCP PDU is sent over the F1-U.

Notes:

1.The QoS group value is received in the Bearer Setup.

1. Counters are updated per BTS, refer to 5G\_L2\_2776\_replaced([11233420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Aqg0PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_L2\_2780\_replaced([11235879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A8NpfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. M55313C26001 … 20 counters are related to EN-DC technology only and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user.

[CB013554-A] Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline.Please see 5G\_L2\_19106\_replaced([11236814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BDiafvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19107\_replaced([11236842](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BDibvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19108\_replaced([11236869](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BEJdPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19109\_replaced([11236885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BEJd_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19110\_replaced([11236901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BEJe_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_19111\_replaced([11236928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BEwgPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB013554-A]

Duplications

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `11236961`)

PM Counters
Criteria and approach to legacy counters

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-13.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11236972`)

PM Counters
[Before CB013554-A] 5G-L2-HI increments the following counters every time when the DL PDCP data PDU is sent over X2-U interface due to duplication:

 M55355C04001 … 20 (DL\_NUM\_DUP\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDUs sent over X2-U due to duplication - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see Note2)

 M55355C05001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_DUP\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDU volume sent over X2-U due to duplication - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see Note2) [End CB013554-A]

The Criteria for Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU are defined in requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6806\_replaced([11220499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-HI does not increment the following legacy counters, when the DL PDCP data PDU is sent over X2-U interface due to duplication:

 M55319C01001 … 20 (DL\_SDU\_TX\_NSA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDUs transmitted for NSA Bearer- QoS Group 01 ...  20

 M55319C02001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_TX\_NSA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDU volume transmitted for NSA Bearer - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55326C02001 … 20 (PDCP\_VOL\_DL\_PLMN\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) PDCP SDU user DL data volume per PLMN-ID - QoS Group 01 ...  20

 M55326C01001 (PDCP\_SDU\_USDAT\_NUM\_DL\_PLMN) DL PDCP user data SDUs transmitted per PLMN-ID

 M55326C00001 (PDCP\_SDU\_USDAT\_VOL\_DL\_NSA\_PLMN) PDCP SDU user DL data volume per PLMN-ID for NSA user

The Criteria for Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU are defined in requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6806\_replaced([11220499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in 5G UP Algorithms module (please note the 22R2 release version of the requirement.)

Note:

1. The detailed information related to legacy counters can be found under /5G System/CFAM/5GC/01200-01399/CFAM 5GC001354, section 1.3.10 Impact on Counters, Performance Monitoring and Tracing.

[Before CB013554-A] 2. M55355C04001 … 20 and M55355C05001 … 20 counters are related to EN-DC technology only and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user. [End CB013554-A]

[CB013554-A] Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline. Please see 5G\_L2\_19293\_replaced([11236977](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BEwifvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_19294\_replaced([11237006](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BEwjvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB013554-A]

DL\_VOL\_DUP\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_20) every time when the DL PDCP data PDU is sent over X2-U interface due to duplication. These counters are pegged only when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf = QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is set to QoS. DL\_VOL\_DUP\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_20) counters in Bytes by DL PDCP data PDU volume sent over X2-U interface due to duplication. 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report M55355C05001 ... M55355C05020 (DL\_VOL\_DUP\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... DL\_VOL\_DUP\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_20) counters in Bytes and BOAM shall convert to kB.

[End CB015891-E]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11237116`)

PM Counters
Discarding

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11237122`)

PM Counters
PDCP PDUs discarded over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13355959`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counters provided the total number of received but discarded downlink GTP-U user data packets over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel for the given QoS Group.:

**M55337C03001 ... 20 (DL\_FW\_SDU\_DSC\_PDUSES\_QoS\_01 ... 20) Number of downlink user data packets discarded over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel - QoS Group 01 ... 20**

GTP-U management messages are not included.

Discard causes :

* Every packet after reception of GTP-U End Marker.
* Every packet after wait timer for GTP-U End Marker expired.
* GTP-U packet with zero payload length.
* GTP-U packet with unsupported extension header for which comprehension is required.

[CB015333-B]

Note:

* 5G-L2-HI (DU) shall peg these counters when HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

[End CB015333-B]

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13356029`)

PM Counters
**Number of DL user data packets discarded over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel per PMQAP profile**

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13356031`)

PM Counters
Measurement: PDCP Cell NRPMQAP2 (PDCPQ2)

NetAct name: NUM\_DL\_FWD\_DISC\_PMQAP

PI ID: M55403C00014

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall peg this counter when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to PMQAP ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment this counter by 1 when a downlink GTP-U user data packet is received over:

* X2-U DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel is discarded by GTP-U layer
* DL PDU session or DRB data forwarding GTP-U tunnel is discarded by GTP-U layer

This counter is the PMQAP version of the legacy QoS Counters NUM\_DL\_FWD\_DATA\_DSC\_QoS\_GRP\_01...NUM\_DL\_FWD\_DATA\_DSC\_QoS\_GRP\_20 defined in [11237122: PDCP PDUs discarded over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BF-pvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and DL\_FW\_SDU\_DSC\_PDUSES\_QoS\_01...DL\_FW\_SDU\_DSC\_PDUSES\_QoS\_20 defined in [11238012: GTP-U discarded over X2-U DL data forwarding tunnel](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BNTZPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11237132`)

PM Counters
PDCP PDUs discarded due to PDCP Reset per NRPMQAP Profile

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11237138`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counter:

M55352C00002 (DL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DISC\_RESET\_PMQAP) DL PDCP PDUs discarded due to PDCP Reset per NRPMQAP Profile

This counter is updated when DL PDCP PDU is discarded due to "pdcpReset" = TRUE per NRPMQAP Profile.

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11237141`)

PM Counters
PDCP PDUs volume discarded over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `13481220`)

PM Counters
[Before CB015891-E]

5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counters provided the total number of received but discarded downlink GTP-U data bytes over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel for the given QoS Group.:

**M55337C02001 ... 20 (DL\_FW\_VOL\_DSC\_PDUSES\_QoS\_01 ... 20) Downlink data volume discarded over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel - QoS Group 01 ... 20**

GTP-U management messages are not included.

Discard causes :

* Every packet after reception of GTP-U End Marker.
* Every packet after wait timer for GTP-U End Marker expired.
* GTP-U packet with zero payload length.
* GTP-U packet with unsupported extension header for which comprehension is required.

Note:

* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall peg these counters when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

[CB015891-E]

Measurement: NR PDU Session or DRB DL Forwarding

NetAct name: DL\_FW\_VOL\_DSC\_PDUSES\_QoS\_01 ... DL\_FW\_VOL\_DSC\_PDUSES\_QoS\_20

PI ID: M55337C02001 ... M55337C02020

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall update this counter when a downlink GTP-U user data packet received over a DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel is discarded by the GTP-U layer for a given QoS Group.  
The specific discard causes include:

* Every packet after reception of GTP-U End Marker.
* Every packet after wait timer for GTP-U End Marker expired.
* GTP-U packet with zero payload length.
* GTP-U packet with unsupported extension header for which comprehension is required.

These counters are pegged when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to QoS. GTP-U management messages are not included in this measurement.

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment these counters by the size of the discarded downlink GTP-U data in Bytes, corresponding to the PDCP SDU size of the GTP-U packet. BOAM shall convert to kB.

[End CB015891-E]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13356158`)

PM Counters

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall peg this counter shall be pegged when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to PMQAP ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

* X2-U DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel is discarded by GTP-U layer
* DL PDU session or DRB data forwarding GTP-U tunnel is discarded by GTP-U layer

This counter is the PMQAP version of the legacy QoS Counters VOL\_DL\_FWD\_DATA\_DSC\_QoS\_GRP\_01...VOL\_DL\_FWD\_DATA\_DSC\_QoS\_GRP\_20 defined in [11237992: Data volume discarded over X2-U DL data forwarding tunnel](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BMsX_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and DL\_FW\_VOL\_DSC\_PDUSES\_QoS\_01...DL\_FW\_VOL\_DSC\_PDUSES\_QoS\_20 defined in [11237141: PDCP PDUs volume discarded over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BF-qvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11237185`)

PM Counters
[Before CB013554-A]

L2-Hi CU increments the following counters:

1) every time the DL PDCP data PDU is retransmitted over F1-U/X2-U due to exceeding Threshold 1 (derived from NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpPduRetxDelayThresh1 received in HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq) for QoS Group 1 ... 20:

 M55354C04001 … 20 (DL\_NUM\_RETX\_THR1\_F1\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDUs retransmitted over F1-U due to exceeding Threshold 1 - QoS Group 01... 20

 M55354C05001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR1\_F1\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDU volume retransmitted over F1-U due to exceeding Threshold 1 - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55355C06001 … 20 (DL\_NUM\_RETX\_THR1\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDUs retransmitted over X2-U due to exceeding Threshold 1 - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see note2)

 M55355C07001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR1\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDU volume retransmitted over X2-U due to exceeding Threshold 1 - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see note2)

2) every time the DL PDCP data PDU is retransmitted over F1-U/X2-U due to exceeding Threshold 2 (derived from NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpPduRetxDelayThresh2 received in HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq) for QoS Group 1 ... 20:

 M55354C06001 … 20 (DL\_NUM\_RETX\_THR2\_F1\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDUs retransmitted over F1-U due to exceeding Threshold 2 - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55354C07001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR2\_F1\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDU volume retransmitted over F1-U due to exceeding Threshold 2 - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55355C08001 … 20 (DL\_NUM\_RETX\_THR2\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDUs retransmitted over X2-U due to exceeding Threshold 2 - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see note2)

 M55355C09001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR2\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) (DL PDCP data PDU volume retransmitted over X2-U due to exceeding Threshold 2 - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see note2)

3) when the PDCP PDU retransmitted due to exceeding Threshold 1 is indicated as successfully retransmitted in DDDS:

 M55320C21001 … 09 (PDCP\_PDU\_RETX\_DLY\_THR1\_BIN\_01 ... 09) Transmission delay of the DL PDCP PDU retransmitted due to exceeding Threshold 1 – Bin 01 … 09

4) when the PDCP PDU retransmitted due to exceeding Threshold 2 is released at PDCP:

 M55320C22001 … 09 (PDCP\_PDU\_RETX\_DLY\_THR2\_BIN\_01 ... 09) Delivery delay of the DL PDCP PDU retransmitted due to exceeding Threshold 2 - Bin 01 … 09

5) every time the DL PDCP data PDU marked for retransmission is not retransmitted due to exceeding maximum delay (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5599\_replaced([11219850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (derived from NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpRetxPduSendMaxDelay received in HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq ) allowed for retransmission of PDCP PDU for QoS Group 01 ... 20:

 M55320C23001 … 20 (PDCP\_PDU\_NOT\_RETX\_MAX\_DLY\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP PDUs not retransmitted after exceeding maximum delay allowed for retransmission - QoS Group 01 ... 20

Note:

1. [End CB013554-A]

For definition of PDCP retransmitted PDU in CU refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The Criteria for Delay Threshold based PDCP PDU Retransmission are defined in requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before CB013554-A]

2. M55355C06001 … 20
3. M55355C07001 … 20
4. M55355C08001 … 20

[End CB013554-A]

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall update M55355C07001 ... M55355C07020 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR1\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR1\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_20) every time the DL PDCP data PDU is retransmitted over F1-U/X2-U due to exceeding Threshold 1 (HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq.DataProcessing.SplitBearerParams.PdcpPduRetx.pdcpPduRetxDelayThresh1 -*[10987630: PdcpPduRetx](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WXwD_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). These counters are pegged only when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf = QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is set to QoS. M55355C07020 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR1\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR1\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_20) counters in Bytes and BOAM shall convert to kB.

DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR2\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_20) every time the DL PDCP data PDU is retransmitted over F1-U/X2-U due to exceeding Threshold 2 (HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq.DataProcessing.SplitBearerParams.PdcpPduRetx.pdcpPduRetxDelayThresh2 -*[10987630: PdcpPduRetx](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WXwD_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). These counters are pegged only when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf = QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is set to QoS. M55355C09020 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR2\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... DL\_VOL\_RETX\_THR2\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_20) counters in Bytes and BOAM shall convert to kB.

PM Counters
For each re-transmitted PDCP PDU [5G\_L1\_5G21A\_890], the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI shall update the following counters according to the QoS group of the bearer

M55320C13001 ... 20 (VOL\_RETRANS\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) - Volume of PDCP PDU retransmitted - QoS Group 1... 20

Please see 5G\_L2\_21397\_replaced([11237448](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BIa6PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_21400\_replaced([11237456](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BIa6vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). which are defined in [11237448: Number of PDCP PDU retransmitted per QoS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BIa6PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). When this PMQAP counter is updated, 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall not update the corresponding legacy QoS counter NUM\_RETRANS\_QoS\_GRP\_01...20 (M55320C12001...M55320C12020).

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall update this counter when a DL PDCP data PDU is retransmitted, and when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to PMQAP ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). The criteria for what constitutes a re-transmitted PDCP PDU in the CU are defined in [11220366: PDCP Retransmission PDU](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment this counter with the size of the retransmitted DL PDCP data PDU for each matching PMQAP profile. This counter is the PMQAP version of the legacy QoS Counters VOL\_RETRANS\_QoS\_GRP\_01...VOL\_RETRANS\_QoS\_GRP\_20 (M55320C13001...M55320C13020), defined in [11237456: Volume of PDCP PDU retransmitted per QoS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BIa6vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). When this PMQAP counter is updated, 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall not update the corresponding legacy QoS counter VOL\_RETRANS\_QoS\_GRP\_01...VOL\_RETRANS\_QoS\_GRP\_20 (M55320C13001...M55320C13020).

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11237474`)

PM Counters
Criteria and approach to legacy counters

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-7.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11237489`)

PM Counters
[Before CB013554-A]

L2-Hi CU increments the following counters

1) every time the DL PDCP data PDU of the source F1-U is re-sent over target F1-U/X2-U due to gNB handover:

 M55354C00001 … 20 (DL\_NUM\_RETX\_HO\_F1\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDUs retransmitted over F1-U during gNB handover - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55354C01001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_HO\_F1\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDU volume retransmitted during gNB handover over F1-U - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55355C00001 … 20 (DL\_NUM\_RETX\_HO\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDUs retransmitted over X2-U during gNB handover - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see note3)

 M55355C01001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_HO\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDU volume retransmitted over X2-U during gNB handover - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see note3)

2) every time the DL PDCP data PDU is retransmitted over F1-U/X2-U due to lost packet report:

 M55354C02001 … 20 (DL\_NUM\_RETX\_LRPT\_F1\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDUs retransmitted over F1-U due to lost packet report - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55354C03001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_LRPT\_F1\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDU volume retransmitted over F1-U due to lost packet report - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55355C02001 … 20 (DL\_NUM\_RETX\_LRPT\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDUs retransmitted over X2-U due to lost packet report - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see note2)

 M55355C03001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_RETX\_LRPT\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP data PDU volume retransmitted over X2-U due to lost packet report - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see Note2)

[End CB013554-A]

In case of retransmitted DL PDCP PDUs, L2-Hi CU does not increment the following legacy counters (/5G System/CFAM/5GC/01200-01399/CFAM 5GC001354, section 1.3.10 Impact on Counters, Performance Monitoring and Tracing.):

 M55319C01001 … 20 (DL\_SDU\_TX\_NSA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDUs transmitted for NSA Bearer- QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55319C02001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_TX\_NSA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDU volume transmitted for NSA Bearer - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55319C11001 … 20 (DL\_SDU\_TX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDUs transmitted for SA Bearer- QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55319C12001 … 20 (DL\_VOL\_TX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDU volume transmitted for SA Bearer - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55326C00501 (PDCP\_SDU\_USDAT\_VOL\_DL\_SA\_PLMN) PDCP SDU user DL data volume per PLMN-ID for SA user

 M55326C01001 (PDCP\_SDU\_USDAT\_NUM\_DL\_PLMN) DL PDCP user data SDUs transmitted per PLMN-ID)

 M55326C02001 … 20 (PDCP\_VOL\_DL\_PLMN\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) PDCP SDU user DL data volume per PLMN-ID - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55328C00002 (PDCP\_SDU\_DATA\_NUM\_DL\_SLICE) DL PDCP SDUs transmitted per Slice per PLMN

 M55328C00003 (PDCP\_SDU\_DATA\_VOL\_DL\_SLICE) DL PDCP SDUs transmitted volume per Slice per PLMN

Note:

1.For definition of PDCP retransmitted PDU in CU or in DU refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before CB013554-A]

2.  Below counters are related to EN-DC technology only and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user:

* M55355C06001 … 20
* M55355C07001 … 20
* M55355C08001 … 20
* M55355C09001 … 20
* M55355C02001 … 20
* M55355C03001 … 20
* M55355C00001 … 20 and M55355C01001 … 20 counters are related to EN-DC technology only and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user. [End CB013554-A]

[CB013554-A] Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline. Please see 5G\_L2\_19388\_replaced([11237495](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BJB8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19389\_replaced([11237519](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BJB9vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19390\_replaced([11237544](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BJpAfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19391\_replaced([11237572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BJpB_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19392\_replaced([11237598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BKQEPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19393\_replaced([11237625](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BKQFfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19394\_replaced([11237652](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BKQGvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_19395\_replaced([11237678](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BK3JPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB013554-A]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11237793`)

PM Counters
Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-2.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `11237813`)

PM Counters
[Before CB013554-A] 5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment:

* M55323C11001...9 (EST\_F1\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_BIN\_01) Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over F1-U - Bin 01...09

after receiving F1-U DDDS in the below way (see: Note1):

- If any DL packets were sent on F1-U since the previous DDDS then L2-HI shall report the last calculated value of PDU\_delay.

- If no DL packets were sent on F1-U since the previous DDDS then L2-HI shall report “max (avgLatencyF1, dataOnFlightUE/tputForPduDelay)”.

* M55323C11001 if "delivery estimation" <= 1ms,
* M55323C11002 if 1ms < "delivery estimation" <= 2ms,
* M55323C11003 if 2ms < "delivery estimation" <= 3ms,
* M55323C11004 if 3ms < "delivery estimation" <= 5ms,
* M55323C11005 if 5ms < "delivery estimation" <= 10ms,
* M55323C11006 if 10ms < "delivery estimation" <= 15ms,
* M55323C11007 if 15ms < "delivery estimation" <= 20ms,
* M55323C11008 if 20ms < "delivery estimation" <= 50ms,
* M55323C11009 if 50ms < "delivery estimation".
* M55323C12001...12 (EST\_F1\_TPUT\_BIN\_01...12) Distribution of Estimated throughput over F1-U - Bin 01...12 (estTput)

according to its value right  after receiving F1-U DDDS (see: Note1).

* M55323C12001 if estTput <= 1Mbps,
* M55323C12002 if 1Mbps < estTput <= 10Mbps,
* M55323C12003 if 10Mbps < estTput <= 20Mbps,
* M55323C12004 if 20Mbps < estTput <= 50Mbps,
* M55323C12005 if 50Mbps < estTput <= 100Mbps,
* M55323C12006 if 100Mbps < estTput <= 500Mbps,
* M55323C12007 if 500Mbps < estTput <= 1Gbps,
* M55323C12008 if 1Gbps < estTput <= 2Gbps,
* M55323C12009 if 2Gbps < estTput <= 3Gbps,
* M55323C12010 if 3Gbps < estTput <= 4Gbps,
* M55323C12011 if 4Gbps < estTput <= 5Gbps,
* M55323C12012 if 5Gbps < estTput.
* M55313C07001...20 (NUM\_OPPT\_DL\_DAT\_SPT\_QOS\_GRP\_01...20) Number of opportunities for the DL Data split over NR F1-U and NR X2-U - QoS Group 01...20

when DL traffic split is allowed (dlDataSplitAllowed = True) as a result of data split gain calculation (see: Note2).

* one of the following counters M55313C05001...09 (EST\_INTF\_LATENCY\_X2\_BIN\_01...09) Distribution of Estimated NR X2-U Latency - Bin 01...09

when Estimated X2-U Latency (x2Latency) is updated after receiving X2-U DDDS (see: Note3):

* M55313C05001 if x2Latency <=1ms,
* M55313C05002 if 1ms < x2Latency <=2ms,
* M55313C05003 if 2ms < x2Latency <=3ms,
* M55313C05004 if 3ms < x2Latency <=5ms,
* M55313C05005 if 5ms < x2Latency <=10ms,
* M55313C05006 if 10ms < x2Latency <=15ms,
* M55313C05007 if 15ms < x2Latency <=20ms,
* M55313C05008 if 20ms < x2Latency <=50ms,
* M55313C05009 if 50ms < x2Latency.

-  one of the following counters M55313C06001...09 (EST\_RLC\_QUEUE\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_01...09) Distribution of Estimated RLC PDU queuing Time over NR X2-U - Bin 01...09

when Estimated RLC PDU Queueing Time (rlcQueueDelayX2) is updated after receiving X2-U DDDS (see: Note3):

M55313C06001 if rlcQueueDelayX2 <=1ms,

M55313C06002 if 1ms < rlcQueueDelayX2 <=2ms,

M55313C06003 if 2ms < rlcQueueDelayX2 <=3ms,

M55313C06004 if 3ms < rlcQueueDelayX2 <=5ms,

M55313C06005 if 5ms < rlcQueueDelayX2 <=10ms,

M55313C06006 if 10ms < rlcQueueDelayX2 <=15ms,

M55313C06007 if 15ms < rlcQueueDelayX2 <=20ms,

M55313C06008 if 20ms < rlcQueueDelayX2 <=50ms,

M55313C06009 if 50ms < rlcQueueDelayX2.

-  M55323C05001...9 (EST\_F1\_INTF\_LATENCY\_BIN\_00...08) Distribution of Estimated F1-U Latency - Bin 00...09

for Estimated NR F1-U Latency (f1Latency) according to its value after receiving F1-U DDDS f1Latency (see: Note3):

* M55323C05001 if f1Latency <=1ms,
* M55323C05002 if 1ms < f1Latency <=2ms,
* M55323C05003 if 2ms < f1Latency <=3ms,
* M55323C05004 if 3ms < f1Latency <=5ms,
* M55323C05005 if 5ms < f1Latency <=10ms,
* M55323C05006 if 10ms < f1Latency <=15ms,
* M55323C05007 if 15ms < f1Latency <=20ms,
* M55323C05008 if 20ms < f1Latency <=50ms,
* M55323C05009 if 50ms < f1Latency.
* M55323C06001...9 (EST\_F1\_RLC\_QUE\_LATENCY\_BIN\_01...09) Distribution of Estimated RLC PDU Queueing Time over F1-U - Bin 01...09

for Estimated RLC PDU Queueing Time (rlcQueueDelay) according to its value after receiving F1-U DDDS rlcQueueDelay (see:Note3):

* M55323C06001 if rlcQueueDelay <=1ms,
* M55323C06002 if 1ms < rlcQueueDelay <=2ms,
* M55323C06003 if 2ms < rlcQueueDelay <=3ms,
* M55323C06004 if 3ms < rlcQueueDelay <=5ms,
* M55323C06005 if 5ms < rlcQueueDelay <=10ms,
* M55323C06006 if 10ms < rlcQueueDelay <=15ms,
* M55323C06007 if 15ms < rlcQueueDelay <=20ms,
* M55323C06008 if 20ms < rlcQueueDelay <=50ms,
* M55323C06009 if 50ms < rlcQueueDelay.

Notes:

1. M55323C11001...09 and M55323C12001...09 counters are deleted for Nokia Flow Control only. There are still working for 3GPP Flow Control.
2. M55313C07001...20 counters are related to EN-DC technology only, and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user.
3. M55313C05001...09 and M55323C05001...09 and M55323C06001...09 and M55313C06001...09 counters are deleted for Nokia Flow Control only.

[CB013554-A] Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline. Please see 5G\_L2\_19366\_replaced([11237819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BLeP_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19367\_replaced([11237830](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BMFQfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19368\_replaced([11237840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BMFQ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19369\_replaced([11237888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BMFV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19370\_replaced([11237903](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BMFZPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19371\_replaced([11237922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BMsUvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_19372\_replaced([11237937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BMsVfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB013554-A]

PM Counters
Measurement: NR F1-U Interface Report BTS (NF1UB)

NetAct name: EST\_F1\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_BIN\_01 ... EST\_F1\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_BIN\_09

PI ID: M55323C11001 ... M55323C11009

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: After receiving F1-U DDDS in the below way:

- If any DL packets were sent on F1-U since the previous DDDS then L2-HI shall report the last calculated value of PDU\_delay.

- If no DL packets were sent on F1-U since the previous DDDS then L2-HI shall report “max (avgLatencyF1, dataOnFlightUE/tputForPduDelay)”.

* M55323C11001 if "delivery estimation" <= 1ms,
* M55323C11002 if 1ms < "delivery estimation" <= 2ms,
* M55323C11003 if 2ms < "delivery estimation" <= 3ms,
* M55323C11004 if 3ms < "delivery estimation" <= 5ms,
* M55323C11005 if 5ms < "delivery estimation" <= 10ms,
* M55323C11006 if 10ms < "delivery estimation" <= 15ms,
* M55323C11007 if 15ms < "delivery estimation" <= 20ms,
* M55323C11008 if 20ms < "delivery estimation" <= 50ms,
* M55323C11009 if 50ms < "delivery estimation".

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11237986`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counter provided the total number of received but discarded downlink GTP-U user data bytes over S1-U DL GTP-U tunnel:

M55315C06001 (DL\_DATA\_VOL\_DISCARD\_S1U) Downlink data volume discarded over S1-U DL GTP-U tunnel

NOTE: GTP-U management messages are not included.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13472346`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counters provided total number of received but discarded downlink GTP-U data bytes over X2-U DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel for the given QoS Group.:

**M55313C03001****... 20 (VOL\_DL\_FWD\_DATA\_DSC\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Downlink data volume discarded over X2-U DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel - QoS Group 01 ... 20**\*\*\*\*

NOTE:

* GTP-U management messages are not included.
* 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall peg these counters when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf is set to QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
* [CB015891-E] 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report **M55313C03001****... 20 (VOL\_DL\_FWD\_DATA\_DSC\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) counters in Bytes and BOAM shall convert to kB. [End CB015891-E]**\*\*\*\*

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13355506`)

Received but discarded downlink user data packets are also included. GTP-U management messages are not included.

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11238034`)

PM Counters
Number of data bytes received over DL data forwarding tunnel

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-3.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `13481551`)

PM Counters
[Before CB015891-E]

5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counters provided the total number of downlink data bytes received over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel for the given QoS Group.:

***\*M55337C04001 ... 20 (VOL\_DL\_FWDT\_RCV\_PDUSES\_QOS\_01 ... 20) DL data volume received over DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel - QoS Group 01 ... 20***\*

Received but discarded downlink user data packets are also included. GTP-U management messages are not included. Counter is incremented by payload (PDCP SDU) size of GTP-U packet.

NOTE:

* Received but discarded downlink user data packets are also included. GTP-U management messages are not included. Counter is incremented by payload (PDCP SDU) size of GTP-U packet.
* These counters are pegged only when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf = QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB015891-E]

Measurement: NR PDU Session or DRB DL Forwarding

NetAct name: VOL\_DL\_FWD\_RCV\_PDUSES\_QOS\_01 ... VOL\_DL\_FWD\_RCV\_PDUSES\_QOS\_20

PI ID: M55337C04001 ... M55337C04020

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall update M55337C04001 ... M55337C04020 (VOL\_DL\_FWD\_RCV\_PDUSES\_QOS\_01 ... VOL\_DL\_FWD\_RCV\_PDUSES\_QOS\_20) counters upon receiving a downlink GTP-U user data packet over the DL data forwarding GTP-U tunnel for the corresponding QoS Group. These counters are pegged only when HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf = QoS ([10987189: PmCountersInfo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is set to QoS.

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment M55337C04001 ... M55337C04020 (VOL\_DL\_FWD\_RCV\_PDUSES\_QOS\_01 ... VOL\_DL\_FWD\_RCV\_PDUSES\_QOS\_20) counters by the payload size (PDCP SDU) of the received GTP-U packet, measured in bytes. BOAM shall convert to kB. GTP-U management messages are not included in this measurement. Received but discarded downlink user data packets are included in this measurement.

[End CB015891-E]
