**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11238100`)

PM Counters
DL PDCP SDU and PDU throughput mechanism

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11238113`)

PM Counters
Burst Identification

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11238117`)

PM Counters
Burst start and end for SDU throughput calculation

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11238141`)

PM Counters
Beginning of a burst shall be [Before CNI-112795]identified as a receiving of PDCP SDU for an active bearer or the transition of bearer from inactive to active state.[CNI-112795] observed, when there is no ongoing burst and one of the below conditions are met:

* receiving the first PDCP SDU for an active bearer from core network
* transition of a bearer from inactive to active state with unsent PDCP SDU(s)(Refer Note 6)
* receiving the PDCP SDU with or without PDCP SN over the forwarding tunnel in inter-gNB HO
* receiving the HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with the cell change and PDCP PDU(s) to be retransmitted to 5G-L2-HI DU in intra-gNB HO.

[End CNI-112795]

Start timestamp tStart to start counting the thpTimeDl of the burst is defined as expiration of Retention Delay Timer.

5G-L2-HI CU shall estimate PDCP PDU transmission time(Guard Timer) during sending the packet towards DU.

5G-L2-HI CU shall set the timestamp end of Burst equal to the timestamp of [CNI-112795] one of the below:

* expiration of the latest Guard Timer, when [Before PR794319]there is no more PDCP SDUs to be sent(normal sending scenario) [PR794319] the PDCP buffer is empty meaning all the PDCP PDUs are delivered and no more PDCP SDUs to be sent.[End PR794319]
* expiration of the latest Guard Timer, when there is no more PDCP PDUs to be retransmitted due to intra-gNB HO(Refer Note 2, Note 3)(burst ending on target cell post intra-gNB HO) [PR794319] and all the PDCP PDUs sent are already indicated as delivered via DDDS[End PR794319]
* the reception of HiUserCu\_BearerDeleteReq
* the reception of HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause = setInactive, irrespective of number of unsent SDUs or whether GT is running or not(Refer Note 5).
* the reception of HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause = suspend with an ongoing burst due to unsent PDCP SDUs or to be retransmitted PDCP PDUs for intra-gNB HO [End CNI-112795][Before CNI-112795](even if it was calculated not for the last sent packet).[End CNI-112795] See also the diagram 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_574\_replaced([11198073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bf-fwvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note 1: Retention Delay is a special case of Guard Timer calculated on first PDU sending. Defines the time of the first packet lagging in the buffer and is excluded from Burst report due to compensation of the time that is needed to calculate the actual time for the packet to exit from gNB/eNB to UE.

[CNI-112795]

Note 2: Lets say we have 10 unacked PDCP PDUs(PDCP PDU1- PDCP PDU10) sent towards source cell when intra-gNB HO happens. When suspend is received on the source, burst on the source cell shall be ended. PDCP shall retransmit all these 10 PDCP PDUs towards the target cell if dataDuplication=TRUE and consider them in the new burst on target cell. If dataDuplication=FALSE, then retransmission starts from the packets which are not indicated as Transmitted in the source cell. If the GT expires after retransmitting PDCP PDU7 towards target cell, then we should not end the burst(if there are no new PDCP SDUs are received) as we have 3 more PDCP PDUs(PDU8 - PDU10) to be retransmitted. Only after retransmitting these 3 PDCP PDUs if there is no more PDCP SDU to be send [PR794319] and all the PDCP PDUs are indicated as delivered via DDDS [End PR794319], the end of burst can be considered upon the later GT expiry.

Note 3: Retransmission due to inactive to active transition(refer Note 6) and Retransmission due to intra-gNB HO only are considered in the burst calculation. All other below retransmission/duplication are not considered in burst(refer Note 7):

- duplication due to TA timer expiry

- retransmission due to threshold timer expiry

- retransmission due to lost packet report.

Also note that, in inter-gNB HO, packets are forwarded from source gNB to target gNB with or without SN assigned. When target gNB re-sends these unacked PDCP PDUs(received as PDCP SDUs with SN assigned)to UE, they are considered as re-sent PDUs and hence considered in the burst.

Note 4: Retransmitted unacked PDCP PDUs after the intra-cell HO shall not be counted in the burst as there is no change in the cell and these PDCP PDUs were already counted before HO.

Note 5: When HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause = setInactive is received, burst shall be ended immediately. GT if running shall be stopped immediately. No need to wait for GT expiry, as bearer at DU is deleted as part of RRC INACTIVE procedure and no possibility of receiving any additional DDDS.

Note 6: When a bearer is transitioned to Inactive state, all the unacked PDUs are stored as SDUs. Hence the same bearer transitions back to Active state, 5G-L2-HI can not make out whether these SDUs are already sent out to DU or not. Hence it is acceptable to count the SDUs twice(Once in the burst before active to inactive state transition and one more time in the new burst after inactive to active state transition of the same bearer)  in this scenario.

Note 7: Retransmission volume or time for the packet due to TA expiry or threshold expiry or lost packet report shall not counted as the volume and time of the original transmission is not deducted/reduced from the calculation. Hence, for a given PDU, single accounting logic should be considered.

[End CNI-112795]

Example 1 - Normal sending of the packets:

1) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives first PDCP SDU1 for an active bearer in the point of time tRec. Due to there is no other PDCP SDUs in the buffer nor Guard Timer is running, tRec is evaluated as start of observing a new burst.

OR

The bearer transits from inactive state to active state at tRec and the same is evaluated as start of observing a new burst.

2) PDCP PDU1 is sent to 5G-L2-Hi DU via F1 in the point of time t1 and Guard Timer for PDCP PDU1 is started and given as per formula:

(PDCP PDU1 Volume/avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]1[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]1[End CNI-112795] (where: avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]1[End CNI-112795] is average estimated throughput for the given PDU1, avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]1[End CNI-112795] is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU1 in the point of time t1). At mentioned t1, also is started the Retention Delay Timer (special case of GT for the first packet) and calculated as avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]1[End CNI-112795] time. Regarding the GT calculation, please refer to 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU2 in the point of time t1 OR PDCP SDU2 was received when the bearer was in inactive state. [Before CNI-112795]Due to gNB buffer is not empty [CNI-112795] As there is unsent PDCP SDU2 present [End CNI-112795]and GT is running, this PDCP SDU2 contributes to the same burst as PDCP SDU1.

4) PDCP PDU2 is sent to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t2 and GT for PDCP PDU2 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU2 Volume/avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]2[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]2[End CNI-112795] (where: avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]2[End CNI-112795] is average estimated throughput for the given PDU2, avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]2[End CNI-112795] is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU2 in the point of time t2). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU2 is longer, 5G-L2-HI CU chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

5) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU3 in the point of time t2 OR PDCP SDU3 was received when the bearer was in inactive state. [Before CNI-112795]Due to gNB buffer is not empty [CNI-112795] As there is unsent PDCP SDU3 present[End CNI-112795] and GT is running, this PDCP SDU3 contributes to the same burst as PDCP SDU1 and PDCP SDU2.

6) Retention Delay expired in the point of time tSent. tSent is considered as a starting point in time to start counting the ThpTimeDl for the given burst. [PR794319] DDDS is received from RLC indicating the successful delivery of PDCP PDU1 and PDU2.[End PR794319]

7) PDCP PDU3 is sent to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t3 and GT for PDCP PDU3 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU3 Volume/avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]3[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]3[End CNI-112795] (where: avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]3[End CNI-112795] is average estimated throughput for the given PDU3, avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]3[End CNI-112795] is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU3 in the point of time t3). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU3 is longer, 5G-L2-HI CU chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

8) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU4 in the point of time t4 OR PDCP SDU4 was received when the bearer was in inactive state. [Before CNI-112795]Due to gNB buffer is not empty [CNI-112795] As there is unsent PDCP SDU4 present [End CNI-112795] and GT is running, this PDCP SDU4 contributes to the same burst as PDCP SDU1, PDCP SDU2 and PDCP SDU3.

9) Due to GT is still running, 5G-L2-HI CU continues counting of thpTimeDl, even PDCP SDU4 is waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-HI DU and GT for PDCP PDU 4 was not recalculated yet. [PR794319] DDDS is received from RLC indicating the successful delivery of PDCP PDUs upto PDU4. [End PR794319]

10) PDCP PDU4 is sent to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t5 and GT for PDCP PDU4 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU4 Volume/avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]4[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]4[End CNI-112795] (where: avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]4[End CNI-112795] is average estimated throughput for the given PDU4, avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]4[End CNI-112795] is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU4 in the point of time t5). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU4 is longer, 5G-L2-HI CU chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

11) 5G-L2-HI CU receives PDCP SDU5 in the point of time t6 OR PDCP SDU5 was received when the bearer was in inactive state. [Before CNI-112795]Due to gNB buffer is not empty[CNI-112795] As there is unsent PDCP SDU5 present [End CNI-112795] and GT is running, this PDCP SDU5 contributes to the same burst as PDCP SDU1, PDCP SDU2, PDCP SDU3 and PDCP SDU4.

12) Due to GT calculated for PDCP PDU 4 is still running, 5G-L2-HI CU continues counting of thpTimeDl, even PDCP SDU5 is waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-HI DU and GT was not recalculated yet.

13) PDCP PDU5 is sent to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t7 and GT for PDCP PDU5 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU5 Volume/avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]5[End CNI-112795]) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU[Before CNI-112795]5[End CNI-112795] (where: avgEstTputPDU[Before CNI-112795]5[End CNI-112795] is average estimated throughput for the given PDU5, avgPduDelvDelay is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU5 in the point of time t7). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU5 is longer, 5G-L2Hi choose it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

14) GT expired [PR794319] and also DDDS is received from RLC indicating the successful delivery of PDCP PDUs upto PDU5 [End PR794319] in the point of time tEndofBurst. Due to [Before PR794319]there is no PDCP SDU waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-HI DU [PR794319] the PDCP buffer is empty[End PR794319], 5G-L2-HI CU shall stop counting thpTimeDl in the point of time tEndOfBurst that represents end of burst in time. In the result, thpTimeDl contribution for the burst is tEndOfBurst – tSent.

[CNI-112795]

Example 2: Intra-gNB HO

1) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with change in Cell Id and intra-gNB HO in the point of time tRec. 5G-L2-HI CU has PDCP PDU1, PDCP PDU2, PDCP PDU3 which needs to be retransmitted to 5G-L2-HI DU.As there is no Guard Timer running, tRec is evaluated as start of observing a new burst.

2) PDCP PDU1 is retransmitted to 5G-L2-Hi DU via F1 in the point of time t1 and Guard Timer for PDCP PDU1 is started and given as per formula:

(PDCP PDU1 Volume/avgEstTputPDU + avgPduDelvDelayPDU where: avgEstTputPDU is average estimated throughput for the given PDU1, avgPduDelvDelayPDU is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU1 in the point of time t1). At mentioned t1, also is started the Retention Delay Timer (special case of GT for the first packet) and calculated as avgPduDelvDelayPDU time. Regarding the GT calculation, please refer to 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3) As there PDCP PDU2 and PDCP PDU3 are yet to be retransmitted from 5G-L2-HI CU, they are also considered in the same burst

4)   PDCP PDU2 is retransmitted to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t2 and GT for PDCP PDU2 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU2 Volume/avgEstTputPDU) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU (where: avgEstTputPDU is average estimated throughput for the given PDU2, avgPduDelvDelayPDU is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU2 in the point of time t2). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU2 is longer, 5G-L2-HI CU chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

5) Retention Delay expired in the point of time tSent. tSent is considered as a starting point in time to start counting the ThpTimeDl for the given burst.

6) PDCP PDU3 is retransmitted to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t3 and GT for PDCP PDU3 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU3 Volume/avgEstTputPDU) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU (where: avgEstTputPDUis average estimated throughput for the given PDU3, avgPduDelvDelayPDU is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU3 in the point of time t3). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU3 is longer, 5G-L2-HI CU chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

7) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU4 in the point of time t4 OR PDCP SDU4 was received when the bearer was in inactive state. As GT is running, this PDCP SDU4 contributes to the same burst as PDCP PDU1, PDCP PDU2 and PDCP PDU3.

8) Due to GT is still running, 5G-L2-HI CU continues counting of thpTimeDl, even PDCP SDU4 is waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-HI DU and GT for PDCP PDU4 was not recalculated yet.

9) PDCP PDU4 is sent to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t5 and GT for PDCP PDU4 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU4 Volume/avgEstTputPDU) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU(where: avgEstTputPDU is average estimated throughput for the given PDU4, avgPduDelvDelayPDU is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU4 in the point of time t5). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU4 is longer, 5G-L2-HI CU chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

10) 5G-L2-HI CU receives PDCP SDU5 in the point of time t6 OR PDCP SDU5 was received when the bearer was in inactive state. As GT is running, this PDCP SDU5 contributes to the same burst as PDCP PDU1, PDCP PDU2, PDCP PDU3 and PDCP SDU4.

11) Due to GT calculated for PDCP PDU 4 is still running, 5G-L2-HI CU continues counting of thpTimeDl, even PDCP SDU5 is waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-HI DU and GT was not recalculated yet.

12) PDCP PDU5 is sent to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t7 and GT for PDCP PDU5 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU5 Volume/avgEstTputPDU) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU (where: avgEstTputPDU is average estimated throughput for the given PDU5, avgPduDelvDelay is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU5 in the point of time t7). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU5 is longer, 5G-L2Hi choose it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

13) GT expired [PR794319] and DDDS is received from RLC indicating all the PDCP PDUs upto PDU5 are delivered [End PR794319] in the point of time tEndofBurst. Due to [Before PR794319]there is no PDCP SDU waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-HI DU [PR794319] the PDCP buffer is empty[End PR794319], 5G-L2-HI CU shall stop counting thpTimeDl in the point of time tEndOfBurst that represents end of burst in time. In the result, thpTimeDl contribution for the burst is tEndOfBurst – tSent.

Note : Change in the Cell Id is considered as the end of ongoing burst, irrespective of there is unsent PDCP SDU or not. Sending of the subsequent PDCP PDU to 5G-L2-HI DU shall be considered under a new burst with the new cell.

When dataDuplication=TRUE, all the PDUs are retransmitted in target cell, whereas when dataDuplication=FALSE, PDUs which are not indicated as TRANSMITTED in source cell are retransmitted in target cell.

Example 3: Intra-gNB HO and pdcpStatusReportWaitTimer = 0 received in HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause=Suspend

1) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause=suspend for intra-gNB HO.

2) 5G-L2-HI CU receives first UL PDCP PDU. Since pdcpStatusReportWaitTimer = 0, 5G-L2-HI CU starts retransimitting PDCP PDU1 to 5G-L2-HI DU. Since no cell change indicated(as no HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cell id change is received), retransmision of PDUs is not considered as a new burst, as these PDUs transmission already accounted in the source cell before the HO.

3) HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq is received with cause=resume and change in cell Id at time point tRec. As there are 2 PDUs PDCP PDU2 and PDCP PDU3 are yet to be retransmitted from 5G-L2-HI CU and no Guard timer is running, this is considered the observation of new burst.

4)   PDCP PDU2 is retransmitted to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t1 and GT for PDCP PDU2 is calculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU2 Volume/avgEstTputPDU) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU (where: avgEstTputPDUis average estimated throughput for the given PDU2, avgPduDelvDelayPDU is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU2 in the point of time t2). At mentioned t1, also is started the Retention Delay Timer (special case of GT for the first packet) and calculated as avgPduDelvDelayPDU time. Regarding the GT calculation, please refer to 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5) Retention Delay expired in the point of time tSent. tSent is considered as a starting point in time to start counting the ThpTimeDl for the given burst.

6) PDCP PDU3 is retransmitted to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t2 and GT for PDCP PDU3 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU3 Volume/avgEstTputPDU) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU (where: avgEstTputPDU is average estimated throughput for the given PDU3, avgPduDelvDelayPDU is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU3 in the point of time t2). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU3 is longer, 5G-L2-HI CU chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

7) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU4 in the point of time t3. As GT is running, this PDCP SDU4 contributes to the same burst as PDCP PDU2 and PDCP PDU3.

8) Due to GT is still running, 5G-L2-HI CU continues counting of thpTimeDl, even PDCP SDU4 is waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-HI DU and GT for PDCP PDU4 was not recalculated yet.

9) PDCP PDU4 is sent to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t4 and GT for PDCP PDU4 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU4 Volume/avgEstTputPDU) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU(where: avgEstTputPDU is average estimated throughput for the given PDU4, avgPduDelvDelayPDU is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU4 in the point of time t4). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU4 is longer, 5G-L2-HI CU chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

10) 5G-L2-HI CU receives PDCP SDU5 in the point of time t5. As GT is running, this PDCP SDU5 contributes to the same burst as PDCP PDU2, PDCP PDU3 and PDCP SDU4.

11) Due to GT calculated for PDCP PDU 4 is still running, 5G-L2-HI CU continues counting of thpTimeDl, even PDCP SDU5 is waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-HI DU and GT was not recalculated yet.

12) PDCP PDU5 is sent to 5G-L2-HI DU via F1 in the point of time t6 and GT for PDCP PDU5 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU5 Volume/avgEstTputPDU) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU (where: avgEstTputPDU is average estimated throughput for the given PDU5, avgPduDelvDelay is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU5 in the point of time t6). As GT calculated for PDCP PDU5 is longer, 5G-L2Hi choose it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

13) GT expired [PR794319] and DDDS is received from RLC indicating the successful delivey of all the PDCP PDUs upto PDU5[End PR794319] in the point of time tEndofBurst. Due to [Before PR794319]there is no PDCP SDU waiting for transmission to 5G-L2-HI DU[PR794319] the PDCP buffer is empty[End PR794319] , 5G-L2-HI CU shall stop counting thpTimeDl in the point of time tEndOfBurst that represents end of burst in time. In the result, thpTimeDl contribution for the burst is tEndOfBurst – tSent.

[End CNI-112795]

Note: For GT calculation please see 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11238149`)

PM Counters
Burst start and end for PDU throughput calculation

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11238155`)

PM Counters
Beginning of a burst shall be identified as a sending of PDCP PDU to 5G-L2-Hi DU for an active bearer or the transition of bearer from inactive to active state.

Start timestamp tStart to start counting the thpTimeDl of the burst is defined as expiration of Retention Delay Timer.

5G-L2-HI CU shall estimate PDCP PDU transmission time(Guard Timer) during sending the packet towards DU.

5G-L2-Hi CU shall set the timestamp end of Burst equal to the timestamp of expiration of the latest Guard Timer, (even if it was calculated not for the last sent packet). See also the diagram 5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_574\_replaced([11198073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Bf-fwvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: Retention Delay is a special case of Guard Timer calculated on first PDU sending. Defines the time of the first packet lagging in the buffer and is excluded from Burst report due to compensation of the time that is needed to calculate the actual time for the packet to exit from gNB/eNB to UE.

Example:

1)    5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU1 OR PDCP SDU1 was received when the bearer was in inactive state and process it into PDCP PDU1.

2) PDCP PDU1 is sent from 5G-L2-Hi CU to DU via F1 and Guard Timer (GT) for PDCP PDU1 is started and given as per formula: (PDCP PDU1 Volume/avgEstTputPDU1) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU1 (where: avgEstTputPDU1 is average estimated throughput for the given PDU1, avgPduDelvDelayPDU1 is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU1). At sending PDCP PDU1, also is started the Retention Delay Timer (special case of GT for the first packet) and calculated as avgPduDelvDelayPDU1 time. Regarding the GT calculation, please refer to 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Sending of PDCP PDU1 towards 5G-L2-Hi DU, L2Hi shall consider as a start of the burst for calculation of PDCP PDU downlink throughput per 5G and LTE leg separately.

3) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU2 OR PDCP SDU2 was received when the bearer was in inactive state and process it into PDCP PDU2.

4) PDCP PDU2 is sent to 5G-L2-Hi DU via F1 and GT for PDCP PDU2 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU2 Volume/avgEstTputPDU2) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU2 (where: avgEstTputPDU2 is average estimated throughput for the given PDU2, avgPduDelvDelayPDU2 is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU2). Due to GT is running already, this PDCP PDU2 contributes to the same burst as PDCP PDU1. In this moment also, 5G-L2-Hi shall recalculate GT at sending PDCP PDU2 and as it is longer than remained part of GT calculated for PDCP PDU1, 5G-L2Hi chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

5) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU3 OR PDCP SDU3 was received when the bearer was in inactive state and process it into PDCP PDU3.

6) Retention Delay expired in the point of time tStart. tStart is considered as a starting point in time for counting the ThpTimeDl for the given burst.

7) PDCP PDU3 is sent to 5G-L2-Hi DU via F1 and GT for PDCP PDU3 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU3 Volume/avgEstTputPDU3) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU3 (where: avgEstTputPDU3 is average estimated throughput for the given PDU3, avgPduDelvDelayPDU3 is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU3). Due to GT is running already, this PDCP PDU3 contributes to the same burst as PDCP PDU1 and PDCP PDU2. In this moment also, 5G-L2-Hi shall recalculate GT at sending PDCP PDU3 and as it is longer than remained part of GT calculated for PDCP PDU2, 5G-L2Hi chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

8) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU4 OR PDCP SDU4 was received when the bearer was in inactive state and process it into PDCP PDU4.

9) PDCP PDU4 is sent to 5G-L2-Hi DU via F1 and GT for PDCP PDU4 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU4 Volume/avgEstTputPDU4) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU4 (where: avgEstTputPDU4 is average estimated throughput for the given PDU4, avgPduDelvDelayPDU4 is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU4). Due to GT is running already, this PDCP PDU4 contributes to the same burst as PDCP PDU1, PDCP PDU2 and PDCP PDU3. In this moment also, 5G-L2-Hi shall recalculate GT at sending PDCP PDU4 and as it is longer than remained part of GT calculated for PDCP PDU3, 5G-L2Hi chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

10) 5G-L2-Hi CU receives PDCP SDU5 OR PDCP SDU5 was received when the bearer was in inactive state and process it into PDCP PDU5.

11) PDCP PDU5 is sent to 5G-L2-Hi DU via F1 and GT for PDCP PDU5 is recalculated as per formula:

(PDCP PDU5 Volume/avgEstTputPDU5) + avgPduDelvDelayPDU5 (where: avgEstTputPDU5 is average estimated throughput for the given PDU5, avgPduDelvDelay is average PDU delivery delay for the given PDU5). Due to GT is running already, this PDCP PDU5 contributes to the same burst as PDCP PDU1, PDCP PDU2, PDCP PDU3 and PDCP PDU4. In this moment also, 5G-L2-Hi shall recalculate GT at sending PDCP PDU5 and as it is longer than remained part of GT calculated for PDCP PDU4, 5G-L2Hi chooses it as the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

12) If GT expired in the point of time tEndofBurst, 5G-L2-Hi shall stop counting thpTimeDl in the point of time tEndOfBurst that represents end of burst in time. In the result, thpTimeDl contribution for the burst is tEndOfBurst – tStart and thpVolumeDl = PDCP PDU1+PDCP PDU2+PDCP PDU3+PDCP PDU4+PDCP PDU5.

Note: For GT calculation please see 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11238161`)

PM Counters
Packet handling

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11238167`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-Hi CU shall handle each packet that was received (not taking SN into consideration) according to the 3GPP specification (TS 28.552).

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11238173`)

PM Counters
Burst lasting time

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11238178`)

PM Counters
[Before 02647778]

L2-Hi CU shall report Burst Lasting Time that is counted from Retention Delay expiry to last GT expiry.

Notes:

 L2-Hi shall not include Retention Delay into reported Burst lasting time counter. However, Burst is considered as ongoing with receiving of first PDU and ends with last GT expiring.

 Burst shall be ended only in case of expiration of GT with bearer PDCP buffer empty OR at Bearer Delete.

[End 02647778]

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11238185`)

PM Counters
Guard Timer

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11238196`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-Hi CU shall calculate Guard Timer expiration according to the following formula:

 Old method: Guard Timer = PdcpPduSize/DDR,

 New method: Guard Timer = (PdcpPduSize/eTh)+F1 delay+DU buffer size = (PdcpPduSize/avgEstTput) + avgPduDelvDelay

Where:

PdcpPduSize – size of PDCP PDU within identified burst,

DDR – Desired Data Rate received as a part of DDDS,

eTh=avgEstTput – average estimated throughput (computed as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5494\_replaced([11219294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpoI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for F1, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5564\_replaced([11219679](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsEYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for X2),

F1 delay+DU buffer size=avgPduDelvDelay – average PDU delivery delay (computed as given in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5497\_replaced([11219322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpoJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for F1, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5568\_replaced([11219701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsEY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for X2).

Notes:

1) Guard Timer is calculated for each packet. 5G-L2Hi always choose the latest GT expiry time to know when burst will end.

2) The following changes in the formula for GT:

- Additional factor avgPduDelvDelay

- change from DDR to avgEstTput

are considered if 5G-L2-Hi CU obtains thpTimeCalc=TRUE in HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq.

3) In case of EN-DC the same principle as described in the 5G\_L2\_7878\_replaced([11238117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6d_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in example shall be applied. The only difference is that if related PDCP PDUx is transmitted via LTE leg to lower layers of eNB via X2 interface in point of time tx then in this point in time (tx) the “GT PDCP PDUxeNB” is started and given as (PdcpPduSize/eTh)+X2 delay+eNB buffer delay = (PdcpPduSize/avgEstTputX2) + avgPduDelvDelayX2.

4)   Special case of GT: Retention Delay=avgPduDelvDelay in case of F1-U OR Retention Delay=avgPduDelvDelayX2 in case of X2-U.

5)   In case of Flow Control is disabled, counters based on Guard Timer [CB010240-B] new method calculation [End CB010240-B] will not be pegged, [Before CB010240-B] if thpTimeCalc=TRUE. [End CB010240-B]

[CB010240-B]

6)   For Calculation of:

- PDCP PDU downlink throughput per 5G and LTE leg separately, shall be used only new method of Guard Timer/Retention Delay calculation.

- PDCP SDU downlink throughput, old or new method of Guard Timer/Retention Delay calculation shall be used  depending on thpTimeCalc is set to FALSE or TRUE.

[End CB010240-B]

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `11238202`)

PM Counters
DDR Handling for GT calculation

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11238208`)

PM Counters
No DDDS reported

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11238215`)

PM Counters
If there is no DDDS report received either from F1-U or Xx-U interface, then the starting value of DDR shall be based on the default value of 125 B/ms (based on default value of NIDD R&D parameter “Minimum throughput from flow control” related to the 3GPP Flow Control Algorithm) to calculate GT expiry.

[02647778]

This requirement is valid only if thpTimeCalc=FALSE. If thpTimeCalc=TRUE, DDR in the formula for Guard Timer is changed to avgEstTput. Please refer to 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 02647778]

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11238221`)

PM Counters
DDDS without DDR or DDR equal to zero

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11238225`)

PM Counters
If newly received DDDS did not contain DDR or DDR is equal to zero, then the DDR value is calculated as following:

DDR Calculated = 80% \* estimatedDDR + 20% \* previousDDR,

Where: estimatedDDR=sumOfOutFlowVolume/elapsedTimeDelta

elapsedTimeDelta=tNow – timePointofLastReceivedDdds

Notes:

 If sumOfOutFlowVolume = 0, then estimated DDR shall be set to 1.

 If elapsedTimeDelta value is 0, then value shall be set to 1.

 The Calculated value of DDR is always rounded up.

 If this is the first DDDS after sending of the first PDU AND no DDR at the same time, then the Time Point of last received DDDS is the sending time of the first PDU.

[02647778]

This requirement is valid only if thpTimeCalc=FALSE. If thpTimeCalc=TRUE, DDR in the formula for Guard Timer is changed to avgEstTput. Please refer to 5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 02647778]

PM Counters
PDCP SDU Throughput

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11238249`)

PM Counters
Volume Counters

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11238254`)

PM Counters
DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11238266`)

PM Counters
[Before CB013554-A]

5G-L2-HI CU shall update below downlink volume counters:

 M55350C01001 … 20 (DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_QOS\_01 ... 20) ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55350C03001... 20 (DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_5G\_QOS01 ... 20) ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level on 5G Leg - QoS Group 01 ... 20

 M55350C05001 ... 20 (DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_LTE\_QOS01 ... 20) ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level on LTE Leg - QoS Group 01 ... 20 (see Note2)

 M55352C01001 (DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_PMQAP) ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level Total NRPMQAP

 M55350C07001 (DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_TOT) ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level Total

for each identified burst (See 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Notes:

Note:

1. 5G-L2-HI CU shall accumulate volume counters after packet sending from PDCP to RLC over F1 interface or from PDCP to RLC located in eNB over X2 interface.
2. M55350C05001 ... 20 counters are related to EN-DC technology only and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user.

[CB013554-A]

Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline.Please see 5G\_L2\_19305\_replaced([11238271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BPIkPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19306\_replaced([11238312](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BPIl_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_19307\_replaced([11238341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BPInPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB013554-A]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11238271`)

PM Counters
DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11238277`)

PM Counters
QoS level

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11238283`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell (PDCPC)

NetAct name: DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_QOS\_01 ... DL\_PDCP\_VOL\_UE\_TPUT\_QOS\_20

PI ID: M55350C01001 ... M55350C01020

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: Counter are updated for each identified burst as defined in 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Additional info:

1. Burst definition can be found under 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. 5G-L2-HI CU shall accumulate volume counters after packet sending from PDCP to RLC over F1 interface or from PDCP to RLC located in eNB over X2 interface

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11238288`)

PM Counters
Total cell level

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11238384`)

PM Counters
Time Counter

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11238388`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI CU shall update downlink time counters:

 M55350C00001 ... 20 (DL\_PDCP\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT\_QOS\_01 ... 20) ThpTimeDl DL UE Throughput Time at PDCP SDU Level - QoS Group 01 ... 20

[CB006898-B]

 M55352C00001 (DL\_PDCP\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT\_PMQAP) ThpTimeDl DL UE Throughput Time at PDCP SDU Level NRPMQAP

[End CB006898-B]

[CB006898-C]

 M55350C08001 (DL\_PDCP\_TIME\_UE\_TPUT) ThpTimeDl DL UE Throughput Time at PDCP SDU Level

[End CB006898-C]

for each identified burst (See 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Updated value shall be decreased by initial retention delay:

Initial delay retention = firstPdcpPduSize / DDR,

Where:

DDR – Desired data rate IE received as a part of Downlink Data Delivery Status,

firstPdcpPduSize – size of first PDCP PDU within identified burst.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `11238395`)

PM Counters
Max Counters

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11238406`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI CU shall update below downlink max throughput counters:

 M55350C02001 (MAX\_DL\_PDCP\_BURST\_TPUT) Max DL PDCP Data burst throughput transmitted for the cell

 M55350C04001 (MAX\_DL\_PDCP\_BURST\_TPUT\_5GLEG) Max DL PDCP Data burst throughput transmitted for the cell on 5G Leg

 M55350C06001 (MAX\_DL\_PDCP\_BURST\_TPUT\_5GLEG) Max DL PDCP Data burst throughput transmitted for the cell on 5G Leg (see note1)

for the cell, with Downlink throughput ThpDli value calculated for each valid burst occurring on any QoS group and corresponding leg, only if the current calculated throughput is greater than the previous max value.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$ThpDl\_i = \frac{ThpVolDl\_i}{TheTimeDl\_i}$, where
The text "where" is also present after the equation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_15401.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

 ThpDli- Throughput of i-th downlink burst

 ThpVolDli– Volume of i-th downlink burst

 ThpTimeDli- Time of i-th downlink burst

Notes:

1. [CB008717-D-UPD004] M55350C06001 counter is related to EN-DC technology only and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user. [End CB008717-D-UPD004]

for each identified burst (See 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-7**  (ID: `11238489`)

PM Counters
Exclusions

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11238494`)

PM Counters
For DL PDCP SDU throughput

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11238501`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI CU shall exclude transmission time and volume of a burst, which is:

1. smaller than [Before CB008009-A] VolThresholdDiscard [CB008009-A] volThresDiscardDl [End CB008009-A]

OR

2. shorter than [Before CB008009-A] DurationThresholdDiscard [CB008009-A] durationThresDiscardDl [End CB008009-A].

Notes:

1. [Before CB008009-A] VolThresholdDiscard and DurationThresholdDiscard [CB008009-A] volThresDiscardDl and durationThresDiscardDl [End CB008009-A] are configured per bearer and delivered to 5G-L2-HI CU via HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq. If any of these thresholds is set to 0, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall report burst only if the value is greater than 0. However, if thresholds are not set at all, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall use default values.

2. In case burst consist both 4G and 5G data, then volume should be summed before comparing it against [Before CB008009-A] VolThresholdDiscard [CB008009-A] volThresDiscardDl [End CB008009-A].

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11238506`)

PM Counters
For DL PDCP PDU throughput per 5G and LTE leg separately

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11238512`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI CU shall exclude transmission time and volume of a burst, which is:

1. In case of 5G leg:

smaller than volThresDiscardDlPdcpPdu5Gleg

OR

shorter than durationThresDiscardDlPdcpPdu5GLeg

1. in case of LTE leg:

smaller than volThresDiscardDlPdcpPduLteLeg

OR

shorter than durationThresDiscardDlPdcpPduLteLeg

Notes:

1. Volume and duration discard thresholds are configured per bearer and delivered to 5G-L2-HI CU via HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq. If any of these thresholds is set to 0, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall report burst only if the value is greater than 0 (everything what is greater than 1us and 1bit).
2. Threshold discard parameters for volume and time can be found under 5G\_L2\_IF\_4992\_replaced([10992699](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2W57gvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
3. If the volume/time threshold discard parameters are invalid (i.e. out of range), L2Hi should not update volume/time counters.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-8**  (ID: `11238517`)

PM Counters
Cell related counters handling

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11238523`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI shall obtain Cell Identity (nrCellIdentity) from the list of cells (nrCellIdsForThroughputReporting) received from 5G-CP-NRT / 5G-CP-RT in message HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq / HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq message.

5G-L2-HI shall match bearers with the cell according to the information received in HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq / HiUserDu\_BearerSetupReq or HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq (CU only, refer to 5G\_L2\_3897\_replaced([11238790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BSy_fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and start collecting counters and reporting them for those cells.

In case of receiving new cell lists via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq / HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq, 5G-L2-Hi shall stop collecting counters and reporting for those cells that are not included in new list of cells.

For not changed cells and existing bearers the collecting counters and reporting shall be continued.

Note: General information about PM Counter management: creation and removing of NRCELL related PM objects can be found under 5G\_L2\_2780\_replaced([11235879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A8NpfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for CU and 5G\_L2\_2778\_replaced([11233560](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3ArH6vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DU.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9**  (ID: `11238528`)

PM Counters
PMQAP Profiles counters handling

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11238535`)

PM Counters
Obtaining PMQAP profile and activation status

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11238551`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-Hi shall obtain PMQAP profile configuration and activation status dependent on non-zero size of pmqapProfileList from

 5G-CP-NRT via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq

 5G-CP-RT via HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq

only when nrCellIdsForThroughputReporting (cell list) is not empty and report counters for only those bearers that fit to profile defined by operator.

5G-L2-Hi shall obtain from Cplane already matched profiles to the bearer by receiving pmqapProfileList in HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq/HiUserDu\_BearerSetupReq.

5G-L2-Hi shall support up to [Before CB008933-A] 20 [CB008933-A] 40 [End CB008933-A] PMQAP profiles.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11238558`)

PM Counters
Profile configuration

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11238569`)

PM Counters
[Before CB008828-A]

5G-L2-Hi shall support up to 20 PMQAP profiles.

Each profile can be configured using the following parameters:

· NRBTS/NRPMRNL/NRPMQAP/nrPmqapId - will be used to uniquely identify the New Radio Performance Monitoring QCI ARP Profiles (NRPMQAP) instance within the same containing NRBTS/NRPMRNL instance.

· MRBTS/NRBTS/NRPMRNL/NRPMQAP/cfgProfType - will be used to determine a type of created profile {NSA, SA or both}.

· MRBTS/NRBTS/NRPMRNL/NRPMQAP/cfgQciRange

· MRBTS/NRBTS/NRPMRNL/NRPMQAP/cfgPlmnId

· MRBTS/NRBTS/NRPMRNL/NRPMQAP/cfg5qiRange

· MRBTS/NRBTS/NRPMRNL/NRPMQAP/cfgSliceId

MRBTS/NRBTS/NRPMRNL/NRPMQAP/cfgSliceId/sst

MRBTS/NRBTS/NRPMRNL/NRPMQAP/cfgSliceId/sd

Note:

1. If cfgProfType is set to "SA" then only parameters applicable to SA bearers (5QI, Slice, PLMN) and only SA bearers themselves are taken into consideration when applying profile checks per bearers.

2. If cfgProfType is set to "NSA" then only parameters applicable to NSA bearers (QCI, PLMN) and only NSA bearers themselves are taken into consideration when applying profile checks per NSA bearers.

3. If cfgProfType is set to "both" then all parameters of SA and NSA bearers are taken into consideration when applying profile checks per bearer. If in CnfgParamReq 5G-L2-Hi will obtain profile Type = both shall ignore SA values for NSA bearer and other way round.

L2Hi shall support the following parameters values:

QCI empty value, range (5-9, 69-70, 79, 98-100, 128-254), (QCI is valid for NSA bearer)

5QI empty value, range (1-9, 71-72, 76, 80, 128-254), (5QI is valid for SA bearer)

PLMN empty value, individual value

Slice empty value, individual value (Slice is valid for SA bearer)

Note: While PLMN and Slice are individual values, QCI and 5QI are in ranges. In case of one profile only one range (from available) per parameter can be set by operator.

Interpretation of received profile parameters values:

1. The Operator can set multiple ranges of values and individual values for the parameter. Only the values from those ranges will be used while applying profile checks.

2. If parameter was not included in the profile definition (empty value was received), then while incrementing counters the value of the according bearer attribute is of no importance and will cause counter to increment. If some profile parameter is not set, then 5G-L2-Hi shall take into account all the bearers for which the rest of profile parameters match (empty value for a valid parameter means “any”).

3. If the profile has not a valid value (out of range), 5G-L2-Hi shall send NOK.

Note:

1. If UE's bearer has not assigned attribute value (e.g. there is no PLMN during emergency call without SIM card) then such bearer is not taken into consideration while incrementing counters regardless of the parameter value set in profile definition.

2. When all parameters for SA part (PLMN, 5QI, Slice) or NSA part (PLMN, QCI) of profile, or all parameters are set as empty, then profile counters will behave as their non-profile counterparts.

3. If cfgProfType is set to "both", the parameters for that profile can be set with values corresponding simultaneously to NSA and SA – in that case 5G-L2-Hi shall take proper values for updating NSA or SA specific counters (e.g. 5QI or Slice of a bearer are considered while incrementing SA counter).

4.   5G-L2-Hi shall not validate ranges of QCI and 5QI that are not supported in the system as:

 they’re not validated on the bearer level

 and such validation does not impact the functionality (counter pegging) at all.

[End CB008828-A]

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-3**  (ID: `11238576`)

PM Counters
Receiving new profile configuration

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11238582`)

PM Counters
In case of receiving new profile configuration via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq/ HiCnfgDu\_ConfigParamReq, 5G-L2-Hi shall stop collecting counters and reporting for those profiles that are not included in new profile configuration. 5G-L2-Hi shall apply new profile configuration for bearers.

Example: During the burst bearer belongs to Profile1. In meantime 5G-L2-Hi obtain new profile configuration via ConfigParamReq and in the result bearer belongs to Profile2. When burst will end, 5G-L2-Hi shall increment counters for Profile2.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-4**  (ID: `11238589`)

PM Counters
Not existing profiles

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11238592`)

PM Counters
Although PMQAP profile reconfiguration for existing bearers is not supported, L2Hi shall handle cases where a given PMQAP profile no longer exists. In such situation, L2Hi shall act on common part of old and new list of profiles and remove not existing PMQAP profiles from the profile list for the given bearer. It can appear in the following cases:

* L2HI receives not existing NR PMQAP IDs:

HiCnfgCu/Du\_ConfigParamReq: new profiles (NR PMQAP IDs) 1,2,3

HiUserCu/Du\_BearerSetupReq: profiles (NR PMQAP IDs) 1,3,5

L2Hi shall have configured profiles: 1 and 3.

* Online PMQAP profiles reconfiguration:

Old HiCnfgCu/Du\_ConfigParamReq (NR PMQAP IDs): 1,2,3,4,5

HiUserCu/DU\_BearerSetupReq (NR PMQAP IDs): 1,3,5

New HiCnfgCu/Du\_ConfigParamReq(NR PMQAP IDs): 1,2,3

Existing Bearer Context (NR PMQAP IDs): 1,3

Bearer context: profiles 1 and 3.

* Profile reconfiguration during bearer setup:

HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq: profiles (NR PMQAP IDs) 1,2,3,4,5

HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq: profiles (NR PMQAP IDs) 1,3,5

L2Hi obtains new profile configuration:

HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq: profiles (NR PMQAP IDs) 1,2,3

Then L2Hi obtains HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq with cause=BearerSetup:

CuPdcpDlOffloadBearerSetupReq: profiles (NR PMQAP IDs) 1,3,5

DL OFFLOAD Bearer context: profiles 1 and 3.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-5**  (ID: `11238600`)

PM Counters
Profiles duplication

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-9.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11238607`)

PM Counters
If any NR PMQAP profile is repeated twice in HiUserCu/Du\_BearerSetupReq, L2Hi shall consider given PMQAP profile only once:

* Profile list in bearer setup contains duplicated NR PMQAP ID:

HiCnfgCu/Du\_ConfigParamReq: profiles (NR PMQAP IDs) 1,2,3,4,5

HiUserCu/Du\_BearerSetupReq: profiles (NR PMQAP IDs) 1,3,5,3

Bearer context: profiles 1,3 and 5.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-10**  (ID: `11238611`)

PM Counters
Mobility cases during Measuring DL PDCP SDU throughput

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-10.0-2**  (ID: `11238621`)

PM Counters
Upon reception of HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq message, 5G-L2-HI shall check if the newly received NrCellIdentity parameter value is set and is different than previously set (in HiCnfgCu\_BearerSetupReq or HiCnfgCu\_BearerModifyReq).

If this condition is fulfilled, 5G-L2-HI shall stop the Burst and incrementing counters for old NrCellIdentity and start incrementing counters for new NrCellIdentity:

* M55350C00001-20 - ThpTimeDl DL UE Throughput Time at PDCP SDU Level - QoS Group 01-20
* M55350C01001-20 - ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level - QoS Group 01-20
* M55350C03001-20 - ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level on 5G Leg - QoS Group 01-20
* M55350C05001-20 - ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level on LTE Leg - QoS Group 01-20 (see Note2)
* M55350C02001 - Max DL PDCP Data burst throughput transmitted for the cell
* M55350C04001 - Max DL PDCP Data burst throughput transmitted for the cell on 5G Leg
* M55350C06001 - Max DL PDCP Data burst throughput transmitted for the cell on LTE Leg (see Note2)
* M55350C08001 - ThpTimeDl DL UE Throughput Time at PDCP SDU Level
* M55350C07001 - ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP SDU Level Total

[CB010240-B]

 M55352C01002 - ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP PDU Level on 5G Leg NRPMQAP

* M55352C01004 - ThpVolDl DL UE Throughput Volume at PDCP PDU Level on LTE Leg NRPMQAP
* M55352C01003 - ThpTimeDl DL UE Throughput Time at PDCP PDU Level on 5G Leg NRPMQAP
* M55352C01005 - ThpTimeDl DL UE Throughput Time at PDCP PDU Level on LTE Leg NRPMQAP

[End CB010240-B]

Rationale: The new NrCellIdentity represents the Target cell in case of intra-gNB Handover, when only modification (ECause\_MobilityResume) of bearer is needed.

Note:

1. The inter-RAT or inter-gNB Handover types need creating new bearer contexts in CU and DU L2-HI instances, so they are handled by bearer setup requests.
2. M55350C05001-20 and M55350C06001 counters are related to EN-DC technology only and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-11**  (ID: `11238627`)

PM Counters
Histogram

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11238633`)

PM Counters
Scale and ranges

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-11.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11238639`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-Hi CU shall provide the distribution of the UE throughput in DL via histogram based on throughput distribution counters (please refer to 5G\_L2\_9887\_replaced([11238411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BPvqvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and DL burst definition (please refer to 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

To configure the throughput ranges of the histogram, 5G-L2-HI CU shall use the following NIDD Distribution Parameters obtained via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq:

 HistScale [Linear, Logarithmic]: This parameter allows the user to set the Histogram BIN distribution ranges as Linear or Logarithmic scale.

 HistDownlinkMaxRange [bps]: This parameter set's the lower bound in range of the highest BIN. This value is the estimated value of the highest BIN i.e., BIN 20 for DL throughput distribution. NOTE: This is an estimated max, thus if during calculation, the DL throughput for a certain measurement period exceeds this value, it is still reported under BIN 20.

 HistDownlinkMinRange [bps]:  This parameter set's the upper bound range of the lowest BIN. This value is the highest value of the lowest BIN i.e., BIN 01 for DL throughput distribution. This parameter is set only when the HistScale parameter is set as Logarithmic.

Note:

1) The distribution of the histogram shall be spread into 20 BINs.

2) 5G-L2-Hi CU shall use PMQAP Profile (please refer to 5G\_L2\_3337\_replaced([11238528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BQ9wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for creating distribution counters when distribution to BIN is done for the Throughput counters per QCI, 5QI, PLMN and Slice. BIN definition is for each PMQAP profile and one for non-PMQAP.

3) The BIN range is set as follows: lower range < thr value < = upper range and under the following excel file: <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB008000%20-%20CB008499/CFAM/CB008009%20Throughput%20distribution%20counters/CB008009%20bin%20ranges.xlsx?d=w3b92ddb0513648e382571ad32c7b126d&csf=1&web=1&e=IpbrPf>

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-11.0-2**  (ID: `11238643`)

PM Counters
BIN triggering

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-11.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11238668`)

PM Counters
[CB013684-G] 5G-L2-Hi shall update throughput distribution BIN counters for:

- DL PDCP SDU (please refer to 5G\_L2\_9887\_replaced([11238411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BPvqvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- UL RLC SDU (please refer to 5G\_L2\_9885\_replaced([11235651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3A6YevvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- RLC PDU (MAC SDU) (please refer to 5G\_L2\_21558\_replaced([11234545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3AycqPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

once per burst or once per second according to the cfgThptDistUpdate received via HiCnfgCu/Du\_ConfigParamReq:PmCountersInfo:ThptHistParams:Histogram (5G\_L2\_IF\_4122\_replaced([10992760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2W57jPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB013684-G]

[CB013684-G] If received cfgThptDistUpdate will be set to 0, it means that [End CB013684-G] 5G-L2-HI shall calculate BIN number based on throughput calculated during 1-second period. If burst is smaller than 1 second, L2-HI shall aggregate all small bursts until sum of their duration will exceed one second. If burst is longer than 1 second, then 5G-L2-Hi shall divide this burst into few 1-second bursts and increment one of the BINs for each period as shown in the following drawing:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a timeline diagram illustrating four bursts of activity, labeled Burst 1 through Burst 4, with their respective durations. Each burst is represented by a blue rectangle, and its duration is indicated by text above or within the rectangle. The timeline is marked by dashed vertical lines, representing 1-second periods. Below the timeline, text indicates "BIN updated for 1 second period" at the beginning of each 1-second interval.
Here's a breakdown of each burst:
\* **Burst 1:** Duration of 0.2 seconds. It is shown as two segments, each 0.2 seconds long, occurring sequentially.
\* **Burst 2:** Duration of 1.2 seconds. It is depicted as two segments: one of 0.8 seconds and another of 0.4 seconds, totaling 1.2 seconds.
\* **Burst 3:** Duration of 1 second. It is shown as two segments: one of 0.6 seconds and another of 0.4 seconds, totaling 1 second.
\* **Burst 4:** Duration of 5.5 seconds. This burst spans multiple 1-second periods and is represented by several segments: 0.6 seconds, 1 second, 1 second, 1 second, 1 second, and 0.9 seconds, totaling 5.5 seconds.
The diagram visually represents how these bursts are distributed over time and how they align with the 1-second update periods for "BIN".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_15444.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

 Due to Burst 1 takes 0,2 sec (< 1-sec period), 5G-L2-Hi shall not trigger the BIN and save information about volume and time for the next Burst 2 calculation.

 Burst 2 takes 1,2 sec, so 5G-L2-Hi shall take the 0,2 sec from the previous Burst 1 and 0,8 sec from the current Burst 2 (that gives 1-second period), count the average throughput and trigger BIN. The remaining 0,4 sec should be saved for the next Burst 3 calculation.

 Burst 3 takes 1 sec, so 5G-L2-Hi shall take remaining 0,4 sec from the previous Burst 2 and 0,6 sec from the current Burst 3 (that gives 1-second period), count the average throughout and trigger BIN. The remaining 0,4 sec should be saved for the next Burst 4 calculation.

 Burst 4 takes 5,5 sec, so 5G-L2-Hi shall take remaining 0,4 sec from the previous Burst 3 and 0,6 sec from the current Burst 4 (that gives 1-second period), count the average throughput and trigger BIN. 5G-L2Hi shall  divide remaining 4,9 sec as shown in the example, count average throughput for the next four 1-second periods and trigger BIN four times. The remaining 0,9 sec should be saved for the next incoming burst.

[CB013684-G] Volume shall be calculated in proportion to the duration period taken into 1-second period.

If received cfgThptDistUpdate will be set to 1, it means that 5G-L2-HI shall calculate BIN number based on throughput calculated for burst.

The moment of updating proper BIN is at the end of the global burst regardless of the cfgThptDistUpdate setting.

[End CB013684-G]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-12.0-1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11238696`)

PM Counters
[Before CNI-112795]

5G-L2-HI CU shall update counters:

 M55350C00030 (DL\_INIT\_BURST\_PDCP) Number of DL initial Bursts

 M55159C00008 (DL\_INIT\_BURST\_PDCP\_PMQAP) Number of DL initial Bursts at Profile level

Notes:

1. Burst identification can be found under 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. PMQAP information can be found under 5G\_L2\_3337\_replaced([11238528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BQ9wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
3. Counters DL\_INIT\_BURST\_PDCP/DL\_INIT\_BURST\_PDCP\_PMQAP can be used as the denominator of DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB/DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB\_PMQAP (5G\_L2\_12939\_replaced([11238716](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BSL6fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) respectively to calculate the average delay per DL INIT Scheduling delay.

[CNI-112795]

Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell

NetAct name: DL\_INIT\_BURST\_PDCP

PI ID: M55350C00030

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Also refer to 5G\_PM\_1225.

Update time: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Additional info:

1. Burst identification can be found under 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. This counter shall be reported only for the burst which is started due to the incoming PDCP SDU from the core to the empty PDCP buffer. This means, the counter is not reported for the burst in the below scenarios:

(i) burst initiated due to the transition of the bearer state from INACTIVE to ACTIVE.

(ii) burst consisiting of PDCP PDU retransmission after the intra-gNB HO.

(iii) burst consisting of sending of forwarded PDCP PDUs/SDUs to DU.

1. Counter DL\_INIT\_BURST\_PDCP can be used as the denominator of DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB(5G\_L2\_12939\_replaced([11238716](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BSL6fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to calculate the average delay per DL INIT Scheduling delay.

[End CNI-112795]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-12.0-2**  (ID: `11238716`)

PM Counters
Initial burst scheduling delay

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-12.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11238720`)

PM Counters
Cell Level

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-12.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11238731`)

PM Counters
[Before CNI-112795]

5G-L2-HI CU shall update  counters:

 M55350C00029 (DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB) DL gNB initial bust scheduling delay

 M55159C00007 (DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB\_PMQAP) DL gNB initial bust scheduling delay at Profile level

Notes:

1. Burst identification can be found under 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. PMQAP information can be found under 5G\_L2\_3337\_replaced([11238528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BQ9wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
3. Counters DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB/DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB\_PMQAP are updated by the Guard Timer value which is used for calculating DL PDCP Throughput based on the method associated to thpTimCalc=TRUE (5G\_L2\_3065\_replaced([11238185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BOhgfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
4. Counters are reported in microsecond, but average delay per DL INIT Scheduling delay(DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB/DL\_INIT\_BURST\_PDCP) should be reported in miliseconds. For this purpose it shall be rounded down the value to the nearest millisecond.
5. Due to limited possibilities of counting the initial burst scheduling delay at the L2Hi level, the value oof those counters will never exceed the value of the retention delay timer.

[CNI-112795]

Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell

NetAct name: DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB

PI ID: M55350C00029

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Also refer to 5G\_PM\_1225.

Update time: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Additional info:

1. Burst identification can be found under 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. This counter shall be reported only for the burst which is started due to the incoming PDCP SDU from the core to the empty PDCP buffer. This means, the counter is not reported for the burst in the below scenarios:

(i) burst initiated due to the transition of the bearer state from INACTIVE to ACTIVE.

(ii) burst consisiting of PDCP PDU retransmission after the intra-gNB HO.

(iii) burst consisting of sending of forwarded PDCP PDUs/SDUs to DU.

1. Counter DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB is updated as the retention delay expiry timepoint and the reception timestamp of the first SDU in the burst.
2. Counter is reported in microsecond, but average delay per DL INIT Scheduling delay(DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB/DL\_INIT\_BURST\_PDCP) should be reported in miliseconds. For this purpose it shall be rounded down the value to the nearest millisecond.
3. Due to limited possibilities of counting the initial burst scheduling delay at the L2Hi level, the value oof those counters will never exceed the value of the retention delay timer.

[End CNI-112795]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-12.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11238737`)

PM Counters
PMQAP Level

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-5.0-12.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11238743`)

PM Counters
[CNI-112795]

Measurement: PDCP Latency PMQAP Profile

NetAct name: DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB\_PMQAP

PI ID: M55159C00007

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Also refer to 5G\_PM\_1225.

Update time: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Additional info:

1. Burst identification can be found under 5G\_L2\_3062\_replaced([11238113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BN6dvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. PMQAP information can be found under 5G\_L2\_3337\_replaced([11238528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BQ9wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
3. This counter shall be reported only for the burst which is started due to the incoming PDCP SDU from the core to the empty PDCP buffer. This means, the counter is not reported for the burst in the below scenarios:

(i) burst initiated due to the transition of the bearer state from INACTIVE to ACTIVE.

(ii) burst consisiting of PDCP PDU retransmission after the intra-gNB HO.

(iii) burst consisting of sending of forwarded PDCP PDUs/SDUs to DU.

1. Counter DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB\_PMQAP is updated as the retention delay expiry timepoint and the reception timestamp of the first SDU in the burst.
2. Counter is reported in microsecond, but average delay per DL INIT Scheduling delay(DL\_INIT\_SCHD\_DLY\_GNB\_PMQAP/DL\_INIT\_BURST\_PDCP\_PMQAP) should be reported in miliseconds. For this purpose it shall be rounded down the value to the nearest millisecond.
3. Due to limited possibilities of counting the initial burst scheduling delay at the L2Hi level, the value oof those counters will never exceed the value of the retention delay timer.

[End CNI-112795]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11238754`)

PM Counters
RoHC decompressed headers

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-6.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12678903`)

PM Counters
During packet processing 5G-L2-HI shall record successful outcome of ROHC decompression operation by updating following counters:

**M55320C19003 (UL\_NUM\_ROHC\_DECOMP\_HEADER) Total number of RoHC decompressed headers**

**M55320C19004 (UL\_VOL\_ROHC\_DECOMP\_HEADER) Total volume of RoHC decompressed headers**

In case ROHC decompression operation fails resulting in discarding of processed packet, following counters shall be updated:

**M55320C07001 ... 20 (UL\_VOL\_DISC\_OTHER\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) UL PDCP PDU volume discarded due to other causes - QoS Group 01 ... 20 [CB010980-D]if pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf = 0 (QoS) is received via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq refer : [10987189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CB010980-D]**

**M55320C08001 ... 20 (UL\_SDU\_DISC\_OTHER\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) UL PDCP PDUs discarded due to other causes - QoS Group 01 ... 20 [CB010980-D]if pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf = 0 (QoS) is received via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq refer : [10987189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CB010980-D]**

[CB010980-D]

**M55352C00017 (UL\_VOL\_DISC\_OTHER\_PMQAP) UL PDCP PDU volume discarded due to other causes per PMQAP profile, if pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf = 1 (PMQAP) and pmqapProfileList > 0 in PmCountersInfo structure are received via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq refer : [10987189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)**

**M55352C00018 (UL\_SDU\_DISC\_OTHER\_PMQAP) UL PDCP PDUs discarded due to other causes per PMQAP profile, if pdcpAndRlcCountersUpdateConf = 1 (PMQAP) and pmqapProfileList > 0 in PmCountersInfo structure are received via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq refer : [10987189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)**

[End CB010980-D]

**M55320CRD50501 (UL\_PDU\_DISC\_ROHC\_DECOMP\_FAILED) Total number of UL PDCP PDUs discarded due to ROHC decompression failure**

**M55320CRD50502 (UL\_VOL\_DISC\_ROHC\_DECOMP\_FAILED) UL PDCP PDU volume discarded due to ROHC decompression failure**

In case ROHC packet containing piggybacked ROHC feedback is discarded then:

**M55320C07001 ... 20 (UL\_VOL\_DISC\_OTHER\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) UL PDCP PDU volume discarded due to other causes - QoS Group 01 ... 20** shall be incremented by the size of entire UL PDCP PDU\*\*\*\*

**M55320C08001 ... 20 (UL\_SDU\_DISC\_OTHER\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) UL PDCP PDUs discarded due to other causes - QoS Group 01 ... 20 shall be incremented by 1,**

**M55320CRD50501 (UL\_PDU\_DISC\_ROHC\_DECOMP\_FAILED) Total number of UL PDCP PDUs discarded due to ROHC decompression failure shall be incremented by 1,**

**M55320CRD50502 (UL\_VOL\_DISC\_ROHC\_DECOMP\_FAILED) UL PDCP PDU volume discarded due to ROHC decompression failure shall be incremented by the size of entire UL PDCP PDU.**

Details regarding triggers for updating above counters are found in [11230315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Note:

Counters M55320CRD50501, M55320CRD50502 are updated as described in [11224588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_xwAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

Counters M55320C07001 ... 20, M55320C08001 ... 20 are updated as described in [11224588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_xwAvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [11224601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_xwBPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11224619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_xwB_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11238770`)

PM Counters
RoHC compressed headers

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11238777`)

PM Counters
During packet processing 5G-L2-HI shall record successful outcome of ROHC compression operation by updating following counters:

M55320C19001 (DL\_NUM\_ROHC\_COMP\_HEADER) Total number of RoHC compressed headers

M55320C19002 (DL\_VOL\_ROHC\_COMP\_HEADER) Total volume of RoHC compressed headers

In case ROHC compression operation fails resulting in discarding of processed packet, following counters shall be updated:

M55320C03001 ... 20 (DL\_VOL\_DISC\_OTHER\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDU volume discarded due to other causes - QoS Group 01 ... 20

M55320C04001 ... 20 (DL\_SDU\_DISC\_OTHER\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) DL PDCP SDUs discarded due to other causes - QoS Group 01 ... 20

M55320CRD50503 (DL\_SDU\_DISC\_ROHC\_COMP\_FAILED) Total number of DL PDCP SDUs discarded due to compression failure

M55320CRD50504 (DL\_VOL\_DISC\_ROHC\_COMP\_FAILED) DL PDCP SDU volume discarded due to compression failure

In case of context reuse during ROHC compression operation following counter shall be updated:

M55320CRD50505 (DL\_NUM\_ROHC\_CONTEXTS\_REUSED) Total number of ROHC contexts re-used by ROHC Compressor in downlink

Details regarding triggers for updating above counters are found in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6281\_replaced([11230315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11238790`)

PM Counters
VoNR Network Quality

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-7.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11238800`)

PM Counters
[Before CNI-116870]

5G-L2-Hi CU shall update below downlink inactivity period for VoNR counter M55350C09001 ... 10 (DL\_INACT\_VONR\_BIN\_01 ... 10) Distribution of dowlink inactivity for VoNR - Bin 01 ... 10  on:  
- reception of DL PDCP SDU when DL PDCP buffer is empty  
- DRB release

Notes:

1. Downlink PDCP buffer is considered empty when PDCP SDU buffer is empty and the last PDCP PDU has been transmitted toward UE(indicated via "Highest Transmitted PDCP SN" in DDDS).
2. Inactivity between bearer setup and first packet is ignored.
3. In this case buffer means buffer of data available for scheduling.
4. During mobility scenarios, at reception of BearerModifyReq, the Counter shall be updated the same way like at reception of BearerDeleteReq in Source Cell and BearerSetupReq in Target Cell. This statement is valid also in case of Intra-Cell handover, where the Cell ID is not changed.

[CNI-116870]

Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell (PDCPC)

NetAct name: DL\_INACT\_VONR\_BIN\_01 ... DL\_INACT\_VONR\_BIN\_10

PI ID: M55350C09001 ... M55350C09010

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall update this counter at sending RTP packet as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7522\_replaced([11223896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyD33fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Increment value: No additional details compared to NIDD.

Notes:

1. L2HI CU shall ignore inactivity between bearer setup and first RTP DL PDCP PDU packet.
2. L2Hi CU shall consider only RTP packets. All nonRTP packets shall be ignored.
3. During intra-gNB mobility scenarios, at mobility resume, the counter shall be updated the same way as at reception of HiUserCu\_BearerDeleteReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_1044\_replaced([10988261](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Wcojfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in Source Cell and HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_1020\_replaced([10987413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WWh6Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in Target Cell.

[End CNI-116870]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-7.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11238822`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell (PDCPC)

NetAct name: VONR\_DL\_BHIF\_MUTE\_DUR\_BIN1 ... VONR\_DL\_BHIF\_MUTE\_DUR\_BIN11

PI ID: M55350C20034 ... M55350C20044

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: No additional details compared to NIDD.

Increment value: No additional details compared to NIDD.

Notes:

1. If difference between RTP SNs is 0, it means that session is not active and L2Hi shall not update the counters.
2. In case there will be a RTP stream (SSRC) change over the same bearer, L2Hi shall stop measurement for the previous stream and start new measurement for the new RTP stream.
3. L2Hi shall count the packets received from core (over NG-U). Packets from forwarding tunnel over Xn-U shall not be included in the counters.

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `11238860`)

PM Counters
Distribution of estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-7.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11238866`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI increments one of the following counters when Average X2-U PDU Delivery Delay (avgPduDelvDelayXx) is updated after receiving X2-U DDDS (see note2 and note3):

* M55313C22001 (EST\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_01) Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U - Bin 01 if avgPduDelvDelayXx <= 1ms,
* M55313C22002(EST\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_02 Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U - Bin 02if 1ms < avgPduDelvDelayXx <= 2ms,
* M55313C22003EST\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_03) Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U - Bin 03if 2ms < avgPduDelvDelayXx <= 3ms,
* M55313C22004(EST\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_04) Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U - Bin 04if 3ms < avgPduDelvDelayXx <= 5ms,
* M55313C22005(EST\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_05) Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U - Bin 05if 5ms < avgPduDelvDelayXx <= 10ms,
* M55313C22006(EST\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_06) Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U - Bin 06if 10ms < avgPduDelvDelayXx <= 15ms,
* M55313C22007(EST\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_07) Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U - Bin 07if 15ms < avgPduDelvDelayXx <= 20ms,
* M55313C22008(EST\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_08) Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U - Bin 08if 20ms < avgPduDelvDelayXx <= 50ms,
* M55313C22009(EST\_PDU\_DELV\_DELAY\_X2\_BIN\_09) Distribution of Estimated PDU Delivery Delay over X2-U - Bin 09if 50ms < avgPduDelvDelayXx.

5G-L2-HI increments one of the following counters when Average estimated throughput over X2 (avgEstTputXx) is updated after receiving X2-U DDDS (see note2 and note3):

* M55313C23001 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_01) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 01 if avgEstTputXx <= 1Mbps,
* M55313C23002 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_02) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 02 if 1Mbps < avgEstTputXx <= 10Mbps,
* M55313C23003 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_03) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 03 if 10Mbps < avgEstTputXx <= 20Mbps,
* M55313C23004 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_04) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 04 if 20Mbps < avgEstTputXx <= 50Mbps,
* M55313C23005 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_05) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 05 if 50Mbps < avgEstTputXx <= 100Mbps,
* M55313C23006 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_06) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 06 if 100Mbps < avgEstTputXx <= 500Mbps,
* M55313C23007 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_07) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 07 if 500Mbps < avgEstTputXx <= 1Gbps,
* M55313C23008 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_08) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 08 if 1Gbps < avgEstTputXx <= 2Gbps,
* M55313C23009 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_09) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 09 if 2Gbps < avgEstTputXx <= 3Gbps,
* M55313C23010 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_10) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 10 if 3Gbps < avgEstTputXx <= 4Gbps,
* M55313C23011 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_11) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 11 if 4Gbps < avgEstTputXx <= 5Gbps,
* M55313C23012 (EST\_TPUT\_X2\_BIN\_12) Distribution of Estimated throughput over X2-U - Bin 12 if 5Gbps < avgEstTputXx.

Note:

1. This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.
2. M55313C22001 ...09 and M55313C23001...12 counters are deleted for Nokia Flow Control only. There are still working for 3GPP Flow Control.
3. [CB008717-D-UPD004] M55313C22001...09 and M55313C23001...12 counters are related to EN-DC technology only and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user. [End CB008717-D-UPD004]
