**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-7.0-5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11238904`)

PM Counters
[Before CB013554-A]

In case of 3GPP flow control,

PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI shall update below counters:

* M55313C24001 (NUM\_OF\_X2\_DDDS\_RCVD) Number of X2-U DDDS - received by 1 when receiving a X2-U DDDS and M55323C14001 (NUM\_OF\_F1\_DDDS\_RCVD) Number of F1-U DDDS received by 1 when receiving a X2-U DDDS (see note1).
* M55313C25001 ... 6 (DDDS\_PERIOD\_X2\_BIN\_01 ... 6) Distribution of DDDS period over X2-U - Bin 01 ... 6 according to time difference since last X2U DDDS (see note1).
* M55323C15001 ... 6 (DDDS\_PERIOD\_F1\_BIN\_01 ... 6) Distribution of DDDS period over F1-U - Bin 01 ... 6 according to time difference since last F1U DDDS.

NR UP instance of 5G-L2-HI increments:

* M55323C04001…20 (DL\_NUM\_LOST\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Number of NR downlink PDU lost on F1-U interface- QoS Group 01 ... 20 on F1-U interface according to the QoS Group when F1-U DDDS message is received.
* M55313C04001…20 (NUM\_DL\_PDU\_LOST\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Number of NR downlink PDU lost on X2-U interface- QoS Group 01 ... 20 on X2-U interface according to the QoS Group when X2-U DDDS message is received.

Notes:

1. M55313C24001 and M55313C25001...06 and M55313C04001…20 counters are related to EN-DC technology only, and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user.

[CB013554-A] Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline. Please see 5G\_L2\_19325\_replaced([11238910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BUBGfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19326\_replaced([11238923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BUoIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19327\_replaced([11238944](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BUoJfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19328\_replaced([11238955](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BUoJ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19329\_replaced([11238977](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BVPMvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_19330\_replaced([11239008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BVPN_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB013554-A]

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-7.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `11238932`)

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-8.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11239102`)

PM Counters
General information

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-8.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11239108`)

PM Counters
For GTP NG-U Packet Loss Rate, L2Hi shall provide the following counters for NRPMQAP:

1. Number of DL PDCP SDUs that are lost over N3 after being sent by UPF (5G\_L2\_20774\_replaced([11239114](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BV2UvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on missed GTP-U SNs over NG-U
2. Number of DL PDCP SDUs that are received at gNB-CU over N3 in order (5G\_L2\_20776\_replaced([11239124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BWdUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on GTP-U SNs received in order over NG-U
3. Number of DL PDCP SDUs that are received at gNB-CU over N3 out of order (5G\_L2\_20778\_replaced([11239134](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BWdU_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on GTP-U SNs received out of order over NG-U
4. These counters are provided based on GTP-U sequence numbers and are updated only if UPF assigns GTP-U SN sent to gNB over NG-U tunnel. For counter updates L2Hi CU shall consider only packets with QoS and QFI mapped to bearer (due to default bearer may handle more QoS flows) received via HiUserCu\_PduSessionSetupReq:sdapDrbConfiguration:qfiDscpList, 5G\_L2\_IF\_2695\_replaced([10988537](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WfExfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or HiUserCu\_PduSessionModifyReq:sdapConfiguration:toAdd:qfiDscpList, 5G\_L2\_IF\_1740\_replaced([10988645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Wfr2vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If packet will be a G-PDU packet and will have GTP-U SN assigned, L2Hi shall handle it and report it into counters.
5. These counters shall not consider indirect forwarded packets received via Core during incoming inter-gNB NG-based handover.
6. Packet shall be counted as lost when there is a gap in the GTPU SN received in order. Such packet may be later received out of order or never received (really lost). Packet received out of order is also counted as lost. Receiving window for GTPU SN is equal to half range of GTPU SN (32767) so any GTPU SN received out of the receiving window should be considered as out of order (not applicable for starting point of counting, L2Hi shall handle first incoming GTP-U SN as described in 5G\_L2\_21923\_replaced([11233543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3ArH5_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For KPI purpose number of really lost packets may be calculated as: number of lost packets - number of packets received out of order.
7. Packets dropped at reception due to:

- bip overload protection (L2Hi discards packets when it runs out of bip descriptors for events),

- unsupported extension header,

shall be counted in normal way into received in order/out of order counters, but not counted in lost counter to not generate artificial losts (discarded packet is formally received packet; whereas lost is counted as difference between discarded packet and last received in order packet). Cases when packets are dropped at reception like: parsing error (malformed packet), no bearer found for packet (based on TEID), incorrect destination IP address shall not be included in received (in order/out of order) nor lost counter.

Note:

1. Packet Loss Rate KPI = (PDCP\_SDU\_LOST\_N3\_PMQP - PDCP\_SDU\_RCV\_N3\_OUTORD\_CU\_PMQP) / (PDCP\_SDU\_LOST\_N3\_PMQP + PDCP\_SDU\_RCV\_N3\_ORDR\_CU\_PMQP)
2. This KPI will have proper results only if UPF assigns GTP-U SNs per QoS flow for packets sent to gNB over the NG-U tunnel.
3. These counters shall be implemented on SDAP layer (counters are for SA only and SDAP layer shall be configured always for SA bearers) because already on SDAP layer there can be packet drops due to overload protection.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11239146`)

PM Counters
Counters for incoming GTP Packet Loss rate over Xn-U

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11239151`)

PM Counters
General information

---

**4.11.0-9.0-3.0-8.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11239156`)

PM Counters
For GTP Xn-U Packet Loss Rate, L2Hi shall provide the following counters for NRPMQAP:

1. Number of DL PDCP SDUs that are lost over XN during data forwarding (5G\_L2\_20781\_replaced([11239162](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BWdWPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on missed GTP SNs over Xn-U
2. Number of DL PDCP SDUs that are received in order at target gNB-CU during data forwarding over XN (5G\_L2\_20783\_replaced([11239172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BWdWvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on GTP SNs received in order over Xn-U
3. Number of DL PDCP SDUs that are received out of order at target gNB-CU during data forwarding over XN (5G\_L2\_20785\_replaced([11239184](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BWdXPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - based on GTP SNs received out of order over Xn-U
4. These counters are provided based on GTP sequence numbers assigned to GTP-U packets. GTP-U SN field is optional in GTP-U header.

L2Hi CU on source gNB shall assign GTP-U SNs only if actGtpUpSeqNum=TRUE (HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq:pmCountersInfo, 5G\_L2\_IF\_5258\_replaced([10987189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsu_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This flag set to TRUE means that L2Hi CU shall assign GTP SNs (please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28659\_replaced([11225210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyLzqvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for directly and indirectly forwarded packets

(In general, GTP-U SN shall be added to all forwarded packets (with user data):

– for mobility case: no matter if HO is bearer level or PDU session level, direct or indirect, 5G-5G or inter rat or inter vendor,

[CB009884-D-UPD001]

- for NR-DC forwarding case: during PSCell Addition and Bearer takeback (only DRB level forwarding is supported, please see the Note no.6)

[End CB009884-D-UPD001]).

Data packets (GTPU carrying PDCP SDU) shall always contain GTPU-SN once flag for this function is activated. Counters shall be updated by L2Hi CU on target gNB during inter-gNB Xn-U based handover only if GTP-U SN will be present in GTP-U packets.

L2Hi CU should not get duplicated GTP-SN on any interface since there is no retx concept on GTP-U (if duplicated GTP-U SN will appear, L2Hi shall accept that packet, and repeated sequence number shall be counted as out of order). GTP-U SN should be assigned only for G-PDU packets with DUD extension header and PDCP Data PDUs (so with non-zero payload). In case of pure polling (DUD without DL data packet) and GTP-U control PDUs (like SEHN, Error Indication, Tunnel Status, End Marker), GTP-U SN shall not be assigned. If packet will be a G-PDU packet and will have GTP-U SN assigned, L2Hi shall handle it and report it into counters.

* In case of DRB level forwarding (direct or indirect) separate GTP-U SN should be kept per bearer. In case of PDU session level forwarding (direct or indirect) separate GTP-U SN should be kept per QoS flow. During PDU session level forwarding L2HI CU shall assign GTP-U SN only for packets with QFI mapped to bearer - for this reason L2Hi CU shall obtain QFI via HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq:qos:mapping (5G\_L2\_IF\_7237\_replaced([10987916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WaMSPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to assign GTP-U SN on source. This is because default bearer may handle more QoS flows, received via HiUserCu\_PduSessionSetupReq:ReqSdapDrbConfiguration:QfiDscpPair (5G\_L2\_IF\_3158\_replaced([10989090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WjWNPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or HiUserCu\_PduSessionModifyReq:SdapConfiguration:ReqSdapDrbConfiguration:QfiDscpPair (5G\_L2\_IF\_1740\_replaced([10988645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Wfr2vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* These counters shall count only DRB and PDU session level direct forwarded GTP-U packets (5G\_UP\_6929\_replaced([11365103](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udPehvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Indirect forwarded packets shall be excluded from counters. In case of DRB level forwarding, L2Hi CU shall obtain the information about direct forwarding (over Xn-U) from Cplane via HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq:PmCountersInfo:HandoverType (5G\_L2\_IF\_7194\_replaced([10992815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2W6ilPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), where value xnBasedInterGnbHo means that forwarding is direct. In case of PDU session level forwarding, L2Hi CU shall obtain the information about direct forwarding (over Xn-U) from Cplane via HiUserCu\_PduSessionSetupReq:ForwardingInfo:HandoverType (5G\_L2\_IF\_7194\_replaced([10992815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2W6ilPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), where value xnBasedInterGnbHo means that forwarding is direct.
* Packet shall be counted as lost when there is a gap in the GTPU SN received in order. Such packet may be later received out of order or never received (really lost). Packet received out of order is also counted as lost. Receiving window for GTPU SN is equal to half range of GTPU SN (32767) so any GTPU SN received out of the receiving window should be considered as out of order (not applicable for starting point of counting, L2Hi shall handle first incoming GTP-U SN as described in 5G\_L2\_21923\_replaced([11233543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3ArH5_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For KPI purpose number of really lost packets may be calculated as: number of lost packets - number of packets received out of order.
* Packets dropped at reception due to:

- bip overload protection (L2Hi discards packets when it runs out of bip descriptors for events),

- unsupported extension header,

shall be counted in normal way into received in order/out of order counters, but not counted in lost counter to not generate artificial losts (discarded packet is formally received packet; whereas lost is counted as difference between discarded packet and last received in order packet). Cases when packets are dropped at reception like: parsing error (malformed packet), no bearer found for packet (based on TEID), incorrect destination IP address shall not be included in received (in order/out of order) nor lost counter.

Notes:

1. Packet Loss Rate KPI = (PDCP\_SDU\_LOST\_XN\_PMQP - PDCP\_SDU\_RCV\_XN\_OUTORD\_CU\_PMQP) / (PDCP\_SDU\_LOST\_XN\_PMQP + PDCP\_SDU\_RCV\_XN\_ORDR\_CU\_PMQP)
2. This KPI will have proper results in target gNB only if source gNB has activated actGtpUpSeqNum and GTP-U SNs are kept per bearer for DRB level forwarding and per QoS Flow (for packets with QoS mapped to bearers only) for PDU session level forwarding during inter-gNB XN-based handover.
3. For PDU session level forwarding GTP-U SN should be assigned per QoS Flow and only for packets with QFI mapped to bearer. QFI of packet should be included in forwarded packet. If QFI to DRB mapping is different on target gNB and given QoS is not mapped to any DRB - then it will be handled by default DRB and counters for GTP Xn-U Packet Loss Rate will not be updated for these packets. On target, for default DRB, counters will be updated only for packets with QFI mapped to bearer.
4. These counters shall be implemented:
5. on SDAP layer for PDU session level forwarding (counters are for SA only and SDAP layer shall be configured always for SA bearers) because already on SDAP layer there can be packet drops due to overload protection,
6. and on PDCP layer for bearer level forwarding.

[CB009884-D-UPD001]

1. Target L2Hi will know if packet is NRDC forwarded during PSCell Addition or Bearer Takeback via HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq:pmCounterInfo:handoverType=nrdcRelocation (5G\_L2\_IF\_7194\_replaced([10992815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2W6ilPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End CB009884-D-UPD001]

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-1.0-2.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `12483689`)

PM Counters
Measurement: PDCP Latency PMQAP Profile

NetAct name: DC\_GBR\_UL\_PDCP\_SDU\_LATE\_PMQP

PI ID: M55159C00014

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Update time: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Note: Bearer is DC-GBR bearer if HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq/Qos/Mapping/resourceType IE is set to dcGBR. MDBV and GFBR compliance information of PDCP PDU is included in GTP-U Extension header/ GbrAssistanceInformationData. [PR841971] GFBR compliance information of PDCP PDU from GTP-U Extension header may be overwitten if the size of UL PDCP SDU exceeds DcGbrPmCounterParams.ulMdbv value (in this case packed is marked as non-compliant). [End PR841971] UL PDCP PDU is sent not within PDB if UL packet delay > ulRanPdb.

If L2-LO does not include DcGbrSchedInfo in LoData\_UlRlcPduReceiveInd (meaning if UL RLC PDU is GFRB and MDBV complaint or non-compliant) for DC-GBR, the packet is treated as non-compliant.

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11239399`)

PM Counters
Data volume over NG-U data tunnel

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-1.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13480749`)

PM Counters
[Before CB015891-E]

For each UL PDCP SDU (before excluding SDAP header and sending SDAP SDU over NR NG-U GTP-U tunnel), PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI sums up the total data volume for respective SA Bearer-QoS group and updates the appropriate counter:

**M55327C04001 ... 20 (UL\_PDCP\_VOL\_SNT\_NGU\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Uplink data volume sent over NG-U UL GTP-U tunnel - QoS Group 01 ... 20**

Note:

The SA Bearer-QoS group value is received in the Bearer Setup (see qciCounterGroup in 5G\_L2\_IF\_1020\_replaced([10987413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WWh6Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6281\_replaced([11230315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed definitions (including units) of PM Counters updated by 5G-L2-HI.18066

**Duration of the measurement period for the NR NG U Interface Report**

##### See (lack of req number)

[CB015891-E]

Measurement: NR NG-U Interface Report

NetAct name: UL\_PDCP\_VOL\_SNT\_NGU\_QOS\_G\_01 ... UL\_PDCP\_VOL\_SNT\_NGU\_QOS\_G\_20

PI ID: M55327C04001 ... M55327C04020

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall update these counters for each UL PDCP SDU (before excluding the SDAP header) sent over NG-U UL GTP-U tunnel.

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment these counters by the uplink data volume for a respective SA Bearer-QoS group. The volume is the size of the UL PDCP SDU in Bytes, measured before excluding the SDAP header. BOAM shall convert the reported value to kB.

[End CB015891-E]

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11239411`)

PM Counters
Data volume per PLMN-ID

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-1.0-3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13478992`)

PM Counters
[Before CB015891-E]

5G-L2-HI (PDCP) shall increment the following counters provided PDCP SDU user UL data volume per PLMN-ID for the given QoS Group.:

**M55326C03001 ... 20 (PDCP\_VOL\_UL\_PLMN\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) PDCP SDU user UL data volume per PLMN-ID - QoS Group 01 ... 20**

[CB015891-E]

Measurement: NR RAN Sharing UP (NRASU)

NetAct name: PDCP\_VOL\_UL\_PLMN\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... PDCP\_VOL\_UL\_PLMN\_QOS\_GRP\_20

PI ID: M55326C03001 ... M55326C03020

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_5KBG5p5DEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall update this counter upon reception of a PDCP SDU containing user UL data per PLMN-ID for the given QoS Group.

Increment value: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment this counter by the size of the received PDCP SDU in Bytes. The value is measured for user UL data per PLMN-ID for the given QoS Group. BOAM shall convert the reported value to kB.

[End CB015891-E]

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-1.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `12689683`)

PM Counters
Max UL Cell throughput in PDCP layer

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-1.0-3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12689684`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell (PDCPC)  
NetAct name: PDCP\_SDU\_CELL\_THP\_UL\_MAX  
PI ID: M55350C00069  
Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 11192143: PM Counter Search in NIDD.

Update time:

If NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount has "PDCP SDU Cell level peak throughput PM Counters" selected (i.e.,Bit 2: PDCPSDUPEAKTHPUT is set in HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount), 5G-L2-HI CU shall sample every 1 sec the cumulative received UL PDCP SDU volume of all DRBs in NRCELL and report the maximum value from all samples during the measurement period.

Increment value:

5G-L2-HI (CU) shall compute cumulative received UL PDCP SDU volume of all DRBs in NRCELL during sampling interval of 1 sec, compares against cumulated UL PDCP SDU volume computed in previous sampling interval of 1 sec and updates if current value is bigger than previous value.

Additional Information:

1. In case of online modification of NRBTS.NRPMRNL.NRPMCCP.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount to select or deselect  "PDCP SDU Cell level peak throughput PM Counters" then 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall consider new value of Bit 2: PDCPSDUPEAKTHPUT in HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq.PmCountersInfo.actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount immediately from the next sampling interval.

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-1.0-5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11239481`)

PM Counters

M55328C00007 (PDCP\_SDU\_DELAY\_UL\_SLICE) UL PDCP SDU delay per Slice per PLMN

NOTE: The delay for PDCP SDU is calculated as time difference between reception of UL PDCP PDU from RLC layer, and when the PDCP SDU is sent towards NG-U.

Note that average delay can be received using UL PDCP SDU amount counters:

"M55328C00004: UL PDCP SDUs transmitted per Slice per PLMN "

[CB008828-A] In case when slices extension feature is enabled, this slice based counter should not be updated. [End CB008828-A]

PM Counters

M55319C10001 ... 20 (UL\_DELAY\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) UL PDCP SDU delay - QoS Group 01 ... 20

NOTE: The delay for PDCP SDU is calculated as time difference between "the reception of the UL PDCP PDU from RLC layer in either gNB or eNB", and "UL PDCP SDU is sent towards S1 or NG-U".

Note that average delay can be obtained using SDU amount counters:

"UL PDCP SDUs received for NSA Bearer - QoS Group 01".

+

"UL PDCP SDUs received for SA Bearer - QoS Group 01".

2. Counters are reported in microsecond, but average delay per UL PDCP SDU (UL\_PDCP\_SDU\_DLY\_CUUP/UL\_PDCP\_SDU\_SENT\_SAP\_TOT) should be reported in miliseconds. For this purpose it shall be rounded down the value to the nearest millisecond.

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11239619`)

PM Counters
Over F1-U

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11239630`)

PM Counters
[Before CB013554-A]

Number of uplink PDCP PDU received over F1-U -  QoS Group

PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI increments the M55323C02001 ... 20 (UL\_NUM\_RCV\_F1\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Number of uplink PDCP PDU received over F1-U - QoS Group 1 counters with the number of UL PDCP PDUs received over F1-U according to the QoS group.

Uplink data volume received over F1-U - QoS Group

PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI increments M55323C03001 ....20 (UL\_VOL\_RCV\_F1\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Uplink data volume received over F1-U - QoS Group 1 ... 20 with the number of kilobytes of UL PDCP PDUs received over F1-U according to the QoS Group .

Min/Max Uplink data volume received over F1-U in sample time- QoS Group

PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI also updates sample counters of Max and Min data volume received over F1-U UL,

M55323C09001...20 (MAX\_UL\_RCV\_F1\_QoS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Max Uplink data volume received over F1-U in sample time- QoS Group 1 ... 20

and M55323C10001...20 (MIN\_UL\_RCV\_F1\_QoS\_GRP\_01) Min Uplink data volume received over F1-U in sample time- QoS Group 1 ...20

according to the QoS group every 1s.

The QoS group value is received in the Bearer Setup.

Duration of the measurement period for the CU NRF1U report

##### PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI increments: M55323C13001 (MEAS\_PERIOD\_NR\_F1\_CU\_REPORT) Duration of the measurement period for the CU NRF1U report

##### by 1 every 1s.

##### Counters of UL PDCP SDUs received over F1-U for the respective StandAlone Bearer QoS group

Number of received UL PDCP SDUs

For each UL PDCP SDU received from RLC layer through F1-U interface, the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI (CU) updates the number of the packets received for a respective SA Bearer-QoS group, by incrementing the appropriate counter:

M55319C15001 ... 20 (UL\_SDU\_RX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) UL PDCP SDUs received for SA Bearer - QoS Group 01 ... 20

Note: Discarded UL PDCP SDUs are not counted.

Data volume of received UL PDCP SDUs

For each UL PDCP SDU received from RLC layer through F1-U interface, the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI (CU) sums up the total data volume of the packets received for a respective SA Bearer-QoS group and updates the appropriate counter:

M55319C16001 ... 20 (UL\_VOL\_RX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) UL PDCP SDU volume received for SA Bearer - QoS Group 01 ... 20

Note: Discarded UL PDCP SDUs are not counted.

Maximum data volume of received UL PDCP SDU

Every 1s the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI (CU) calculates the volume of data of the packets received for the respective SA Bearer-QoS group. If the value is bigger than for the previous sample, the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI (CU) updates the appropriate counter:

M55319C17001 ... 20 (MAX\_UL\_VOL\_RX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Max UL PDCP SDU volume received for SA Bearer in sample time - QoS Group 01 ... 20

Minimum data volume of received UL PDCP SDU

Every 1s the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI (CU) calculates the volume of data of received packets for respective SA Bearer-QoS group. If the value is smaller for than the previous sample, the PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI updates the appropriate counter:

M55319C18001 ... 20 (MIN\_UL\_VOL\_RX\_SA\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Min UL PDCP SDU volume received for SA Bearer in sample time - QoS Group 01 ... 20

Note:

The SA Bearer-QoS group value is received in the Bearer Setup (see qciCounterGroup in 5G\_L2\_IF\_1020\_replaced([10987413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WWh6Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6281\_replaced([11230315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed definitions (including units) of PM Counters updated by 5G-L2-HI.

[CB013554-A] Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline.Please see 5G\_L2\_19168\_replaced([11239687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BaHt_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19169\_replaced([11239713](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BaHvPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19170\_replaced([11239739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BauwfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19171\_replaced([11239754](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BauxPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19172\_replaced([11239769](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Baux_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19173\_replaced([11239783](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BauyvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19174\_replaced([11239797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BauzfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19175\_replaced([11239814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BbV0fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_19176\_replaced([11239830](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BbV1PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).   [End CB013554-A]

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11239664`)

PM Counters
[Before CB013554-A]

PDCP PDU received NR X2-U UL GTP-U tunnel - QoS Group

PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI increments:

M55313C12001…20 (UL\_PDCP\_NUM\_RCV\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Number of uplink PDCP PDU received NR X2-U UL GTP-U tunnel - QoS Group 01 .. .20, according to the QoS group, with the number of UL PDCP PDUs received over X2-U (see note2).

Number of DL PDCP PDU sent over NR X2-U DL GTP-U tunnel - QoS Group

PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI increments:

* M55313C13001…20 (DL\_PDCP\_NUM\_SNT\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Number of DL PDCP PDU sent over NR X2-U DL GTP-U tunnel - QoS Group 01...20, according to the QoS group, with the number of kilobytes of UL PDCP PDUs received over X2-U (see note1 and note2)

Data volume received over X2-U UL GTP-U tunnel in the sample

Every sample period (1 second) PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI increments:

* M55313C19001…20 (MAX\_UL\_PDCP\_RCV\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Max data volume received over X2-U UL GTP-U tunnel in the sample time- QoS Group 0 1... 20
* M55313C20001…20 (MIN\_UL\_PDCP\_RCV\_X2\_QOS\_GRP\_01 ... 20) Min data volume received over X2-U UL GTP-U tunnel in the sample time- QoS Group 01 ... 20 counters,

according to the QoS group, with the number of kilobytes of UL PDCP PDUs received over X2-U during sample period, M55313C21001 (MEAS\_PERIOD\_NR\_X2\_REPORT) Duration of the measurement period for the NRX2U report.

Notes:

1. M55313C13001…20 counters are deleted for Nokia Flow Control only. There are still working for 3GPP Flow Control
2. M55313C12001…20 and M55313C13001…20 counters are related to EN-DC technology only and should not be updated over secondary link (SCG F1-U) by NR-DC user.

[CB013554-A] Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline.Please see 5G\_L2\_19212\_replaced([11239847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BbV1_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19213\_replaced([11239876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BbV3PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19214\_replaced([11239900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Bb84fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L2\_19215\_replaced([11239914](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Bb85PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_19216\_replaced([11239930](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Bb85_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB013554-A]

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-10.0-1.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13384160`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI CU shall execute below things:

1. If list of PMQAP Profiles with actUlPdcpPduDistCounters = TRUE is not changed from previous context, then 5G-L2-HI CU shall not take any action.

2. If list of PMQAP Profiles with actUlPdcpPduDistCounters = TRUE is changed from previous context, then  
        a. For each existing non-GBR Bearer in monitoring list for which PMQAP Level counter (defined in [13350628: UL PDCP PDU data volume distribution PMQAP counters](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_qoLK1uu9EfCnwLcpJWh_Zw)) is                    being pegged for the removed PMQAP profiles, 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report accumulated UL volume at PMQAP Level at the end of the measurement interval for these                        removed PMQAP profiles and not update further at PMQAP Level for removed profiles.

1. For each existing non-GBR Bearer in monitoring list (for which Cell Level counter defined in [12480376: Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell(PDCPC)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_5hvX4A7WEfCvOvZoOJBSnQ) is already being pegged):

a. 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall report accumulated UL volume at Cell Level at the end of the measurement interval and not update further at Cell Level.

b. Remove from monitoring list if there is no matching designated PMQAP Profile.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-10.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13382705`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell(PDCPC)

NetAct name: UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN1...UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN20

PI ID: M55350C00048...M55350C00067

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in [11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Update time: Updated every sampling interval(100ms) with the received UL PDCP PDU DRB volume at PDCP from RLC layer.

* M55350C00048 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 0 Byte < x < 1 kByte,
* M55350C00049 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 1 kByte <= x < 2 kByte,
* M55350C00050 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 2 kByte <= x < 5 kByte,
* M55350C00051 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 5 kByte <= x < 10 kByte,
* M55350C00052 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 10 kByte <= x < 20 kByte,
* M55350C00053 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 20 kByte <= x < 50 kByte,
* M55350C00054 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 50 kByte <= x < 100 kByte,
* M55350C00055 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 100 kByte <= x < 200 kByte,
* M55350C00056 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 200 kByte <= x < 500 kByte,
* M55350C00057 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 500 kByte <= x < 1 MByte,
* M55350C00058 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 1 MByte <= x < 1.5 MByte,
* M55350C00059 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 1.5 MByte <= x < 2 MByte,
* M55350C00060 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 2 MByte <= x < 2.5 MByte,
* M55350C00061 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 2.5 MByte <= x < 3 MByte,
* M55350C00062 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 3 MByte <= x < 3.5 MByte,
* M55350C00063 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 3.5 MByte <= x < 4 MByte,
* M55350C00064 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 4 MByte <= x < 4.5 MByte,
* M55350C00065 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 4.5 MByte <= x < 5 MByte,
* M55350C00066 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 5 MByte <= x < 10 MByte,
* M55350C00067 if the UL PDCP PDU DRB volume calculated on a sampling interval is within the range 10 MByte <= x.

Note : UL PDCP PDU for non-GBR DRB only is considered for the counter update.

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Additional Note :

1. 5G-L2-HI CU shall add the non-GBR bearer to the monitoring list upon the reception of HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq(Refer : [10987302](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WV60vu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) or HiUserCu\_BearerModifyReq(Refer : [10987931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WaMS_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) with Cause:SetActive if the current number of monitored bearers(after considering the current bearer) is less than countersMaxDrb [CB0109080-C-UPD001]and actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount = xxxxxxx1(LSB is set)[End CB010980-C-UPD001](received in HiCnfgCu_ConfigParamReq refer [10986933](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WS3h_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
2. Updating the counter during CPU overload is as defined in [11229083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymDVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), [11229095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymDVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), [11229108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymDWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
3. Any change in counterMaxDrb shall be considered only from the next sampling interval.
4. If the countersMaxDrb is modified(indicated via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq ) to a lower value than the current DRB monitored list [CB010980-C-UPD001]and actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount = xxxxxxx1(LSB is set)[End CB010980-C-UPD001], then 5G-L2-HI CU shall remove the monitored DRBs from the list to match the new value of countersMaxDrb from the next sampling interval.
5. 5G-L2-HI CU shall remove the DRB from the monitoring list if the DRB is suspended due to the transition of UE to RRC INACTIVE state. As the suspended bearer does not carry any traffic, this is removed from the monitoring list to impact the counter measurement.
6. Once the non-GBR DRB is added to the monitoring list, it shall be monitored continuously except for the conditions below:
7. CPU load exceeds the critical threshold value
8. bearer is suspended due to RRC INACTIVE transition of UE
9. bearer is released[CB010980-C-UPD001]
10. actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount = xxxxxxx0(LSB is reset).[End CB010980-C-UPD001]
11. 5G-L2-HI CU shall update the counter with the UL volume of the non-GBR bearer before it is removed from the bearerMonitoringList  for the reasons [CB010980-C-UPD001]a, b and c[End CB010980-C-UPD001] mentioned in Step 6.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-10.0-3**  (ID: `13350628`)

PM Counters
UL PDCP PDU data volume distribution PMQAP counters

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-10.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13350629`)

PM Counters
Measurement: PDCP Cell NRPMQAP2 (PDCPQ2)

NetAct name: UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN1\_PMQP... UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN10\_PMQP

PI ID: M55403C00001... M55403C00010

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 11192143.

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall increment one of these BIN counters UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN1\_PMQP... UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN10\_PMQP by 1, if received UL PDCP PDU DRB volume at PDCP from RLC is within the respective counter BIN range.   
Note: UL PDCP PDU for non-GBR DRB only is considered for this counter update.

Increment value: No additional details as compared to NIDD.

Additional Note:   
1.    BIN range is defined as below:

* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN1\_PMQP is 0 Byte < x < 2 kByte.
* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN2\_PMQP is 2 kByte <= x < 10 kByte.
* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN3\_PMQP is 10 kByte <= x < 50 kByte.
* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN4\_PMQP is 50 kByte <= x < 200 kByte.
* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN5\_PMQP is 200 kByte <= x < 1 MByte.
* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN6\_PMQP is 1 MByte <= x < 2 MByte.
* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN7\_PMQP is 2 MByte <= x < 3 MByte.
* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN8\_PMQP is 3 MByte <= x < 4 MByte.
* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN9\_PMQP is 4 MByte <= x < 5 MByte.
* BIN range for UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_DRB\_VOL\_BIN10\_PMQP is >= 5 Mbyte

2.    Updating these counters during CPU overload is as defined in

* [11229083: Actions when CPU load is below Non-critical CPU Load Threshold and above Normal CPU Load Threshold](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymDVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* [11229095: Actions when CPU load is above Non-critical CPU Load Threshold but below Critical CPU load threshold](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymDVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* [11229108: Actions when CPU load is above Critical CPU Load Threshold](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymDWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* [12343554: Actions when CPU load reduces below Normal CPU Load Threshold](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8e28oQSLEfCJ0Mh_3UUzdQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

3.    Any change in counterMaxDrb shall be considered only from the next sampling interval.

4.    If the countersMaxDrb is modified(indicated via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq ) to a lower value than the current DRB monitored list, and            actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount =  xxxxxxx1(LSB is set) or some PMQAP profiles with actUlPdcpPduDistCounters = TRUE, then 5G-L2-HI CU shall remove the monitored DRBs from the list in below priority order to match the new value of countersMaxDrb from the next sampling interval.

a.    Random monitored bearers that are not part of any designated PMQAP profiles  
b.    Random monitored bearers that are part of any designated PMQAP profiles.

5.    5G-L2-HI CU shall remove the DRB from the monitoring list if the DRB is suspended due to the transition of UE to RRC INACTIVE state as the suspended      bearer does not carry any traffic, this is removed from the monitoring list to impact the counter measurement.

6.    Once the non-GBR DRB is added to the monitoring list, it shall be monitored continuously except for the conditions below:

* a.    CPU load exceeds the critical threshold value
* b.    bearer is suspended due to RRC INACTIVE transition of UE
* c.    bearer is released
* d.    actPdcpAndRlcMeasCount = xxxxxxx0(LSB is unset) and also there are no matching PMQAP profiles with actUlPdcpPduDistCounters = TRUE

7.    5G-L2-HI CU shall update the counter with the UL volume of the non-GBR bearer at PMQAP level before it is removed from the bearerMonitoringList for the      reasons a, b and c mentioned in Step 6

---

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11240022`)

PM Counters
UL F1-U Packet Loss Rate

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11240027`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-Hi CU shall update below uplink F1-U packet Loss rate counters:

 Number of uplink PDCP PDUs over F1-U (UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_F1\_PMQAP) (M55362C00001)

 Number of uplink PDCP PDUs lost over F1-U (UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_LOST\_F1\_PMQAP) (M55362C00002)

per each configured PMQAP profile.

Note:

1) 5G-L2-Hi shall update counters only when the sequence number is included in the GTP-U header.

2) 5G-L2-Hi DU adds GTP sequence numbers in uplink only for User Plane traffic, not for DDDS message. In case of multivendor environment if other vendor DU have enabled sequence number for DDDS message, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall count such sequence number in those counters.

3) For M55362C00002, 5G-L2-Hi shall not count as lost UL GTP sequence numbers which are received out of order but evaluated as successfully received.

PM Counters

 Number of uplink PDCP PDUs over X2-U (UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_X2\_PMQAP) (M55364C00001)

 Number of uplink PDCP PDUs lost over X2-U (UL\_PDCP\_PDU\_LOST\_X2\_PMQAP) (M55364C00002)

per each configured PMQAP profile.

Note:

1) 5G-L2-Hi shall update counters only when the sequence number is included in the GTP-U header.

2) eNB adds GTP sequence numbers in uplink only for User Plane traffic, not for DDDS message. In case of multivendor environment if other vendor eNB have enabled sequence number for DDDS message, 5G-L2-Hi CU shall count such sequence number in those counters.

3) For M55361C00002, 5G-L2-Hi shall not count as lost UL GTP sequence numbers which are received out of order but evaluated as successfully received.

[Before CNI-134375-F]

Measurement: Spare counters per NRBTS level (SCBTS)

NetAct name: GNB\_SUM\_M55900C6

PI ID: M55900C00006

Update time: This counter is updated when a PDCP UL PDU is discarded due to the following reasons:  
                    - A PDCP PDU, which is outside the re-ordering window  
                    - A PDCP PDU, which is duplicated (received during lower layer re-establishment)

Increment value: Incremented by 1 each time PDCP PDU is discarded due to above reasons.

Note:

1. This spare counter is activated in 24R3 and 25R1 releases. It will be replaced by UL\_PDU\_DISC\_SN\_OUT\_ WNDW\_OR\_DUP from 25R2 release onwards.
2. PM counter definition can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

PI ID: M55320C00004

Update time: This counter is updated when a PDCP UL PDU is discarded due to the following reasons:  
                    - A PDCP PDU, which is outside the re-ordering window  
                    - A PDCP PDU, which is duplicated (received during lower layer re-establishment)

Increment value: Incremented by 1 each time PDCP PDU is discarded due to above reasons.

Note:

1. PM counter definition can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11240089`)

PM Counters
[Before CNI-116870]

5G-L2-Hi CU shall update below uplink inactivity period for VoNR counter:   
M55350C10001... 10 (UL\_INACT\_VONR\_BIN\_01 ... 10) Distribution of uplink inactivity for VoNR - BIN 01 ... 10

on:  
- reception of UL PDCP PDU  
- DRB release

Note:

1. Inactivity between bearer setup and first packet is ignored.
2. During mobility scenarios, at reception of BearerModifyReq, the Counter shall be updated the same way like at reception of BearerDeleteReq in Source Cell and BearerSetupReq in Target Cell. This statement is valid also in case of Intra-Cell handover, where the Cell ID is not changed.

[CNI-116870]

Measurement: NR PDCP Report Cell (PDCPC)

NetAct name: UL\_INACT\_VONR\_BIN\_01 ... UL\_INACT\_VONR\_BIN\_10

PI ID: M55350C10001 ... M55350C10010

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: 5G-L2-HI (CU) shall update this counter at sending RTP packet as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7522\_replaced([11223896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyD33fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Increment value: No additional details compared to NIDD.

Notes:

1. L2Hi CU shall ignore inactivity between bearer setup and first RTP UL PDCP SDU packet.
2. L2Hi CU shall consider only RTP packets. All nonRTP packets shall be ignored.
3. During intra-gNB mobility scenarios, at mobility resume, the counter shall be updated the same way as at reception of HiUserCu\_BearerDeleteReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_1044\_replaced([10988261](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Wcojfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in Source Cell and HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq (5G\_L2\_IF\_1020\_replaced([10987413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WWh6Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in Target Cell.

[End CNI-116870]

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11240182`)

PM Counters
Integrity Protection failures in SA mode

---

**4.11.0-9.0-4.0-3.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11240188`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-Hi CU shall update below integrity protection failure counter in SA mode:

M55350C00031 (INTEGRITY\_VERIF\_FAIL\_DRB\_SA) - Number of times integrity verification fails for SA DRBs for the cell.

Note:

1. Integrity Protection failure is detected when the number of consecutive PDCP PDU discards due to integrity failure are more than rdNumOfConsecutiveDrbIpFailures as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12024\_replaced([11223779](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyDQyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**4.11.0-9.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12566138`)

**Activation of DPI measurements**

---

**4.11.0-9.0-6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12566140`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI (CU) shall follow procedure for DPI monitoring as per [11228713](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyjnHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

DPI parameters are delivered to 5G-L2-HI (CU) upon reception of HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq--PmCountersInfo--[DpiMeasurementsParams](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUFpvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ) structure.

5G-L2-HI shall enable DPI monitoring for the DRB based on activation parameter(s) which are set to true under [DpiMeasurements](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WXwBPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ) structure via HiUserCu\_BearerSetupReq and conditions from [11228742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kykOIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) are fulfilled.

Counters for DL - [12484148](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_N3TckQ-4EfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

Counters for UL - [12484459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI__OsbIw-8EfCvOvZoOJBSnQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

**4.11.0-9.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `12566141`)

PM Counters
Online modification of DPI parameters

---

**4.11.0-9.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12566143`)

PM Counters
In case of online modification of any DPI parameter (see Note) when feature is activated (refer [12566138](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_R6YuqSvfEfCNjfqfyUlvmw)), all the DRBs and TCP Flow contexts selected for DPI measurements are stopped and PM counters are collected. Only new DRBs are eligible for DPI (see Rationale).

Rationale:

During intermediate period of counter collection (when online modification happened), counters might contain not valid information due to change in DPI calculations.

Note:

Parameters are modified online upon reception of consecutive HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq--PmCountersInfo--[DpiMeasurementsParams](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUFpvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ) structure with updated IE(s) value(s).

**4.11.0-9.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `12656943`)

PM Counters
Active/Inactive time calculation

---

**4.11.0-9.0-6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12656944`)

PM Counters
Requirement refers to [1122881](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kykOO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

When a new TCP ACK packet is received, 5G-L2-HI shall calculate the time difference between this packet and the previous TCP packet for each DRB. This time difference shall be recorded and in case calculated value is greater or equal to dpiInactivityDetectionTime, then 5G-L2-HI shall sum the TCP volume for the given burst associated with that DRB and store the result internally.

When the summed TCP volume for a burst is less than dpiMinTrafficVolThreshold, then 5G-L2-HI shall exclude this burst from the goodput calculation and increment the Inactive Time by the duration of the excluded burst.

See attached graph below for an example of volume burst detection and Active Time calculation (v1,v2,v3 - volume of transfer in each TCP flow for given DRB):

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating different states of a data transmission process, labeled "DRB". The diagram shows three vertical lines representing "v1", "v2", and "v3", which appear to be different channels or streams. These lines are segmented into colored blocks, green indicating "active" periods and white indicating "inactive" periods within those streams.
The diagram is laid out along a horizontal timeline, starting with "DPI start" and ending with "DPI stop". The timeline is divided into alternating "Active Time" and "Inactive Time" segments.
Several annotations are present:
\* **"volume burst >dpiMinTrafficVolThreshol"**: This annotation points to a section of green blocks, indicating a period of high traffic volume.
\* **"< dpilnactivityDetection Time"**: This annotation points to the transition from an "Active Time" to an "Inactive Time" segment, suggesting that if the inactivity detection time is less than this threshold, the state remains active.
\* **"short volume burst = dpilnactivityDetection Time"**: This annotation points to the transition from an "Inactive Time" to an "Active Time" segment, suggesting that if the inactivity detection time is greater than or equal to this threshold, the state becomes inactive.
The diagram visually represents how the system transitions between active and inactive states based on traffic volume and inactivity detection time. The green blocks represent periods where traffic is present and the system is considered active. The white blocks represent periods of no traffic within a stream. The red blocks, specifically in the "short volume burst" section, indicate a different type of event where traffic is present but below a certain threshold, leading to an inactive state. The overall timeline shows a cyclical pattern of active and inactive periods.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/bursts.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Note:

dpiMinTrafficVolThreshold and dpiInactivityDetectionTime are received via HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq--PmCountersInfo--DpiMeasurementsParams--[DpiGoodputParams](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUFqPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ) structure.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `13421220`)

PM Counters
Creation of TCP Flow Context

---

**4.11.0-9.0-6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13421221`)

PM Counters
Requirement refers to [11228769](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kykOLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

5G-L2-HI CU shall use a 5-tuple TcpFlowKey to uniquely identify TCP flow contexts.

The TcpFlowKey shall be composed of:

* bearerIndex
* Source IP Address
* Destination IP Address
* Source TCP Port
* Destination TCP Port

Each unique 5-tuple TcpFlowKey shall map to a separate TCP Flow Context, ensuring independent contexts for each DRB, even when multiple DRBs carry the same TCP flow (identical 4-tuple values).

Rationale:

Due to protocol layer misconfigurations or specific network scenarios, it is possible that a TCP flow (identified by the same 4-tuple) may be carried by 2 or more DRBs within the same 5G-L2-HI instance.

Without bearerIndex in the key composition, such DRBs would produce identical TcpFlowKey values and incorrectly share the same TCP Flow Context. Although these DRBs would still have DPI enabled and perform measurements, counter values would be completely inaccurate. Note when DRBs are located in different Bearer Groups, creating a single shared TCP Flow Context is architecturally not feasible.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-7**  (ID: `11240280`)

PM Counters
Slice counters updating with slices extension

---

**4.11.0-9.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11240290`)

PM Counters
Feature CB008828 introduces extension of slices number from 20 to 2000. Slice is changed to slice range and this function is overtaken by profiles where operator selects slice IDs to be monitored via PMQAP. According to that:

- When slices extension is enabled, L2Hi shall stop reporting legacy non-PMQAP slice based counters

- When slices extension is disabled, L2Hi shall keep updating legacy non-PMQAP slice based counters

Legacy non-PMQAP slice based counters configuration is controlled via plmnSliceList (5G\_L2\_IF\_3266\_replaced([10987174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2WUsuPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and shall be processed as following:

[vsd\_desc]=== Diagram Content ===
Feature enabled [actSliceNumExt = TRUE]
The following legacy slice based nonPmqap counters stopped updated (due to reporting those counters with up to 2000 slices could be serious performance impact):
1) M55328C00001 (MEAS\_PERIOD\_NR\_PDCP\_SLICE) - 5G\_L2\_10278
2) M55328C00002 (PDCP\_SDU\_DATA\_NUM\_DL\_SLICE) - 5G\_L2\_12294
3) M55328C00003 (PDCP\_SDU\_DATA\_VOL\_DL\_SLICE) - 5G\_L2\_12296
4) M55328C00004 (PDCP\_SDU\_DATA\_NUM\_UL\_SLICE) - 5G\_L2\_10270
5) M55328C00005 (PDCP\_SDU\_DATA\_VOL\_UL\_SLICE) - 5G\_L2\_10272
6) M55328C00006 (PDCP\_SDU\_DELAY\_DL\_SLICE) - 5G\_L2\_10274
7) M55328C00007 (PDCP\_SDU\_DELAY\_UL\_SLICE) - 5G\_L2\_10276
=== Diagram Metadata ===

**4.11.0-9.0-8**  (ID: `11240296`)

PM Counters
Duration of the measurement period for a QosFlow to be in session state

---

**4.11.0-9.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11240302`)

PM Counters
Measuring period to be in session state mechanism

---

**4.11.0-9.0-8.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `12879638`)

PM Counters
L2-HI is in charge of handling following counters:

* SA:

- **NG\_FLOW\_IN\_SESSION\_DUR (M55350C00022) - please refer to 5G\_L2\_17490\_replaced([11240403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BfANfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),**

***\*- NG\_FLOW\_IN\_SESSION\_DUR\_PMQAP (M55357C00001) - please refer to  5G\_L2\_17492\_replaced([11240428](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BfAOfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),***\*

**[CB012582-B]**

- **NG\_FLOW\_IN\_SESSON\_DUR\_VONR (M55350C20050) - Applicable to only for 5QI1 bearer.** Please refer to 5G\_L2\_20562\_replaced([11240416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BfAN_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))\*\*\*\*

**[End CB012582-B]**

* NSA:

- **NX2CC\_RAB\_IN\_SESSION\_DUR (M55350C00038) - please refer to 5G\_L2\_17200\_replaced([11240474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BfnQfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),**

- **NX2CC\_RAB\_IN\_SESSION\_DUR\_PMQAP (M55357C00002) - please refer to 5G\_L2\_17202\_replaced([11240486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BfnRPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),**

which are responsible for storing duration of measurement period for a QoSFlow to be "in session state".

"In session state" means:

* [PR856219] For Bursty QoS flow, [End PR856219]there is user data in the PDCP queue in any of the directions or if any QoS flow data (UL or DL) has been transferred during the last 100 ms for that 5QI
* [PR856219] For Continuous QoS flow, [End PR856219]as long as the UE is in RRC connected state and [PR856219] there is user data in the PDCP queue either in UL or DL direction OR if any QoS flow data(UL or DL) has been transferred during the last 100ms for the 5QI.[End PR856219] The session time is increased from the first data transmission on the QoS flow until 100 ms after the last data transmission on the QoS flow. A particular QoS flow is defined to be of type continuous flow if the 5QI is any of {1, 2, 65, 66}. **This point is applicable only for SA counters.**

Note: L2Hi shall consider duplications and retransmissions as ''in session'' for the bearers.

These counters are valid for CU and increment during data transfer in **Bursty QoSFlow or** Continuous QoSFlow. Data transfer means when PDCP PDU is sent (DL direction) or SDU is sent (UL direction).\*\*\*\*

In case of **Bursty QosFlow data transfer, performed is checking during 100ms period whether at least one packet was received or the dl/ul buffer status is not empty. If the transfer is recorded, the counter should be incremented by 100ms.  The same logic is applicable for UL and DL respectively. The procedure should be performed during bearer setup until bearer deletion started.**

In case of **Continuous QosFlow data transfer counter should be incremented by the time when data is transmitted continuously plus 100ms period of time when no packet was received.**

In case of **Continuous QosFlow delete - continuous counter should be updated with:**

* [PR856219] if PDCP buffer is not empty when bearer delete is received, then  [End PR856219]"bearer delete timestamp" - "session begin timestamp"[Before PR856219] + 100ms [PR856219] OR
* **if PDCP buffer is empty when bearer delete is received, then min[("bearer delete timestamp"), ("timestamp when the last data was sent in either direction" + 100)] - "session begin timestamp". [End PR856219]**

**Continuous QosFlow is applicable only for SA counters.**

The mechanism shall be the following:

L2Hi shall check if in the last 100ms there was data in buffer (DL or UL) or data transfer (DL or UL) that it is showing if L2Hi was "in session" to counters could be updated.

L2Hi shall update counters on the events in system, that can be the following:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **DL:** | **UL:** |
| On push of packet to the PDCP buffer | On push of PDCP SDU to the the buffer |
| On delete of the packet from PDCP buffer | On delete of the packet from the buffer |
| On sending of PDCP PDU to DU | On sending of UL PDCP SDU |
| On data forwarding during intra-gNB mobility | On bearer delete |

On each of such event, L2Hi shall check if counters can be updated for the last 100ms.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating four different scenarios of "Bursty QoSFlow" with corresponding timelines and events. Each scenario is broken down into time intervals (20ms, 40ms, 60ms, etc.) and shows the status of "New packet entering/deleting to the buffer," "Data in buffer," "Data transferred," and "Event in the system." Explanations are provided for specific time points and events. A legend at the bottom clarifies the color coding for "data transferred," "data in buffer," and "Bearer Delete."
Here is the table representation of the diagram:
**1. Bursty QoSFlow**

| Time Interval | New packet entering/deleting to the buffer (per DL or UL) | Data in buffer (per DL or UL) | Data transferred (per DL or UL) | Event in the system | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 20ms - 100ms | Green | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 101ms |  |  |  | Event present | 101ms: check and increment the counter by 100ms; in 101ms there is event present in the system (buffer monitoring/packet sending, etc.) and on this incident we check what was sent in last 100ms |
| 100ms - 200ms | Green | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 201ms |  |  |  | Event present | 201ms: there is event in the system, that triggers the counter update (nothing new in buffer/no data transfer, etc.) so there will be no counter update |
| 200ms - 300ms | Green | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 301ms |  |  |  | No Event | 301ms: there was no any system event (no data in buffer, no data transferred, etc.) so counter not |
| 300ms - 320ms | Green | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 321ms |  |  |  | Event present | 321ms: check and increment the counter by 100ms; here is only the first event in the system and only here L2Hi will report the counter for the period from 100-200ms |
| 320ms - 380ms | Green | Green | Green | Green |  |
| **Counter will be updated as 200ms.** |  |  |  |  |  |
| **2. Bursty QoSFlow (case when for 100ms there is no new new packet sent but buffer is still not empty)** |  |  |  |  |  |

| Time Interval | New packet entering/deleting to the buffer (per DL or UL) | Data in buffer (per DL or UL) | Data transferred (per DL or UL) | Event in the system | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 20ms - 100ms | Green | Green | White | White |  |
| 101ms |  |  |  | No Event | 101ms: no event in the system (no any new packet entering/deleting to/from the buffer, etc.) so there is no counter update |
| 100ms - 200ms | Green | Green | White | White |  |
| 201ms |  |  |  | Event present | 201ms: there is event in the system, that triggers the counter update (nothing new in buffer/no data transfer, etc.) |
| 200ms - 240ms | Green | Green | White | White |  |
| 241ms |  |  |  | Event present | 241ms: check and increment the counter by 200ms (update possible because of event in the system) |
| 240ms - 300ms | Green | Green | White | White |  |
| 301ms |  |  |  | No Event | 301ms: there was no any system event (no data in buffer, no data transferred, etc.) so counter not |
| 300ms - 380ms | Green | Green | White | White |  |
| **Counter will be updated as 200ms.** |  |  |  |  |  |
| **3. Bursty QoSFlow - BearerDeleteReq received in third period when inSession=0** |  |  |  |  |  |

| Time Interval | New packet entering/deleting to the buffer (per DL or UL) | Data transferred OR data in buffer (per DL or UL) | Event in the system | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 20ms - 100ms | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 101ms |  |  | Event present | 101ms: check and increment the counter by 100ms |
| 100ms - 200ms | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 201ms |  |  | Event present | 201ms: there is no event in the system, that triggers the counter update (nothing new in buffer/no data transfer, etc.) |
| 200ms - 260ms | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 261ms |  |  | Event present (Bearer Delete) | 261ms: check and increment the counter by 100ms (for what happened between 100ms and 200ms) |
| 260ms - 380ms | Green | Green | Green |  |
| **Counter will be updated as 200ms.** |  |  |  |  |
| **4. Bursty QoSFlow - BearerDeleteReq received in third period when inSession=1** |  |  |  |  |

| Time Interval | New packet entering/deleting to the buffer (per DL or UL) | Data transferred OR data in buffer (per DL or UL) | Event in the system | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 20ms - 100ms | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 101ms |  |  | Event present | 101ms: check and increment the counter by 100ms |
| 100ms - 200ms | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 201ms |  |  | Event present | 201ms: check and increment the counter by 100ms |
| 200ms - 260ms | Green | Green | Green |  |
| 261ms |  |  | Event present (Bearer Delete) | 261ms: check and increment the counter by 60ms (for what happened between 200ms and 260ms) |
| 260ms - 380ms | Green | Green | Green |  |
| **Counter will be updated as 200ms (200+60ms).** |  |  |  |  |
| **NOTE: Updating counter value is performed only when new "InSession" starts** |  |  |  |  |
| **Legend:** |  |  |  |  |
| \* Green: data transferred |  |  |  |  |
| \* Orange: data in buffer |  |  |  |  |
| \* Red line: Bearer Delete[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_15740.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] |  |  |  |  |

[Before PR856219]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image displays three timelines illustrating the concept of "Continous QoSFlow" with different scenarios involving "Data transferred" and "BearerDelete" events. Each timeline has a numerical scale from 0 to 360, representing milliseconds.
The first timeline, labeled "Continous QoSFlow," shows "Data transferred" occurring from 0ms to 100ms. A "BearerDelete" event is indicated at 320ms, and the text below states that the counter will be updated as 220ms (120ms data transfer + 100ms), with a note that the counter is checked and incremented by 220ms at 320ms.
The second timeline, "Continous QoSFlow - BearerDelete received in third period when inSession = 0," shows "Data transferred" from 0ms to 140ms. A "BearerDelete" event is received at 260ms. The counter is updated as 240ms (140ms data transfer + 100ms), and it is checked and incremented by 240ms at 260ms.
The third timeline, "Continous QoSFlow - BearerDelete received in third period when inSession = 1," shows "Data transferred" from 0ms to 260ms. A "BearerDelete" event is received at 260ms. The counter is updated as 360ms (260ms - 0ms + 100ms), and it is checked and incremented by 360ms at 260ms.
A legend at the bottom clarifies that green bars represent "data transferred" and red vertical lines represent "Bearer Delete." A note states that updating the counter value is performed only when a new "InSession" starts.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m24dng\_5G\_L2\_Entity\_Level\_file\_15740.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[PR856219]

[image-2][image\_desc]The image displays a document with four distinct sections, each detailing a scenario related to "Continuous QoSFlow." Each section includes a visual representation of data flow over time, depicted as colored blocks, and accompanying text explaining the counter update behavior.
**Section 1: Continuous QoSFlow**
This section shows a timeline with green and orange blocks. The text states: "Counter will be updated as 180+100ms."
**Section 2: Continuous QoSFlow (case when for 100ms there is no new new packet sent but buffer is still not empty)**
This section presents a longer timeline with a sequence of green and orange blocks. The text indicates: "Counter will be updated as 240ms."
**Section 3: Continuous QoSFlow - BearerDeleteReq received in third period when inSession=0**
This section illustrates a timeline with green and orange blocks, followed by a red vertical line. The text reads: "Counter will be updated as 240ms at 201ms and noth".
**Section 4: Continuous QoSFlow - BearerDeleteReq received in third period when inSession=1**
This section shows a timeline with green and orange blocks, also followed by a red vertical line. The text states: "Counter will be updated as 200ms at 201ms and repo".
There are also two small colored rectangles at the bottom left, one green and one orange, likely serving as a legend for the blocks used in the timelines.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-11111401.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

---

**4.11.0-9.0-8.0-2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11240399`)

PM Counters
5G-L2-HI(PDCP) shall increment the following counters:

- M55350C00022 (NG\_FLOW\_IN\_SESSION\_DUR) Duration QosFlow is considered to be in session

- M55357C00001 (NG\_FLOW\_IN\_SESSION\_DUR\_PMQAP) Duration QosFlow is considered to be in session per profile

per each configured PMQAP profile (5G\_L2\_3337\_replaced([11238528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BQ9wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB012582-B]

- M55350C20050 (NG\_FLOW\_IN\_SESSON\_DUR\_VONR) Duration QosFlow is considered to be in session. Applicable to only for 5QI1 bearer.

[End CB012582-B]

The counter measures the duration for a QosFlow to be "in session" state in the gNB. The duration measurement is started at the time of QosFlow/Bearer is setup.

Requirement divided and aligned to 'PM Counter Specification in L2 EFS' guideline.Please see 5G\_L2\_17490\_replaced([11240403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BfANfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L2\_17492\_replaced([11240428](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3BfAOfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

PM Counters

NetAct name: UP\_TNL\_DLY\_H\_XN\_HO\_VONR, UP\_TNL\_DLY\_M\_XN\_HO\_VONR, UP\_TNL\_DLY\_T\_XN\_HO\_VONR

PI ID:  M55379C00022, M55379C00023, M55379C00024

Note: Three different bins (High, Moderate and Target) are defined to update the corresponding counter based on the calculated tunnelling delay duration. PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time: No additional details compared to NIDD.

Increment value: No additional details compared to NIDD.

Notes:

1) start time is sent from source gNB to target gNB via GTP-U message using proprietary field along with forwarding packets (Refer 5G\_UP\_IF\_14457\_replaced([11547502](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tY9uWPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

4) End time is marked with the timestamp when first DL forwarded Data is received from source gNB or End Marker received or EndMarker timer expired whichever is occurred first.

5) if the bearer, for any reason, released before L2Hi receives first DL data from source gNB, counter is not incremented.

**4.11.0-9.0-12.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11240833`)

PM Counters
Number of time intervals for which the L2HI-CU is in non-critical load state

---

**4.11.0-9.0-12.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11240839`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR L2 overload report per CU-UP (OVCU)

NetAct name: NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_L2\_CUUP

PI ID: M55382CRD50001

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time:

If rdCpuOverloadCounters (5G\_L2\_21298\_replaced([11233340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Ap5wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled, this R&D counter is updated for 5G-L2-HI (CU) by each 5G-L2-HI instance when average CPU load (as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13832\_replaced([11228962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  for cloud and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13833\_replaced([11228977](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  for classical deployment) of this 5G-L2-HI instance over measurement interval (100ms) is greater than or equal to rdCpuNonCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13448\_replaced([11229407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyn4iPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than rdCpuCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13446\_replaced([11229333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kynRevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Increment value: Each 5G-L2-HI shall increment by 1 each time average CPU load (as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13832\_replaced([11228962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of this 5G-L2-HI instance

over measurement interval (100ms) is greater than or equal to rdCpuNonCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13448\_replaced([11229407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyn4iPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than rdCpuCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13446\_replaced([11229333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kynRevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Additional Information:

Classical Deployment:

1. In case of Classical Deployment, 5G-L2-HI (CU) and 5G-L2-HI (DU) are co-located and share the cores, average CPU load computed (as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13833\_replaced([11228977](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) will be same for both 5G-L2-HI (CU) and 5G-L2-HI (DU). Hence counters NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_PDCP\_CUUP and NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_RLC\_DU will have same values. Similarly, CRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_PDCP\_CUUP and CRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_RLC\_DU will have same values.

2. In case of multiple 5G-L2-HI instances, BOAM shall aggregate this counter values across multiple 5G-L2-HI instances and report the aggregated value under NRCUUP.

Cloud Deployment:

1. In case of Cloud Deployment, 5G-L2-HI instance in vCU only shall report this counter under NRCUUP.

---

**4.11.0-9.0-12.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11240850`)

PM Counters
Measurement: NR L2 overload report per CU-UP (OVCU)

PI ID: M55382CRD50002

Note: PM counter definitions can be found in NIDD as explained in 5G\_L2\_13022\_replaced([11192143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28iOyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Update time:

If rdCpuOverloadCounters (5G\_L2\_21298\_replaced([11233340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3Ap5wPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled, this R&D counter is updated for 5G-L2-HI (CU) by each 5G-L2-HI instance when average CPU load (as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13832\_replaced([11228962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  for cloud and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13833\_replaced([11228977](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  for classical deployment) of this 5G-L2-HI instance over measurement interval (100ms) is greater than or equal to rdCpuCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13446\_replaced([11229333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kynRevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Increment value: Each 5G-L2-HI increment shall increment by 1 each time average CPU load (as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13832\_replaced([11228962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of this 5G-L2-HI instance over measurement interval (100ms) is greater than or equal to rdCpuCriticalLoadThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13446\_replaced([11229333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kynRevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Additional Information:

Classical Deployment:

1. In case of Classical Deployment, 5G-L2-HI (CU) and 5G-L2-HI (DU) are co-located and share the cores, average CPU load computed (as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13833\_replaced([11228977](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kylcRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) will be same for both 5G-L2-HI (CU) and 5G-L2-HI (DU). Hence counters NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_PDCP\_CUUP and NONCRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_RLC\_DU will have same values. Similarly,  CRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_PDCP\_CUUP and CRITIC\_CPU\_LOAD\_RLC\_DU will have same values.

2. In case of multiple 5G-L2-HI instances, BOAM shall aggregate this counter values across multiple 5G-L2-HI instances and report the aggregated value under NRCUUP.

Cloud Deployment:

1. In case of Cloud Deployment, 5G-L2-HI instance in vCU only shall report this counter under NRCUUP.
